The Golden Order (黄金律, Ōgonritsu ) is a philosophical and theological movement in Elden Ring . It refers to the removal of the Rune of Death from the Elden Ring and the historic reign of Queen Marika the Eternal . Its greatest symbols are the Erdtree and the Grace of Gold . It is the dominant set of beliefs in the Lands Between .
Prior to the Golden Order, the Rune of Death was part of the Elden Ring. [ 1 ] Its power was wielded as the god -slaying black flame by the Empyrean known as the Gloam-Eyed Queen , [ 2 ] who led the Godskin Apostles on their god hunt . [ 3 ] The apostles' purge ended in defeat when Maliketh , Marika's half-brother and Shadowbound Beast , [ 4 ] triumphed over the Gloam-Eyed Queen. [ 5 ] [ 6 ] Destined Death was subsequently removed from the Elden Ring and sealed away by Maliketh inside his Black Blade , [ 7 ] [ 8 ] [ 9 ] [ 10 ] and he became known as the "Death of the Demigods." [ 11 ]
The confinement of the Rune of Death marked the beginning of the Golden Order. [ 12 ] With its establishment, Marika suppressed the power of her rival and granted immortality to herself and her demigod offspring, the Golden Lineage . [ 13 ]
The Golden Order was a governing principle, a religion, and a philosophy. It was founded on the principle that Marika was the one true god, [ 14 ] and was propagated by the Two Fingers . [ 15 ] It replaced the concept of Destined Death with that of Erdtree Burial .
The Golden Order was capable of integrating conflicting ideologies and practices. The dragon cult of the royal capital was compatible because the ancient dragons' lightning was imbued with gold. [ 16 ] Later, the Erdtree faith absorbed the practice of glintstone sorcery . [ 17 ] Concepts that threatened to shatter the Order entirely, such as life in death , were labeled as heresy and violently persecuted by the Golden Order. [ 18 ]
The Golden Order changed in the age of Elden Lord Radagon
Golden Order Fundamentalism was a scholarly pursuit that combined both intelligence and faith. [ 19 ] It attempted to interpret the fundamentals of the Golden Order. [ 20 ] Fundamentalism was based on two concepts: the Law of Regression , the pull of meaning and the yearning to converge; [ 21 ] and the Law of Causality , the pull between meanings which links all things in a chain of relation. [ 22 ]
Among the Golden Order Fundamentalists were the hunters of Those Who Live in Death , who abandoned learning in search of an absolute evil to contend with. [ 23 ] Miquella , who once created Fundamentalist incantations to give to his father Radagon , abandoned Fundamentalism as it could not treat Malenia 's rot. [ 24 ] Other notable followers of Golden Order Fundamentalism included Brother Corhyn , Goldmask , and the twins D. Hunter of the Dead and D, Beholder of Death .
The Rune of Death goes by two names; the other is Destined Death. The forbidden shadow, plucked from the Golden Order upon its creation... - Finger Reader Enia
The Rune of Death (死のルーン, Shi no Rūn ), also known as Destined Death (運命の死, Unmei no Shi ), [ 1 ] is an unobtainable Great Rune in Elden Ring that controls the fated deaths of the Demigods . [ 2 ] Once part of the Elden Ring , it was removed by Queen Marika and sealed away when she established her Golden Order . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ] [ 4 ] It appears during the cutscene that plays when the player defeats Maliketh, the Black Blade at Crumbling Farum Azula .
Destined Death is a crimson, cross-shaped rune with tapered ends, resembling Marika's Rune with a downward arc. Smoke emanates from the rune as a jagged black fissure splits it vertically through its center. It manifests within a font of Darkness upon its unsealing.
The Rune of Death can grant Destined Death, or true and fated death. [ 2 ] When used to carve the Cursemark of Death in a full ring, it kills the recipient in both body and soul ; however, incomplete rings can apply partial effects under specific circumstances. Known as half-wheels of the centipede, the waxing crescent burns away the flesh while the waning crescent destroys only the soul. [ 5 ]
The Rune also produces crimson flames with golden motes that inflicts the Destined Death status effect , which reduces maximum HP and deals damage over time. [ 6 ] [ 7 ] The power of Destined Death could be repelled by the Blasphemous Claw [ 8 ] or a depiction of the eclipsed sun . [ 9 ]
The Rune of Death was once embedded within the Elden Ring, [ 2 ] empowering the black flames to deliver Destined Death to even gods . [ 10 ] It was venerated by the Godskin Apostles [ 11 ] and wielded by the Gloam-Eyed Queen , whose sacred Godslayer's Greatsword channeled black flames. [ 12 ] The Queen, an Empyrean chosen by the Fingers , led the Apostles on their god hunt ; [ 13 ] [ 14 ] however, she was ultimately vanquished by Maliketh, [ 12 ] the shadowbound beast and loyal vassal of Queen Marika. [ 4 ]
Maliketh was known as the "Death of the Demigods".
With the Gloam-Eyed Queen defeated, [ 11 ] Marika extracted the Rune of Death from the Elden Ring, [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ] and Maliketh sealed it within his Black Blade . [ 4 ] [ 15 ] This act was the foundation of the Golden Order [ 3 ] and established Marika as the one true god. [ 16 ] It exempted the Demigods from dying true deaths, granting them immortality, [ 2 ] and also conferred a form of unending life to the Erdtree people . [ 17 ] With the true lethality of Godslayer incantations suppressed, [ 11 ] [ 10 ] only Maliketh held the power to destroy the Demigods, and there was not one among them who did not fear him. [ 18 ] [ 19 ]
At a later point in history, a fragment of the Rune of Death was stolen from Maliketh by Ranni the Witch , who used it to create the godslaying Black Knives through a fearsome rite. [ 20 ] On the Night of Black Knives , the Black Knife Assassins used these blades to murder Godwyn the Golden , the first Demigod to perish in all of recorded history. [ 21 ] However, due to Ranni carving the Cursemark of Destined Death into her flesh at the same moment as Godwyn's death, he was unable to die a proper death and perished in soul alone. [ 22 ] [ 5 ] Meanwhile, Ranni's flesh perished and her soul continued to live, inhabiting a doll body. [ 5 ] After the Night of Black Knives, Maliketh bound his sword within his own flesh in order to ensure that none would ever steal Death again. [ 15 ]
On the night of the dire plot the stolen Rune of Death enabled the first Death of a demigod. Later, the Rune of Death spread across the Lands Between through the underground roots of the Greattree, sprouting in the form of Deathroot. - Deathroot
Godwyn was given an Erdtree Burial at the Erdtree's roots in the Deeproot Depths beneath Leyndell, Royal Capital . [ 23 ] However, his soulless body soon began a grotesque transformation into the blighted Prince of Death . [ 22 ] Fragments of the Rune of Death began to spread through the underground Greattree roots connected to Godwyn's corpse, [ 24 ] [ 25 ] sprouting in the form of Deathroot , [ 26 ] [ 27 ] and leading to the rise of Those Who Live in Death . [ 28 ] [ 29 ]
The Beast Eye quivers in the presence of Deathroot.
As Gurranq, Beast Clergyman , Maliketh attempts to reclaim the stolen shards by consuming Deathroot, an endeavor he believes will restore the Golden Order and end his hunger. After devouring all nine Deathroots, his hunger persists and he realizes that the Golden Order cannot be restored. [ 30 ] [ 31 ] He was, in truth, betrayed by Marika. [ 4 ]
Marika's daughter, Melina , aids the Tarnished knowing their quest will ultimately violate the Golden Order. [ 32 ] [ 33 ] Her purpose as the Kindling Maiden is to commit the Cardinal Sin and unlock the path to Maliketh and Destined Death. [ 34 ] [ 35 ] Although Maliketh unbinds the Black Blade, [ 36 ] he is defeated. The Tarnished interacts with the Rune, unleashing a burst of crimson flame. The Erdtree is engulfed in crimson flames, and its impenetrable thorns are burned away. [ 37 ] [ 38 ]
If the Tarnished rises as the Lord of Frenzied Flame after using the Frenzied Flame to spare Melina, [ 39 ] she gains or unlocks the power of Destined Death. [ 40 ]
It happened during the Golden Age of the Erdtree, long before the shattering of the Elden Ring. Someone stole a fragment of the Rune of Death from Maliketh, the Black Blade. And on a bitter night, murdered Godwyn the Golden. - Sorcerer Rogier
The Night of Black Knives (黒き刃の陰謀の夜, Kuroki Yaiba no Inbō no Yoru ) was an event mentioned in Elden Ring . It involved the theft of Destined Death and the assassination of Godwyn the Golden , a son of Queen Marika the Eternal . It would serve as the catalyst of the conflict known as The Shattering . [ 1 ] [ 2 ]
Although the conspirators behind it remained unknown to the wider world, [ 3 ] it was in fact orchestrated by Lunar Princess Ranni [ 4 ] as she was looking for a way to free herself from the control of the Two Fingers . [ 5 ] Ranni, who sought to change her fate , stole a piece of the Rune of Death from Maliketh , who served as the guardian of the rune. With the stolen fragment, Ranni proceeded to imbue the Black Knives of Numen Assassins , all of them being women from the Eternal Cities with ties to Marika, [ 6 ] with the powers of Destined Death. [ 7 ] [ 8 ]
On the same night, Ranni gifted her brother, Praetor Rykard , with the Blasphemous Claw , a rock engraved with traces of the Rune of Death, as a reward for helping her in the plot and to make Rykard able to challenge Maliketh on the day of his blasphemy. [ 9 ]
Wishing to shed her Empyrean body but preserve her spirit , she knew that the spirit of someone else had to die as well. On the night of the plot, the assassins arrived in Leyndell, the Royal Capital , and slew Godwyn the Golden, carving the Cursemark of Death into his flesh. The Cursemark was supposed to form a circle; however, as Ranni perished in the same moment as Godwyn, the mark was split into two half-wheels. [ 10 ] Godwyn's soul alone perished, while Ranni became the first Demigod to die in the flesh. [ 11 ]
Immediately following the assassination, the Black Knives fled the capital. Tiche , the daughter of the Black Knife Ringleader Alecto , died protecting her mother during the escape. [ 12 ]
Godwyn's body was interred in the Deeproot Depths at the base of the Erdtree 's roots, where he mutated and deformed into the being that would become known as the Prince of Death. [ 13 ] Later, the traces of the Rune of Death used to slay him spread through the network of Greattree roots that span the Lands Between , taking the form of Deathroot , the source of Those Who Live in Death .
Ranni, whose Empyrean body perished upon the carving of the Cursemark, transferred her soul into a doll modeled after her mentor . [ 14 ] She maintained a low profile following the Night of Black Knives, and it is unknown whether her death was widely known. [ 15 ]
Following the Night of Black Knives, the Elden Ring was shattered by Queen Marika. As a result, the great war known as The Shattering ensued. [ 2 ]
In the aftermath of the Shattering, a Tarnished known as Fia, the Deathbed Companion , came into contact with the soulless body of Godwyn. [ 16 ] Fia sought the two half-wheels, wishing to reunite them and produce a Mending Rune , which could introduce Those Who Live in Death to the Elden Ring. [ 17 ] During this time, another Tarnished named Rogier began to study the Night of Black Knives, [ 2 ] bringing him into contact with Fia.
The primordial form of the Erdtree is close in nature to life itself, and this spear , modeled on its crucible, is imbued with ancient holy essence. - Siluria's Tree
The Crucible (坩堝, Rutsubo ), also known as the crucible of life (生命の坩堝), the golden Crucible (黄金の坩堝), or primordial crucible , was the primordial matter in which all life was blended together and the prior form of the Erdtree . [ 2 ]
The primordial Crucible was the divine essence that became the Erdtree and the place where all life energy was once blended together. [ 2 ] [ 4 ] [ 5 ] It was said to be close in nature to life itself, [ 6 ] [ 7 ] and was represented by the reddish tint in primordial gold —the color of homeward yearning. [ 8 ] The power of the Crucible was also held in the armor of the Crucible Knights , [ 9 ] and channeled by their weapons. [ 6 ]
The "mother of all Crucibles" appeared on a Giant
The aspects of various creatures, such as feathers, scales, and knots, once grew on the bodies of humanoids. Ancient legends from the tower of Enir-Ilim claim that the "mother of all Crucibles" first appeared among the giants long ago. [ 10 ]
At some point, a group of people made contact with the Crucible, only to have their bodies mutated, becoming the chimeric Misbegotten , humanoid creatures with different aspects of other lifeforms like fur, scales, wings, tails and beast fangs. [ 11 ] Identified as the mark of the Crucible, their presence was a signifier of divinity in ancient times. [ 12 ] Of the Crucible's gifts, [ 13 ] the Hornsent considered the tangled horn to be the most significant sign of primacy. [ 14 ]
As Queen Marika 's society advanced, signs of the Crucible were increasingly disdained as impurities. [ 15 ] The Crucible Knights were shunned, the Omen were banished, and the Misbegotten were enslaved by the Erdtree, which deemed their corrupted appearance to be a punishment for their act. [ 11 ] Perfumers like Tricia attempted to heal the Omen and Misbegotten, but were unsuccessful in curing these conditions. [ 16 ] Rarely, budding horns and overlapping fangs still sprout on herbivorous and carnivorous beasts that typically would bear no horns, as a recessive trait considered a vestige of the Crucible's influence. [ 17 ] [ 18 ]
The Scadutree is the shadow of the Erdtree. Born of dark notions that bear no sense of Order, that twist and bend its stock, rendering it brittle. - Remembrance of the Shadow Sunflower
The Scadutree (影樹, Eiju ; lit. "Shadow Tree") is a colossal tree in Elden Ring , included in the Shadow of the Erdtree expansion.
It is the shadow of the Erdtree which looms over the Land of Shadow , [ 1 ] born of dark notions that bear no sense of Order , that twist and bend its stock, rendering it misshapen and brittle. [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
The Scadutree is holy but its gold is veiled in shadow and covered in impenetrable thorns . [ 4 ] [ 5 ]
Like the Erdtree, the Scadutree can manifest avatars to defend itself and its offspring. Scadutree Avatars take the form of giant Shadow Sunflowers .
The Scadutree is located at the northernmost point in the Realm of Shadow, found at the Scadutree Base .
A Scadutree Fragment
The blessed sap of the Scadutree once fell like tears into the Scadutree Chalice , but it has since scattered, pooling deeply within the Furnace Golems . [ 6 ]
Its splinters were collected, displayed, and prayed to in some Churches of Marika by the people of the Erdtree. [ 7 ] Scadutree Fragments bestowed a Scadutree blessing of great power, although it has no influence outside of the Realm of Shadow . [ 8 ] The remains of the warriors who perished in the realm of shadow were touched by the gold of the Scadutree, a blessing said to be the highest honor that can be afforded to the dead. [ 9 ]
For those who abandoned the practice of incantations after devout faith rewarded them with only despair, the image of the misshapen Scadutree is an edict: “Spurn all that exists. Wound all that exists. For we have been abandoned. Denounce their ways. Do them harm. For they have abandoned us.” [ 10 ] [ 11 ]
Let a new epoch begin. An epoch glistening with life. Brandish the Elden Ring, for the Age of the Erdtree! - Queen Marika the Eternal — Melina
Queen Marika the Eternal is the central character in the world of Elden Ring . She is the divine ruler of the Lands Between and the current vessel of the Elden Ring , a god in truth. [ 4 ] She grew the towering Erdtree , concealed the Realm of Shadow , and established the Golden Order . By the time of the game's events, she has long vanished from public view, though her influence persists through the Grace of Gold . Her Demigod offspring became shardbearers when they claimed Great Runes that dispersed when she shattered the Elden Ring. [ 5 ] [ 6 ]
Information about Marika is primarily provided by Melina , Finger Reader Enia , and various item descriptions.
Queen Marika was a tall Numen [ 7 ] woman with fair skin and long, flowing golden hair gathered into two uneven braids, the right being longer. [ 8 ] She typically wore a circlet, gold armbands, gold serpentine bracelets, and either a black dress or a robe patterned with golden floral motifs. Often depicted in cruciform poses with her head bowed, she simultaneously evoked divinity, fragility, regality, and martyrdom.
In the present era, her body appears as a stone-like, petrified husk, fractured and cracked like broken porcelain. She is shackled and suspended on a great Rune Arc with a red needle-like shard piercing her abdomen like a spear. During the final confrontation, her body transforms into Radagon of the Golden Order before the Elden Beast reveals itself. Following the player's victory, she ultimately reverts to a fractured, statuesque form.
Marika's Rune was the official seal of Queen Marika, used by her to control vassals, [ 9 ] bestow grace, [ 10 ] and seal away threats to her power. [ 11 ]
Bearing a close resemblance to the Rune of Death , Marika's Rune is a Y-shaped Elden Rune with an upward crescent resembling the lower arc of the Elden Ring, believed to be the basin in which its blessing pool. [ 6 ] Its shape parallels Marika's crucified form within the Erdtree. Variations of the Rune recur throughout the Lands Between, such as the Effigies of the Martyr , statues found in churches of Marika , and the numerous crosses found throughout Limgrave and Dominula, Windmill Village .
Queen Marika is found near the Fractured Marika site of grace on the Stone Platform within the Erdtree , accessible from Leyndell, Ashen Capital .
Marika came from the Shaman Village in the Scaduview . [ 8 ] Her people had an affinity for trees and flesh that melded harmoniously with that of others. [ 12 ] The hornsent tortured and sliced up shamans before stuffing them into the jars to be reborn as saints. [ 13 ] The Two Fingers recognized Marika as an Empyrean and bestowed her a shadowbound beast in the form of her half-brother, Maliketh [ 14 ] —a faithful follower, incapable of treachery. [ 15 ] At some point during this period, Marika took the warrior Hoarah Loux as her consort, who later vowed to become Godfrey , her first Elden Lord . [ 16 ] [ 17 ] Through seduction and betrayal, she ascended to godhood at the Gate of Divinity atop the tower of Enir-Ilim , [ 18 ] and became the vessel for the Elden Ring . [ 4 ] This affair led to the birth of the Erdtree and Scadutree , [ 19 ] [ 20 ] and was considered a betrayal by the Hornsent. The Scadutree veiled the land of shadow upon its creation. [ 21 ]
Eventually, Marika returned to the Shaman Village to find it abandoned, the people of her village were stolen away from their home, never to return. [ 22 ] After cutting off a braid of her hair as an offering to the Grandmother , she bathed her home in the healing light of gold, knowing full well that there was no one to heal. [ 23 ] She would never return again. [ 8 ]
In the early days, everything was in opposition to the Erdtree . [ 24 ] With Godfrey’s aid, [ 25 ] Marika waged a War Against the Giants atop the frigid northern mountains , where dwelled the Flame of Ruin capable of burning the Erdtree. [ 26 ] Ultimately victorious, Marika was believed to have slain the Fell God of the Fire Giants . [ 27 ] Upon learning that the Flame of Ruin would never die, however, she cursed the last of the giants to tend to it for eternity. [ 28 ] Marika declared the path to the mountains as Forbidden Lands and excised details of the war from history. [ 29 ]
Marika and Godfrey would rule together and have at least three children: Godwyn the Golden and the twins Morgott and Mohg . The twins were both born as accursed Omen and were hidden in the depths below the capital . Even so, Godfrey and his Golden Lineage would be counted as the first of the demigods. [ 16 ] Godfrey went on to conquer many lands for the Erdtree.
At some point during Marika's rule, the Gloam-Eyed Queen and her Godskin Apostles wielded the power of god-slaying black flame to carry out a god hunt . [ 30 ] [ 31 ] Marika thus desired to seal the Rune of Death 's power. Her Shadowbound Beast and half-brother Maliketh defeated the Gloam-Eyed Queen and her apostles, and then she extracted the Rune of Death from the Elden Ring. Maliketh sealed it in his black blade , [ 14 ] founding the Golden Order [ 32 ] [ 33 ] and establishing Marika as the one true god.
When the Erdtree sensed its mortality for the first time and released its Golden Seeds to spawn the Minor Erdtrees [ 34 ] , revealing itself not as perfect and eternal as those who worshipped it believed it to be, [ 35 ] Marika would abandon blind faith and declare at the Minor Erdtree Church her intent to inquire into the depths of her Golden Order in an attempt to strengthen its grace through understanding. [ 36 ]
Queen Marika punished the cutting-gifted tribe for discovering the nature of her original sin . [ 37 ] [ 38 ]
Queen Marika desired to conquer Liurnia of the Lakes , the land of the Academy of Raya Lucaria and the Carian Royal Family . She declared war on the glintstone sorcerers and sent a golden host led by her secret other half: a red-haired champion named Radagon . The champions of the moon, led by Rennala , repelled the glorious warriors of the Erdtree for a time, but it ended in a draw. In the second Liurnian War, Radagon invades again, but this time, he uses the Celestial Dew at the Church of Vows in a ritual to recant his aggressions and seek absolution. The Carian Queen accepted, and their wrongdoings were washed away. The two were wed and produced three children: Radahn , Rykard , and Ranni .
Marika sent her son Messmer away on a crusade into the lands of the Hornsent. Despite her precautions, her fear of the Abyssal Serpent sealed within him led her to trap him within the Realm of Shadow , where he would wage war to exterminate the Hornsent and devastate their lands. No matter how many of her enemies burned in his flame , however, Messmer received no sign from Marika to end his crusade. Marika kept these events and the land of shadow hidden away and removed from history. [ 11 ] [ 39 ]
With her rule secure, Marika announced her intention to search the depths of the Golden Order, declaring the early days of blind belief a thing long past. [ 40 ] When Godfrey's last foe fell, it was said the hue of his eyes had faded. [ 41 ] Marika banished him and his kinfolk from the Lands Between, robbing them of their grace , [ 42 ] thus creating the first Tarnished , all in the hope that they would grow stronger by waging war in lands outside her rule, dying, and then eventually being revived with their guidance of grace returned. [ 43 ]
After Godfrey's banishment from the Lands Between, Marika took Radagon as her second husband and King Consort, elevating him to become the second Elden Lord. [ 44 ] Radagon already had three children with Queen Rennala of the Carian Royal Family , and after his union with Marika, she would raise her new step-children, Radahn , Rykard , and Ranni to demigod status. [ 45 ]
Marika and Radagon would go on to have two more children of their own, the twins Malenia and Miquella , [ 46 ] who like Marika herself and Radagon's daughter Ranni, were Empyreans, [ 47 ] and were thus potential successors to Marika. However, Radagon and Marika were in truth the same. Radagon was described as Marika's male "other self". [ 48 ] Thus, the twins were the children of a single god, and they were both born afflicted: Malenia with rotting sickness and Miquella with eternal childhood. [ 49 ]
On the Night of Black Knives , a fragment of the Rune of Death was stolen from Maliketh. [ 50 ] For a long time, it was not known who was behind the plot, [ 51 ] but it is finally revealed it was in fact Ranni who stole the fragment of the rune to forge god-slaying black knives through a fearsome rite. [ 52 ]
The Black Knife Assassins , Numen women purported to have close ties to Marika herself, [ 53 ] used these knives to slay Godwyn the Golden, the first recorded death of a demigod in all history. [ 54 ] Queen Marika is said to have been driven to the brink by the death of Godwyn, [ 55 ] and she instructed her Demigod children to fight for the positions of Elden Lord and that of godhood. [ 56 ]
Some time after the Night of Black Knives, Queen Marika used her Numen hammer to shatter the Elden Ring. [ 5 ] Fragments of the ring splintered into Great Runes and spread across the Lands Between, starting a conflict between her demigod children. War after war was fought, but there was no victor. [ 57 ] For her part, Marika would be imprisoned inside the Erdtree, [ 58 ] possibly by the Elden Beast or the Greater Will itself. [ 59 ]
Marika's trespass demanded a heavy sentence. But even in shackles, she remains a god, and the vision's vessel. - Two Fingers — Finger Reader Enia
True to her promise to Godfrey and his warriors, grace was restored to the banished Tarnished. [ 60 ] They would rise from their graves and journey to the Lands Between to once again brandish the Elden Ring. The Tarnished formed the Roundtable Hold , where they worked to realize the goal Marika had given them. They would be served by a Misbegotten blacksmith named Hewg , whom Marika herself had charged with smithing a "god-slaying weapon" before his imprisonment in the Hold. [ 61 ]
Eventually, the Tarnished manages to fight their way into the Erdtree, where the shattered Marika lies imprisoned. Marika is suddenly released from her bonds, as Radagon asserts control over their shared body and confronts the Tarnished. After defeating Radagon and the Elden Beast itself, the Tarnished may choose what to do with the fractured body of Marika. Marika's head is restored to her frame if the Elden Ring is mended, either by itself or with a Mending Rune. If Ranni is summoned, she picks up Marika's head gently, peacefully dissipating along with the rest of her body. If the Tarnished is the Lord of Frenzied Flame, Marika's head breaks apart and crumbles into ash.
By choosing to go down the Elden Lord path, whether the regular one or using any of the three Mending Runes to fix the Elden Ring within Marika, the Tarnished champion ushers in a new age. They become the third Elden Lord and effectively Marika's new consort in every one of them, [ 62 ] except in the Age of the Stars (where they become consort to Ranni) and in the Lord of Frenzied Flame ending (where they make the whole world burn). However, Queen Marika remains shattered and unresponsive, with only the Elden Ring itself shining brightly within her body.
At certain Sites of Grace found in churches , the very words of Queen Marika yet linger. Melina offers to share them with the Tarnished if she is traveling with them. [ 63 ] [ 64 ] The game does not establish a chronological order for the seven Echoes of Marika. They are as follows:
O Radagon, leal hound of the Golden Order. Thou'rt yet to become me. Thou'rt yet to become a god. Let us be shattered, both. Mine other self. - Melina — Queen Marika the Eternal
Radagon of the Golden Order is a boss in Elden Ring . He is encountered inside the Erdtree in Leyndell, Ashen Capital , and is the first half of the final boss fight, with the Elden Beast as the second half.
Radagon first rose to prominence during the Liurnian Wars, when he joined the heroes' ranks. [ 1 ] A great champion with flowing red locks, he arrived in Liurnia at the head of a golden host, where he met Queen Rennala in battle. [ 2 ] Although two wars would be fought between them, the First and Second Liurnian Wars, [ 3 ] , no victor would emerge from either. [ 4 ] Radagon eventually repented his territorial aggressions by cleansing himself with Celestial Dew , and swore his love to Rennala. [ 5 ] He became husband to the Carian Queen, [ 6 ] wedding her at the Church of Vows . [ 7 ] Rennala bequeathed him a greatsword , bestowed by a Carian queen upon her spouse to honor long-standing tradition. [ 8 ] [ 9 ] After entering into marriage with Rennala and joining the Carian line, [ 10 ] he ordered the Carian magic preceptors to don masks of confidence, to make it clear that all of their matters were to be kept strictly private. [ 11 ]
Radagon and Rennala had three children: Radahn , Rykard and Ranni . [ 12 ] While husband to Rennala, Radagon studied glintstone sorcery taught at the Academy of Raya Lucaria . [ 13 ]
After Godfrey, the First Elden Lord was stripped of grace and hounded from the Lands Between , Radagon returned to the capital where he went on to marry Queen Marika and become her King Consort and second Elden Lord. [ 14 ] Before leaving Rennala, Radagon gifted her an amber egg . [ 15 ] His departure left her heartbroken, and eventually led to her being deposed by the academy and imprisoned in the Grand Library . [ 16 ] His three children from the previous marriage would be raised to demigod status as stepchildren of Queen Marika. [ 17 ]
A sculptor from Leyndell was commissioned to create a statue of Radagon. [ 18 ] In doing so, he discovered a secret - that Radagon is Marika. This secret was hidden within the statue, and is revealed by casting Law of Regression in front of it, causing the statue's form to change from Radagon to Marika.
Radagon and Marika had a twin daughter and son: Malenia [ 19 ] and Miquella . [ 20 ] As they were born of a single god, they were both Empyreans , but were born afflicted: Malenia with a rotting sickness and Miquella with eternal childhood. [ 21 ]
While married to Marika, Radagon studied incantations. [ 13 ] He is heavily associated with Golden Order Fundamentalism, a branch of the Golden Order said to be scholarship in all but name [ 22 ] , which incorporates incantations that rely on a combination of faith and intelligence. His son Miquella followed in his fundamentalist footsteps, and created several incantations as gifts for his father. [ 23 ] [ 24 ] Radagon would return the favor with his own gift of gratitude to young Miquella, however Miquella later abandoned Fundamentalism, realising that it could do nothing to treat Malenia's Rot. [ 25 ]
Radagon trying to repair the Elden Ring.
Following the Night of Black Knives , Marika shattered the Elden Ring , breaking the Golden Order . Radagon, on the other hand, remained loyal to the Golden Order, and attempted to repair the Elden Ring with the same hammer used to shatter it. [ 26 ] As punishment, Marika was imprisoned inside the Erdtree . [ 27 ] While Radagon had opposed Marika's treachery, he would share Marika's sentence, as the two were now bound in a single body.
When a Tarnished sets fire to the Erdtree in order to burn away the wall of thorns denying their entry, they encounter the imprisoned Marika. Suddenly released from her bonds, her hair immediately turns red as Radagon assumes control of their shared body and wields Marika's hammer to fight the Tarnished. However, Radagon is unable to defeat them and falls at their hands, with his body being subsumed by the Elden Beast to transform into a large sword [ 28 ] , as it emerges to be the Tarnished champion's final challenge.
Radagon is the first of two enemies that compose the final boss fight of Elden Ring , with the Elden Beast being the second. Players will have to fight Radagon again if they die to the Elden Beast.
Radagon relies on very fast hammer swings, and some of his attacks will generate shockwaves. These shockwaves will either be immediate, or will occur after a brief delay- for the latter, golden cracks will appear in the ground moments before the explosion.
At range, Radagon can throw golden spears at the player. He will either leap into the air and throw a single, giant spear, or quickly hurl five spears in a loose fan. These spears will remain in the ground for a second before exploding. He also has a grab attack which he may perform at close- or mid-range. During the grab, his left arm will glow gold and he will wind it back behind him before lunging. The shockwave generated by the grab may still cause damage even if the grab itself misses.
All of his gold attacks will inflict Holy damage.
After his health has been lowered somewhat, he will leap into the air and perform a Gold Breaker attack, creating a large area of effect shockwave. During this phase, Radagon will sometimes teleport, generating an explosion when he reappears. In addition to the golden spear attacks used in the previous phase, he may now jump up and throw a volley of spears. His stomp will also now create a shockwave that deals Holy damage.
Once his health is below half, Radagon will teleport into the middle of the arena and perform three rapid hammer strikes on the ground, each producing a large shockwave. He will now teleport much more often, and can perform two shockwave-inducing hammer strikes in quick succession.
The arena is a featureless, oval platform with no obstacles. It is not possible to fall of the edges.
Alas, I am returned. To be granted audience once more. Upon my name as Godfrey, The first Elden Lord! - Godfrey, First Elden Lord
Hoarah Loux, Warrior , also known as Godfrey, First Elden Lord and the Lord of the Battlefield , is a mandatory boss in Elden Ring .
Godfrey is a former consort of Queen Marika the Eternal and the first Elden Lord of the Golden Order . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] Although his actions directly shaped much of the history of the Lands Between , Queen Marika stole his grace and banished him to the badlands .
Both encounters with Godfrey are mandatory boss fights:
Lord Godfrey was once known as Hoarah Loux, [ 3 ] [ 4 ] [ 5 ] a simple, yet ferocious warrior with a ceaseless lust for battle. [ 6 ] He was an unmatched champion who earned his right to Lordship through sheer strength. Later, he took the name Godfrey when he took the spirit of Serosh upon his back. The Lord of Beasts suppressed his rage, [ 7 ] [ 8 ] allowing him to conduct himself in a manner befitting Marika's first Elden Lord . [ 9 ] [ 10 ]
Godfrey led Marika's golden armies
Before it came to be an embodiment of Order , everything was in opposition to the Erdtree . [ 11 ] Godfrey led Marika's golden armies in the War Against the Giants , [ 12 ] a decisive conflict thay ended with the Giants ' defeat and the confinement of the Fell God 's Flame of Ruin . [ 13 ] This war heralded the birth of the Erdtree , [ 14 ] and the beginning of an age of Order ruled over by Marika and her Elden Lord.
The age of the Erdtree began amidst conflict, and Godfrey was regarded as the "Lord of the Battlefield." [ 15 ] [ 12 ] He fought the Storm Lord alone and emerged the new lord of Stormveil . Later, during the siege of Castle Morne , Godfrey bested a lone hero who wielded a grafted blade and fought for vengeance. [ 16 ] [ 17 ] Godfrey was commander of the Crucible Knights , and Ordovis and his men honored their master by wearing the crest of the axe, a symbol of Godfrey's. [ 18 ]
Godfrey and his offspring with Queen Marika were the first Demigods , known as the Golden Lineage . [ 19 ] His bond with Serosh became an emblem of this lineage, [ 20 ] guiding them as they conquered the Lands Between. [ 21 ] Godfrey's double-headed axe symbolized his warrior's vow of conduct and would later become a symbol of the Golden Lineage. [ 22 ] [ 23 ]
Godfrey's Axe shattered during his Long March
At the end of his campaign, Lord Godfrey's golden armies remained unvanquished and unbowed. [ 12 ] When his last enemy fell, it was said that the golden hue of Godfrey's eyes faded. He found his Grace lost, tattered, and faded.
Godfrey and his warriors were then informed by Queen Marika that she had divested them of their Grace. [ 24 ] She drove them from the Lands Between to wage war in a distant land, where they would live and die. Marika promised Godfrey and his men that after their deaths, [ 25 ] they would regain what she had taken from them. They would return to the Lands Between with the strength required to brandish the Elden Ring .
Thus, Godfrey and his kinfolk became the Tarnished . [ 26 ] They left the Lands Between together on a pilgrimage known as the Long March , at the end of which Godfrey divested himself of kingship and became a simple warrior once more. [ 3 ] [ 27 ]
Godfrey became a chieftain of the Badlands under the name of Hoarah Loux. [ 5 ] The head of his axe had been broken in a battle fought during the Long March. [ 22 ] His loyal warriors honored him by wielding axes of their own, and they became the weapon of choice for Badlands chieftains. [ 28 ]
Hoarah Loux's Grace is returned
At some point, Hoarah Loux died. However, when the Elden Ring was shattered following the death of his son Godwyn the Golden , [ 29 ] the Tarnished that died outside the Lands Between were returned to life by the call of their long-lost Grace. [ 30 ] The Tarnished, who had grown strong in the face of death, crossed the fog and returned to the Lands Between, to stand before the Elden Ring and become Elden Lord. [ 31 ] Godfrey was among those who made their way back to the Lands Between.
Godfrey and Serosh prepare for battle
After the Tarnished champion has claimed the Great Runes , burned the Erdtree, and unbound the Rune of Death , [ 32 ] they return to the city of Leyndell and approach the Erdtree. At the Elden Throne , they find Godfrey, Serosh on his back, mourning the death of his son Morgott , whom the Tarnished had previously slain. [ 33 ]
Godfrey rises to his feet and addresses the Tarnished. He acknowledges their effort; however, he declares his intention to seek an audience once again. [ 34 ] The two Tarnished do battle, and Godfrey finds himself overpowered. The former Elden Lord grabs the head of Serosh, thanks him for his service, and then tears him from his back. [ 35 ] Drenched in the blood of his loyal regent, Godfrey resumes the fight, now as the savage Hoarah Loux. [ 4 ] Nevertheless, the Tarnished defeats Hoarah Loux, who declares that their strength befits a crown. [ 36 ]
This is a boss fight against a golden, spectral version of Godfrey. He is fought within the Erdtree Sanctuary, accessed by climbing up a large root south of the West Capital Rampart Site of Grace. This battle is not optional as he must be defeated to progress Leyndell further and continue the story. Compared to the later encounter, this version of Godfrey has a greatly reduced moveset, mainly consisting of close-range axe swings. He can create areas of effect by stomping or smashing his axe into the ground, and he may also throw his axe at the player from a distance.
Nepheli Loux, Warrior and Shabriri are both available as summons for this fight, provided their questlines have been completed. Like the first battle, this fight is not optional and must be defeated to reach the final bosses of the game.
Godfrey will usually initiate the fight by throwing his axe at the player and then dashing after it.
Godfrey has a stomp attack similar to that of the Crucible Knights, causing spikes to come out of the ground that are easier to dodge by jumping than to i-frame with a roll. He will generally follow up on the spike stomp with a series of axe swings, but can do a second stomp at any time, even repeatedly.
Godfrey's primary offense will be axe swing combos. They can be dodge rolled safely and involve enough delays for the player to sneak in a hit before having to dodge again.
He retains his moves from the earlier fight, with the addition of more close-range axe attacks and some abilities that generate earthquakes.
After his health drops below 50%, a cutscene plays and phase 2 begins. Godfrey no longer has Serosh or his axe, and has an almost entirely new, grappling-based fighting style.
Phase 2 always starts with him rushing towards the player with a delayed command grab. He will always briefly go into slow-motion mid-jump, which can roll-catch. He will attempt to grab the player like this multiple times over the course of phase 2. Properly rolling out of the way of it gives you one of the largest time windows to attack him out of his entire phase 2.
He will do many other grab attacks, ground-slams, leap attacks, delayed kicks and delayed stomp attacks. Panic-rolling and blocking is not recommended.
When he begins to crack the ground after a leap attack by smashing his hands into the ground, the player must run away from him as far as they can, otherwise they will get blown up by an explosion that is very difficult to roll through. He often announces this attack by knocking the player away from him with a roar.
Wilful traitors, all. Thy kind are all of a piece. Pillagers. Emboldened by the flame of ambition. Have it writ upon thy meagre grave: Felled by King Morgott! Last of all kings. - Morgott, the Omen King
Morgott, the Omen King, is a remembrance boss in Elden Ring . He is a Demigod and a Shardbearer who is encountered in Leyndell, Royal Capital . He is not an optional boss and must be defeated to unlock Mountaintops of the Giants and progress the story.
Morgott was cursed from birth
Morgott was a direct offspring of Lord Godfrey and Queen Marika , and the rightful heir to their Golden Lineage . [ 1 ] Despite his royal pedigree, he and his twin brother, Mohg , [ 2 ] were born with accursed blood that caused tangled horns to sprout from their infant bodies. Once revered as divine aspect of the Crucible , these growths branded them as Omen spurned by the Erdtree and excluded from its grace . [ 3 ] Though spared the painful excision of their horns, they were nonetheless banished to the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds beneath Leyndell, Royal Capital . [ 4 ] A Regal Omen Bairn was made in secret to honor Morgott in a long-standing tradition. [ 5 ] [ 6 ]
Unlike his twin, Morgott's devotion to the Erdtree never wavered. [ 3 ] He renounced his omen blood, extracted a portion of it, and sealed it away. The blood that formed Morgott's Cursed Sword caused it to shimmer in shifting hues, and so he encased it in stone and wielded it like a cane. [ 7 ] Several horns were removed from his brow line.
Morgott's Great Rune
When Queen Marika shattered the Elden Ring , Morgott claimed one of the Great Runes , which proved that he was indeed the Lord of Leyndell. With Leyndell in disarray, Morgott claimed the Erdtree capital for himself and defended it from the assault of his fellow demigods. While he succeeded in securing Leyndell against outsiders, he found that the Erdtree would not admit him, or anyone else, to claim the title of Elden Lord. Despite the fact that he had been reviled as an accursed fiend by the Golden Order , Morgott took it upon himself to become the Erdtree's protector.
He assumed the name Margit the Fell Omen during the Shattering , slaughtering champions who approached the Erdtree in the hopes of becoming Elden Lord. [ 8 ] Under this pseudonym, he also lead the Night's Cavalry , who assisted him in the killing of great warriors, knights and champions. [ 9 ] Simultaneously, he ruled Leyndell as the Veiled Monarch. [ 10 ] He was able to project himself to various parts of the Lands Between .
When the Tarnished returned, Morgott and his Night's Cavalry hunted them throughout the realm. Morgott first encounters the Tarnished at Stormgate , where he tests their mettle as Margit before allowing them to challenge Godrick for his Great Rune . Later, he ambushes the hero again by disguising a commoner as himself in the war-torn Capital Outskirts .
The Tarnished gains entrance to Leyndell, Royal Capital and challenges Morgott at the Elden Throne after claiming two shards of the Elden Ring . Denouncing the Tarnished and his siblings as willful traitors, Morgott launches his assault. As he falters during the battle, he unleashes his sealed curse to aid him, though he feels unbearable shame in doing so. Despite his efforts, he is ultimately defeated and stripped of his Great Rune .
Without his Rune, Morgott is freed from his curse, and transforms into an enfeebled old man. He warns the Tarnished the impenetrable thorns would bar them from becoming Elden Lord , just as they rejected him. After the Cardinal Sin and the release of the Rune of Death , Morgott was finally able to truly die. At the Ashen Capital , Godfrey returned just in time to find his son in his final moments, cradling him tenderly as Morgott's body crumbled into golden dust. [ 11 ] [ 12 ]
Morgott is a highly aggressive and fast-moving enemy, chaining together attacks in rapid succession while leaving few openings. His curved sword inflicts blood loss on impact, while the holy armaments he summons deal holy damage. He has ranged attacks, such as his throwing knives and spear, and utilises jumps, cartwheels, and dashes to close or create distance.
Once his health drops to 50%, Morgott performs an area of effect attack in which his cursed blood erupts from the ground. His blade becomes infused with his cursed blood, and he gains a number of bloodflame-based attacks. He may also summon golden blades that rain down from the sky.
The arena is a wide, circular platform with no obstacles, aside from the throne which will break if hit.
"Foul Tarnished, In search of the Elden Ring. Emboldened by the flame of ambition. Someone must extinguish thy flame. Let it be Margit the Fell!" - Margit
Margit the Fell Omen is a boss in Elden Ring .
Margit is an Omen who gained notoriety during The Shattering , in which he slaughtered countless champions who harbored ambitions for Lordship, [ 1 ] stacking high their corpses during the Second Defense of Leyndell. [ 2 ]
He is encountered by the Tarnished at the gates of Stormveil Castle , where he makes clear his disdain towards the Tarnished, and attempts to put an end to their quest for Lordship. Although he is defeated, Margit's voice is heard as he disappears.
Later, he appears once more outside Leyndell, Royal Capital , initially in the guise of a Commoner . After being defeated by the Tarnished once more, he vanishes, leaving the corpse of the commoner behind.
After the Tarnished has made their way through Leyndell and reached the Elden Throne, Margit stands between them and the Erdtree . He repudiates the other Demigods , calling them all traitors, before revealing himself to be Morgott, the Omen King , a Demigod of the Golden Lineage, [ 3 ] who took up the responsibility of protecting the Erdtree, despite receiving no love in return. [ 4 ] He fights the Tarnished once more and, upon his defeat, he warns them that the Erdtree will reject them, as it did him. [ 5 ]
As the Tarnished approaches the gates of Stormveil Castle, Margit will materialize on a nearby tower and jump down the courtyard to confront his opponent. This encounter will not take place if Morgott, the Omen King is defeated beforehand.
As the Tarnished treks through the Capital Outskirts, Margit will possess the body of a nearby Commoner to once again hunt down his enemy. This encounter does not count as a boss fight, and it is possible to run away when he appears.

Margit is quick and relentless, his powerful combos and rapid follow-ups make it hard to find a window to punish him, but there are two types of attacks that leave him open amply: overhead strikes and ground stabs.
Since both can be easily evaded by running to the right, the key to victory is learning how to bait out these moves, which is generally done by dodging away from the first part of a combo, while remaining just in range for him to keep going through with it fully.
His jumping stab can also be exploited, as he always tells this move by tossing his holy dagger twice, while the player is far way: as he finishes throwing his weapons, walk towards him and dodge through the jump attack.
Without being particularly weak to anything, he still takes some additional damage from slashing and fire attacks, and he can also be poisoned and bled, which makes the Uchigatana a particularly favorable choice against this boss.
While standard light attacks won't impact him much, an aggressive playstyle made of jump attacks, charged attacks and Ash of War will see Margit repeatedly falling on his knees, leaving him open to a critical strike.
Margit's Shackle can be used during this phase to temporarily stun him, opening him to attacks. This will not work in phase 2.
As his health drops to 60% or below, he will enter Phase 2 always executing the same hammer sweep plus jumping strike.
Even with the addition of some new moves, the bait-and-punish strategy of Phase 1 is still applicable.
While the moves made with his holy weapons cannot be parried, the majority of his regular weapon attacks are susceptible to interruption.
Margit's arena is a narrow and long pathway with chasms on each side. While the boss himself cannot fall to his death, the player must constantly reposition himself to avoid having their back against the wall or the brink.
The area is also filled with obstacles and while the weapons scattered through out can be broken by dodging into them, the wooden barricades might just get in the way of a safety roll.
One must also not overestimate the length of the arena, as Margit's gap-closing attacks are fast and cover a long distance.
I command thee, kneel! I am the lord of all that is golden! - Godrick the Grafted
Godrick the Grafted ( 接ぎ木のゴドリック , Tsugiki no Godorikku ) is a Boss in Elden Ring . He is a Demigod and a Shardbearer encountered in Stormveil Castle .
Godrick is a descendant of the Golden Lineage , the bloodline that began with Queen Marika the Eternal and her first consort Godfrey . [ 1 ] Only a distant relation of Marika's line, his divine blood was sorely diluted, and he was viewed as the runt of the litter. [ 2 ] Godrick idolized the first Elden Lord , desiring his ancestor to witness his feats. [ 3 ] He wielded an axe emblazoned with a lion , a symbol of Godfrey, [ 4 ] [ 5 ] and furnished his army with the Erdtree and Serosh emblems of the Golden Lineage. [ 6 ] [ 7 ] Though he styled himself “lord of all that is golden,” [ 8 ] he commanded far less respect than his forebear and was despised by many of his own servants. [ 9 ]
After the Elden Ring was shattered , Godrick inherited the Great Rune from the center of the Elden Ring, referred to as the anchor ring . During The Shattering , he was hounded from Leyndell, Royal Capital . He claimed a multitude of treasures, including the Mimic's Veil , [ 10 ] and hid among the womenfolk to flee the city. [ 11 ] Godrick made his way south, settling in Limgrave with an army of soldiers who had fled Leyndell. [ 12 ] He took up residence in Stormveil Castle, using it as a refuge to hide from General Radahn . [ 13 ] When Malenia marched southward, Godrick insulted her, [ 14 ] leading to a confrontation that left him beaten and humiliated, forced to beg for mercy. [ 15 ]
Godrick again retreated to Stormveil Castle to practice grafting , the forbidden art of attaching the parts of other beings to oneself to gain power. [ 16 ] When the Tarnished returned to the Lands Between , Godrick sent his soldiers on Tarnished hunts, seeking new subjects to graft. [ 17 ] He also produced Grafted Scions ; abhorrent beings comprised of many different limbs, seemingly grafted onto children.
The Tarnished journeys to Stormveil Castle in search of Godrick's Great Rune, on the advice of White Mask Varré [ 18 ] and Melina . [ 19 ] The castle shows many examples of his grafting: severed limbs hanging in the dining hall, a dismembered Troll over a courtyard, and piles of corpses, including the companions of Roderika . [ 20 ] Eventually the Tarnished finds Godrick in a graveyard, addressing a dead dragon impaled on a statue . [ 21 ] He grafts the dragon's head to his own arm mid-fight, but is defeated, and his Great Rune is claimed.
Later, Nepheli Loux can become the lord of Limgrave at the appointment of Kenneth Haight . [ 22 ]
The fight begins after a cutscene. Godrick primarily uses his axe and enlarged left arm, generating cyclones and quakes for area-of-effect damage. He rolls to reposition and uses a homing wind projectile.
At roughly 60% HP, a cutscene plays, and he grafts the dragon's head to his arm. He gains ranged and area fire attacks layered onto his Phase 1 kit.
The arena is a narrow, paved approach flanked by graveyards, with a wider entrance near the steps. Movement through gravestones is possible, but it can hinder dodging.

He is fought as a challenge at the end of each day. However, he can only be encountered after Day 1 of both the Augur , Fissure in the Fog , and the Night Aspect expeditions.
Foul trespasser. Send word far and wide. Of the last Queen of Caria, Rennala of the Full Moon. And the majesty of the night she conjureth. - Ranni the Witch
Rennala, Queen of the Full Moon ( 満月の女王、レナラ , Mangetsu no Joō, Renara ) is a character in Elden Ring . She is a Shardbearer Boss encountered in the Academy of Raya Lucaria . While this encounter is not required to advance the story, Rennala must be defeated to unlock the ability to respec , Moonlight Altar , and " Age of the Stars " ending.
The young Lunar Princess was an astrologer who gazed at the night sky and chased the stars . In her youth, Rennala and her younger sister, Rellana , encountered moons that one day made them champions. [ 1 ] Hers was an enchanting full moon . Later, she bewitched the Academy of Raya Lucaria with her lunar magic, becoming its master. She prohibited study of the primeval current at the academy, exiling its founders, Azur and Lusat . She established the house of Caria as royalty and anointed the enchanted Carian Knights , heroes of the highest honors. [ 2 ] [ 3 ] [ 4 ] [ 5 ] [ 6 ]
When the sorceries of the Carians were still only the prototypes of the latter sword-phalanx sorceries . [ 7 ] , Rennala gifted a braid of her hair to Rellana, who disavowed her birthright to join Messmer the Impaler in his Crusade in the Realm of Shadow . [ 8 ]
In the age of the Erdtree , a champion known as Radagon led Queen Marika 's armies against Liurnia of the Lakes . Rennala and the academy rallied forces to repel the invasion. She led her Glintstones Knights and, [ 4 ] despite numbering fewer then twenty, their magic made them a match for even the champions of gold in battle. [ 9 ] Two Liurnian Wars were fought, both of which saw no clear victor. [ 10 ] [ 11 ]
Radagon ended the Second Liurnian War by cleansing himself with Celestial Dew . Repenting his territorial aggressions, he swore his love to Rennala. [ 12 ] They married at the Church of Vows , uniting the houses of the Erdtree and the Moon. [ 13 ] As a Carian Queen, Rennala bestowed Radagon a Moon greatsword in accordance with a long-standing tradition. [ 14 ] [ 15 ] They had three children: Radahn , Rykard , and Ranni . [ 16 ] Rennala led young Ranni by the hand to meet her Dark Moon . [ 17 ]
Later, Radagon gifted an amber egg , the Great Rune of the Unborn , to Rennala, [ 18 ] and left her side to become the second King Consort of Queen Marika , receiving the title of second Elden Lord . [ 19 ] When Radagon left, Rennala's heart left with him.
Realizing their heartbroken queen was no champion at all, the Academy rebelled against the Carian Royal Family and Rennala was locked away in the grand library . [ 20 ] [ 21 ] Clutching the amber egg left to her by Radagon, she dissociated, devoting herself to the grim art of reincarnation . She would use it on Juvenile Scholars found around her, calling them her "sweetings", continuously rebirthing them in an imperfect process which would leave their memories fading into oblivion. [ 22 ] The children born anew by Rennala were all frail and short-lived, imperfect beings, each and all. [ 23 ]
Rennala remained in the Grand Library throughout the reign of Lord Radagon and the ensuing Shattering war . She hovered idly in the air, clutching her egg, while her reborn Juvenile Scholars sang a lullaby that shielded her in a golden, moonlike bubble.
If the Great Rune separates from Rennala, a protective mechanism activates, releasing a dense black fog. The disembodied voice of Ranni the Witch warns intruders as an illusory image of Rennala emerges from the darkness to battle the player upon a moonlit sea. This apparition reflects Rennala as she once was, at the height of her power.
If the illusion is defeated, the present Rennala regains her egg and sits quietly in her bassinet at the center of the library, calling softly to her timid sweetings.
A tall, barefooted woman with an immaculate, pale complexion and lustrous black hair. She is dressed in deep blue and red robes with gold trim and wears a large hat curved like the crescent moon .
Throughout both phases, Rennala resists magic but is more vulnerable to physical attacks.
Rennala's first phase occurs in a circular room with an open inner area and a more narrow outer area, divided by bookcases. Rennala floats around the room encased in a golden sphere that prevents her from taking damage. The majority of her Juvenile Scholars congregate in the inner arena, however a few can be found hiding behind the bookcases.
Rennala rarely attacks directly during this phase. Instead, the Juvenile Scholars lunge, breathe fire, and use telekinesis to assault the player with the books and globes. They also drop chandeliers from the ceiling if the player stands underneath them. However, Rennala periodically converts scholars to gravestones, which she sends flying towards the player. She also summons new Scholars to replace those the player has slain.
One of the Scholars sings, surrounded by a golden aura. The song grows louder as the player draws near. Hitting the singing Scholar at least once—without necessarily killing them—causes another to begin singing. Disrupt three singing Scholars to shatter Rennala’s sphere, dropping her to the ground and leaving her vulnerable. While she lies stunned, the Scholars cease their attacks, giving the player an opening to strike. After a few seconds, Rennala releases a golden explosion and rises again, her protective sphere restored. Repeating this process several times creates additional opportunities to damage her.
Defeating Rennala triggers a cutscene, and advances the fight to Phase Two. A spell placed by Ranni the Witch on the amber egg activates, releasing a dense fog of darkness.
After the cutscene, the arena transforms into a vast, moonlit watery plane with no obstacles or clutter. Ranni's illusory Rennala engages the player directly with a full health bar. She relies primarily on ranged magical attacks but also swings her staff to strike if the player approaches too closely.
When her health drops below 60%, she begins summoning spirits for assistance. Each time she summons, a glowing circle expands around her, dealing damage to anything within it. She can call forth a Bloodhound Knight , three wolves , a Flying Dragon , or a Troll Knight , each lasting only a few seconds before vanishing. During this phase, Rennala moves more evasively, making it difficult for melee fighters to land consistent attack chains.
Moving away from Rennala's homing attacks is simple, as there is nothing to get stuck on or blocked in by. However, there is nothing to separate Rennala from her summoned allies.
After defeating her, Rennala becomes an NPC , remaining in the library where she was fought in phase 1. As an NPC she offers two services: Rebirth allows the player to reallocate levels to different stats at the cost of a Larval Tear , while Cosmetics allows the player to alter their character's appearance, which is the same function that the mirror in Roundtable Hold has.
When Sorceress Sellen moves to the Academy of Raya Lucaria during her questline, she will temporarily occupy Rennala's spot, while Rennala will move behind one of the bookshelves in the library. She will return to her usual place once Sellen's questline is completed.
I was born a champion's cub. Now I am the Lord of the Battlefield's lion. - Radahn's Redmane Helm
Starscourge Radahn ( 星砕きのラダーン , Hoshikudaki no Radān ) , also known as General Radahn , the Red Lion General , and later as Promised Consort Radahn and Radahn, Consort of Miquella , is an optional Demigod boss in Elden Ring and a mandatory God boss in Elden Ring : ; Shadow of the Erdtree .
General Radahn was feared as the strongest Demigod during the Shattering . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ] [ 4 ] This Shardbearer must be defeated to access the Realm of Shadow and achieve the " Age of the Stars " ending.
Red-maned Radahn was the son of Radagon , a champion of the Erdtree , and Queen Rennala of the Full Moon , head of both the Carian royal family and Academy of Raya Lucaria , born after the Second Liurnian War . He had two siblings, Rykard and Ranni . Radahn inherited his father's flaming red hair and was fond of its heroic implications. [ 5 ] From a young age, he was enamored with the Elden Lord Godfrey . Attempting to emulate his idol, Radahn adorned his armor with lions, the symbol of Godfrey and Serosh . [ 6 ]
At some point, the first Elden Lord , Godfrey, was robbed of grace and hounded from the Lands Between . Radahn's father, Radagon, left Rennala to become Queen Marika's new consort and the second Elden Lord. [ 7 ] Radahn and his siblings were thus raised to demigod status by their new step-mother, Marika. [ 8 ]
In their youth, Radahn's Empyrean half-brother Miquella deeply admired him for his kindness and strength, seeing in him the qualities of a lord . When he decided to pursue godhood , he made a vow with Radahn that, [ 9 ] upon his deific return, he would take Radahn as his consort. [ 10 ] In return, Miquella would uphold some unspecified part of the vow. [ 11 ]
Not wanting to abandon his scrawny but beloved steed, Leonard , [ 12 ] [ 13 ] Radahn studied gravitational magic in Sellia under a master who was an Alabaster Lord . [ 14 ] Radahn befriended the Albinauric Gaius , a senior disciple of his teacher, and the two formed a competitive yet friendly rivalry. Radahn's step-brother Messmer the Impaler was also friends with Gaius, and the two became as elder brothers to Radahn. [ 15 ]
Mastering gravitational magic allowed Radahn to manipulate the forces of gravity and challenge the stars themselves. [ 16 ] During the Starscourge Conflict , Radahn saved Sellia by conquering the stars and arrested their cycles, delaying fate . Having earned himself the moniker "Starscourge," he engraved the gravity crest upon his blades. [ 4 ] [ 17 ]
Radahn's soldiers were known as the Redmanes for the red-maned lion raising a sword in the image of Radahn on their surcoats. [ 18 ] The longest serving of the Redmane Knights was Ogha , who studied gravitational techniques alongside Radahn in Sellia. [ 19 ] It was popularly said that the Redmanes knew no weakness. [ 20 ] At an unknown period in time, Jerren , a guest of the Carian royals, became a guest commander for Radahn's armies, and they swore a mutual oath of honorable death. [ 21 ] [ 22 ] During his youth, Radahn witnessed the valor of a gladiator called Freyja , who he asked to become another member of his knights; an offer Freyja accepted. [ 23 ]
Radahn duels Malenia at the Battle of Aeonia
At some point following the Night of Black Knives , Queen Marika shattered the Elden Ring , and her offspring acquired the Great Runes. The maddening taint of their newfound strength led to the Shattering , a war between Marika's demigod descendants, each seeking to become the new ruler of the Lands Between. [ 24 ]
From his stronghold of Redmane Castle in the Caelid Wilds , Radahn led his armies against the forces of the other demigods. Radahn tried to challenge Godrick the Grafted in Limgrave , but the latter hid in Stormveil Castle . [ 25 ]
By the end of the Shattering, only Radahn and his half-sister Malenia, Blade of Miquella were left standing. The two fought to a stalemate in the Battle of Aeonia , their duel ending inconclusively when Malenia unleashed her Scarlet Rot . [ 26 ] As the Scarlet Aeonia flower blossomed, Malenia whispered in Radahn's ear, "Miquella awaits thee, O promised consort." [ 27 ]
The Scarlet Rot ravaged Caelid and consumed Radahn from the inside, eating away at his psyche but failing to kill him. Following the Battle of Aeonia, Radahn roams the Wailing Dunes as a mindless beast who devours the flesh of friend and foe alike, howling at the sky. [ 28 ] Without their commander, the Redmane Knights burned the crest on the left breast of their armor to indicate their resolve not to return home, and to serve as a bulwark against the spread of the rot in Caelid using fire . [ 29 ] [ 30 ]
Despite his madness, Radahn continues to ride his scrawny steed, as well as halt the motions of the stars. The Radahn Festival has been organized by his men in Castle Redmane to celebrate his last battle. It is a gathering of mighty warriors who might finally put the General out of his misery and claim his Great Rune for themselves. The festival serves as Jerren 's way of fulfilling his oath of honorable death to Radahn. [ 31 ] [ 32 ]
Upon the participation of a Tarnished Champion , the Radahn Festival is a success, and Radahn is freed from his tortured existence. His death causes the stars to resume their cycles, some of which come crashing down upon the Lands Between. One such falling star lands in Limgrave, opening the path to Nokron, Eternal City , and allowing the fate of Ranni the Witch to progress. [ 33 ] [ 34 ]
Following Radahn's defeat, his soul met its end. However, Miquella sought to revive it, [ 35 ] still desiring for Radahn to be his lord consort. Miquella successfully revived Radahn, placing his soul into a vessel made from the remains of Mohg, Lord of Blood , another Demigod slain by the same Tarnished who had defeated Radahn. [ 36 ] The Tarnished encounters the newly-resurrected Radahn at the Gate of Divinity at the top of Enir-Ilim . Radahn stands guard as Miquella completes his ascension to godhood and battles the Tarnished once more. During the ensuing battle, Miquella steps out of the Gate of Divinity and embraces Radahn as his consort and fights the Tarnished with Radahn. [ 37 ] The Tarnished triumphs over Radahn and Miquella, thus preventing Miquella's age of compassion. [ 38 ]
Radahn's Great Rune
Torrent can be called during this fight and is useful for closing distance and evading Radahn's ranged attacks.
Multiple NPCs are available to be summoned during the fight, and their summons can be located throughout the arena. Six can be summoned at a time, and once a summon sign is used it will vanish, however each NPC has multiple summon signs that can be used.
The following eight champions are available:
The player will spawn some distance away from Radahn, with the boss visible at the top of a dune in the distance. Immediately, Radahn will begin firing volleys of arrows which rain down from above, homing in on the player, as well as gravity arrows. The latter can be avoided by hiding behind the clusters of weapons dug into the ground, however the weapons will break when struck. Riding Torrent will make it easier to avoid the volleys. Summon signs can be found in clusters all around the arena, and can be used to summon NPCs to assist in the fight.
Once the player is close enough, Radahn will begin attacking using his swords. He is very mobile, using his horse to cover distance easily. He also uses a number of gravity-based attacks, such as Cragblade, gravity waves, and Collapsing Stars.
Once his health is below 50%, Radahn will launch himself into the sky, disappearing for several seconds. He will then come crashing down in a ball of fire, dealing devastating damage to anyone caught in the impact. Radahn now gains the ability to raise four floating rocks, which will hover beside him and then launch at the player or their summons. He also gains the ability to float into the air and spin rapidly while charging.
The Wailing Dunes is a very large arena consisting of many tall dunes, with Radahn initially standing at the top of the largest dune close to the centre of the area. Clusters of weapons can be found stuck in the sand, and can be used to hide from Radahn's arrows. Summon signs can be found throughout the arena, often in clusters of two or three.
The second encounter with Radahn serves as the final boss of the Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree expansion. The first phase is Promised Consort Radahn and the second is Radahn, Consort of Miquella .
Just like in the base game, players will spawn a distance away from Radahn. While retaining his gravity magic, and as his soul now possessed Mohg's remains, Radahn now employs Bloodflame, and seamlessly switches between the two elemental magics while in combat. To defeat him, it is always important to time your attacks in between Radahn's string of attacks or pull off counters at the very end of a combo. Because of his recovery time, this makes his boss battle complicated, as he can launch other attacks almost instantly after finishing a heavy attack. As a result, it is important to note that patience and appropriate timing are the keys to defeating Radahn. The optimal moment to attack is when he finished his basic sword combos, and would take a brief pause to recover.
At the start of his boss battle, he will nearly always use a gravity attack to prevent players from summoning or buffs upon entry into the boss battle. Because of this, players are recommended to use buffs before accessing the boss and cast summons right after dodging the initial attack. During his first phase, Radahn will use a flurry of combos aside from special abilities such as a Bloodflame Slash and his Gravity attacks. After being reduced to 65% of his health, this will trigger a cutscene leading to Phase 2.
In this phase, Radahn's previous attacks are improved and he gains new powerful abilities. Most of them are Holy-powered and have a wider AoE. Overall, while his attacks become more lethal, Radahn is now faster in speed, now capable of creating mirror images to attack and using strong Holy-based abilities, making the boss battle more difficult and challenging. However, despite gaining immense power, Radahn's health has already been reduced to 75%, allowing players to gain a slight edge. It is important to capitalize on the pauses of Radahn's combo attacks, as there are opportunities to strike. Constantly taking advantage of them can deplete his health and because Radahn's attacks can be very punishing if caught off-guard, you have to be prepared to switch between offensive and defensive at times.
While Radahn can still perform similar combos from Phase 1, they have an additional Holy damage explosion at the end. As Miquella is now mounted on his back, he can do a grab attack where he will glow and jump at the player in order to grab them. If successful, Radahn will bring them close to Miquella, who will then place the player under a charm. While this doesn't deal any damage, if Radahn successfully grabs the player a second time while they are charmed, this will ultimately result in instant death. Using Miquella's Great Rune will undo the charm.
The arena consists of a very wide area, with a rough white surface filled with gray-white decomposed corpses, which can be found sticking from the ground. At the other end of the arena, stands the Gate of Divinity itself, where Miquella will step out in divine aspect in the second phase.
Join the Serpent King, as family... Together, we will devour the very gods! - Rykard, Lord of Blasphemy
Rykard, Lord of Blasphemy is a boss in Elden Ring . He is a Demigod and a Shardbearer who is encountered in Volcano Manor .
Rykard was born the son of Radagon , a champion of the Erdtree , and Queen Rennala , head of both the Carian Royal Family and the Academy of Raya Lucaria . [ 1 ] He had two siblings, Radahn and Ranni .
At some point, the first Elden Lord, Godfrey , was robbed of grace and hounded from the Lands Between . Rykard's father, Radagon, left Rennala to become Queen Marika's new consort and the second Elden Lord . [ 2 ] Rykard and his siblings were thus raised to demigods by their new stepmother, Marika. [ 3 ]
Under the Golden Order , Rykard was a ruthless justiciar who commanded a company of inquisitors. [ 4 ] His inquisitors persecuted and mercilessly tortured those considered heretics to the Golden Order, such as the Albinaurics . He spent time in the volcanic Mt. Gelmir, where he discovered the ancient magma hexes of a forgotten serpent-worshiping religion native to the region, which he brought back into practical use as new sorceries. [ 5 ] [ 6 ] Rykard also travelled to a foreign land where he encountered a dancer by the name of Tanith , who he would eventually take as his consort. [ 1 ]
Rykard was also known for the construction of the Iron Virgins , automatons which were capable of both battlefield carnage and abducting victims to transport them to the Volcano Manor. [ 7 ]
Rykard's budding blasphemous inclinations led him to assist his sister, Ranni, in orchestrating the Night of Black Knives. On the night of the plot, Ranni rewarded Rykard with a slab of rock engraved with the traces of the Rune of Death, which would allow him to challenge the black beast of Destined Death , should the coming trespass one day transpire. [ 8 ]
At some point following the the Night of Black Knives, Queen Marika shattered the Elden Ring , and her offspring acquired the Great Runes. The maddening taint of their newfound strength led to the Shattering, a war between Marika's demigod descendants, each seeking to become the new ruler of the Lands Between. [ 9 ]
Rykard was indignant, and viewed the Erdtree and the gods demanding that the demigods fight over miserly scraps of power to be debasing. [ 10 ] He launched a blasphemous campaign against the Erdtree and the Greater Will . [ 11 ] When he turned to heresy, taking by force became the rule, the gods themselves being no different. [ 12 ] Rykard's ambitions, though blasphemous, marked him a worthy sovereign, [ 13 ] and drew many followers to his cause who admired his heroic aspirations. His rebels were known as the Recusants .
Based in the Volcano Manor on Mt. Gelmir, his forces battled the armies of the Leyndell in what would become the most appalling battle of the Shattering, [ 14 ] a wretched, unending war with no glory. [ 15 ] Acts of cannibalism became a sickening reality across the battlefields, and some forces from both sides became afflicted with the Frenzied Flame sickness.
At some point during the Shattering, Rykard fed himself, Great Rune and all, to the blasphemous serpent that dwelled inside Mt. Gelmir, [ 3 ] an ancient traitor to the Erdtree, [ 16 ] merging with the creature. In the final moments before being devoured, he briefly had a vision of the future wherein he witnessed a serpent devouring the world. [ 17 ]
Following this, his lofty ambition degraded into gluttonous depravity. [ 18 ] He fed on his greatest champions, and in the bowels of the serpent, they became the lord's family. [ 19 ] Disturbed by what had become of their master and by the costly battles waged in his name, Rykard's forces abandoned him. [ 18 ] [ 20 ] Some attempted to put him to rest by searching for a mighty weapon capable of killing their lord. Such a weapon was found in the Serpent-Hunter , an enchanted spear crafted to hunt an immortal serpent in the distant past. [ 21 ] However, all attempts made to take his life failed. The spear would come to reside in Rykard's chambers, left by a former Recusant who hoped a worthy champion might one day appear to wield it and spare the once-noble Rykard from further dishonor. [ 22 ]
When Rykard gave himself to the elder serpent, the birth of the man-serpents followed, [ 23 ] the deformed offspring of a repellent birthing ritual. [ 24 ] [ 25 ] One such man-serpent, known as Zorayas , would go on to be adopted by Tanith, and learn to assume an illusory human form in which she went by Rya. She was unaware of the origins of her birth, as Tanith concealed the truth of the Volcano Manor from her and insisted she was born of the grace of a king. [ 26 ] It is implied that the woman known as Daedicar was one such woman subjected to the ritual, the biological mother of Zorayas and other man-serpents. [ 27 ]
At some point before giving himself to the serpent, Rykard offered Tanith the Tonic of Forgetfulness to purge her memories of him. However, she refused, claiming "My Lord, there could be no greater distress than to forget you." [ 28 ] Tanith was the only human known to stand with Rykard after he merged with the serpent of blasphemy; as in that moment, she was truly charmed by him. [ 29 ] The Crucible Knight bodyguard of Tanith may have also served the Volcano Manor before Rykard was devoured, and as such, would have been the second human known to remain loyal, but this remains unknown. Tanith would continue her lord's legacy by leading a new force of Recusants, recruiting unsuspecting Tarnished after their return to the Lands Between following the end of the Shattering. The worthiest of these Tarnished champions would be granted an audience with Rykard, which ended with them being devoured by the serpentine demigod to increase his power further.
Eventually, a Tarnished champion managed to reach Rykard's chambers, and defeated the serpentine demigod to claim his Great Rune. Rykard took notice of this and awoke to confront the Tarnished, then pulled out a massive sword from the serpent's mouth, while boasting that they would join the Serpent King as family. After a hard battle, Rykard was ultimately slain by the Tarnished. Upon his death, he claimed "A serpent never dies", proven true when his initially vanished corpse began to regenerate. After Rykard is slain, Tanith suggested she planned to soon depart, having no reason to remain at Volcano Manor. However, afterwards she secretly journeyed to Rykard's chambers and attempted to eat his tremendous corpse, muttering her hopes that Rykard might live on within her, just as he had the serpent.
Rykard's Great Rune
The Serpent-Hunter can be found sticking out of a pile of corpses near the entrance to the arena, and can be obtained without alerting the boss. This weapon makes the fight significantly easier, as it produces blades of light when swung that allow for long-distance attacks.
Defeating this boss will terminate Tanith's questline, regardless of how far one has progressed it. Any Volcano Manor targets not yet unlocked will also be missed.
The God-Devouring Serpent is slow-moving, surrounded by a pool of magma. The magma makes it difficult to get close without taking damage, however the Serpent-Hunter allows for one to attack from a safer distance. It uses a combination of quick biting attacks and eruptions of magma, as well as a poison attack.
After reducing the Serpent's health to 0, a cutscene plays and phase 2 begins. Rykard, armed with a sword, moves around the arena similarly to the Serpent, however his moveset is almost entirely new.
Rykard's arena is a spacious cavern, dotted with piles of corpses and tall corpse pillars, which can be broken by Rykard's attacks. The size of the arena is helpful for avoiding Rykard's Rancor and Rancor Rain, as one can run around the room until the attack ends.
I am Malenia. Blade of Miquella. And I have never known defeat. - Malenia
Malenia, Blade of Miquella , later known as Malenia, Goddess of Rot , is an optional remembrance Boss in Elden Ring . She is a Demigod Shardbearer who is encountered in Elphael, Brace of the Haligtree .
Malenia and Miquella found comfort in their childhood
