A Demigod daughter of Queen Marika the Eternal and her second Elden Lord , King Consort Radagon , Malenia was born during the age of the Elden Ring . Like her elder twin brother, Miquella , [ 1 ] a dreadful curse afflicted her from birth. The Scarlet Rot , an incurable, radiating sickness, ravaged Malenia, threatening to consume her from within. Although her condition eventually claimed her eyes and several limbs, the Two Fingers identified her as an Empyrean , a candidate to replace her mother as the god of a new age. [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
Miquella worked to undo the curses they had both inherited. While unable to find a cure for his sister within the Golden Order , Miquella designed a needle of unalloyed gold to keep the rot at bay. [ 4 ] He also crafted the prostheses that enabled her to continue fighting. [verification needed] At some point, Malenia encountered the legendary blind swordsman of the Flowing Curved Sword , who had long ago sealed away an Outer God of Rot . [ 5 ] The swordsman became her master, [ 6 ] enabling her to gain wings of unparalleled strength. [ 7 ] Malenia eventually became a peerless warrior and her brother's sworn blade and protector.
Malenia's Great Rune
After the Elden Ring was shattered , Malenia claimed a shard of the fractured Elden Ring . [ 2 ] She attracted loyal Cleanrot Knights , who vowed to fight next to her, despite the inevitable, gradual putrefaction of their flesh. [ 8 ] During the Shattering , Malenia led an army that marched south from the Haligtree down the Bellum Highway . She won many battles against the other Demigods, even humbling fellow Shardbearer , Godrick the Grafted , [ 9 ] who groveled at her feet for mercy after first insulting her and then suffering defeat.
Malenia and Radahn in Caelid
Malenia and her half-brother Radahn would eventually be the last two demigods left standing in the conflict. Their forces clashed in the Caelid Wilds , and the two fought the Battle of Aeonia , a bitter duel to fulfill an unhonored vow . In the midst of the combat with Radahn, Malenia unleashes Scarlet Rot, resulting in her first Scarlet Aeonia . [ 10 ] [ 11 ]
The rot did not kill Radahn but robbed him of his wits, turning him feral. Malenia herself was left slumbering in a coma. She was rescued by one of her Cleanrot Knights, Finlay , who carried her across the Lands Between . [ 12 ] When Malenia and Finlay took refuge at the Shaded Castle , Maleigh Marais , the sickly-born head of House Marais , was naturally drawn to the unconscious Demigod. [ 13 ] He saw in her his personal goddess. [ 14 ] Finlay carried Malenia back to the Haligtree, [ 12 ] far north of the Erdtree. [ 15 ]
The unleashed scarlet rot devastated Caelid, leaving it a rotting wasteland, and created the Swamp of Aeonia . Malenia inadvertently brought forth the Scarlet Butterflies and Kindred of Rot . The pests, including Sage Gowry , who worshipped her as a goddess and hoped to cause her to bloom once again, believing that she would usher in a new age of rot. [ 16 ] However, Malenia rejected her fate and never embraced the Servants of Rot . [ 17 ]
Miquella had encased himself within the Haligtree in an effort to create a new Erdtree of his very own, hopefully granting him the power to cure both his and his sister’s curses. [citation needed] However, during Malenia's absence, [verification needed] Miquella was ripped from the womb of the tree and taken away by Mohg, Lord of Blood before he could emerge from his cocoon . Malenia dreamt while awaiting Miquella's return, and the scarlet rot seeped out from her and began infecting the Haligtree.
Malenia dreamt for ages
Malenia's slumber is eventually disturbed by a Tarnished , who found their way to the roots of the Haligtree. The two fight, and Malenia finally meets her match, but she suffers her first true defeat. However, in the end, Malenia succumbs to the Scarlet Rot and blossoms yet again, reborn as a nascent goddess. She unleashes her full fury against the invader, but falls short yet again, her dying words an apology to her vanished brother. Having bloomed twice, Malenia withdraws within her scarlet blossom. [ 18 ]
Malenia is fought at the end of Elphael, Brace of the Haligtree , in a large chamber beyond the Haligtree Roots Site of Grace .
Her arena is an open cavern with a shallow pool of water at its center. There are no obstacles, so there is plenty of space to gain distance during some of Malenia's more devastating attacks.
In phase 1, Malenia will primarily make use of melee attacks using her sword. Her quick attacks, combined with her HP regeneration on hit, mean that she can rapidly recover from any damage dealt. However, she staggers easily, and her attacks can be cancelled by attacking during her wind-up animations. Frostbite and Blood Loss are especially good for staggering her.
Once Malenia's health reaches 0, a transformation cutscene will play, wherein she embraces the rot, releasing a swarm of butterflies and initiating phase 2. Malenia, Goddess of Rot starts the second phase with 80% of her maximum health, but can recover it with her HP regeneration.
The phase always begins with a scripted Scarlet Aeonia attack, which can immediately end the fight if the player does not immediately get some distance. She flies on wings made from her hair and butterflies, and many of her regular attacks can now inflict Scarlet Rot buildup. She gains a variety of rot-based attacks and can also create phantom projections of herself, which vanish after attacking. The most dangerous attack in her arsenal is her signature Waterfowl Dance .
I promise you. A thousand year voyage guided by compassion. - Miquella the Kind
Miquella the Kind , [ 3 ] also known as Miquella of the Haligtree , [ 8 ] Empyrean Miquella , [ 9 ] and the Unalloyed , is a Remembrance Boss in the Elden Ring add-on Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree . He is an Empyrean and a son of Queen Marika the Eternal and King Consort Radagon . He is the older twin brother of Malenia , and together they are known as the Twin Prodigies (天賦の双子, Tenpu no Futago ). His other self is St. Trina , whom he divested and cast into the depths of the Stone Coffin Fissure . He is encountered at the Gate of Divinity atop Enir-Ilim in the Realm of Shadow , where he fights alongside Radahn, Consort of Miquella .
Young Miquella seen in a memory flashback
Miquella and his twin sister were born with incurable afflictions, with Miquella's curse being perpetual youth. [ 10 ] Miquella made a promise to Malenia and experimented tirelessly in an attempt to undo their curses. The twins were very close, and Malenia became Miquella's sworn blade and protector. [ 11 ] Miquella was loved by many people and had a remarkable ability to compel affection from others. [ 9 ] For this reason, many regarded him as the most fearsome Empyrean. [ 12 ] [ 13 ]
Just as his parents were two halves of the same person, Miquella also had another half— St. Trina —who held the power of Sleep . [ 14 ] St. Trina was Miquella's fate, [ 15 ] and she was his "love". [ 16 ] [ 17 ]
Miquella was chosen by his Two Fingers to become an Empyrean, destined to succeed Queen Marika . [ 18 ] He was an adherent of Golden Order Fundamentalism , and developed new incantations as gifts to his father Radagon. [ 19 ] [ 20 ] However, Miquella abandoned Fundamentalism when it failed to treat Malenia's rot. He then began creating Unalloyed Gold , [ 21 ] which he used it to craft needles that could ward away the meddling of outer gods and forestall Malenia's incurable rot. [ 22 ] These needles could even be used to subdue the power of the Frenzied Flame . [ 23 ] He also unsuccessfully sought a solution for his half-brother Godwyn 's state of incomplete death. [ 24 ] [ 25 ]
Miquella's Great Rune once cast powerful charms
At some point, Miquella started watering a sapling with his own blood in the hope that it would become a new Erdtree . [ 26 ] The sapling was grown on top of the fortress of Elphael and became known as the Haligtree . Soldiers and Knights sworn to protect the Haligtree would use unalloyed gold to symbolize their loyalty and devotion to Miquella, wearing braided crowns made of the metal and creating shields embedded with it. [ 27 ] [ 28 ] [ 29 ] [ 30 ]
Miquella was also said to favor the low and meek, [ 27 ] and his Haligtree was intended to be the eventual salvation for the many. It became a hidden haven for the persecuted and the unwanted of the Lands Between , [ 31 ] such as the Misbegotten and Albinaurics . [ 32 ]
As Miquella pursued godhood, he knew that he would have to take a consort, to which his eyes fell upon his half-brother General Radahn , for he was strong but remained kind. He approached Radahn with his naive offer, to which the General vowed that he would become as such, [verification needed] in return for unspecified terms on Miquella and Malenia's behalf. [ 33 ] [ 34 ]
Malenia journeyed with her armies to Caelid to confront Radahn. The resulting Battle of Aeonia ended with Malenia unleashing her Scarlet Aeonia , whispering beforehand in Radahn's ear that "Miquella awaits thee, O promised consort." [ 35 ] After using her last resort attack, Malenia entered a comatose state, and one of her knights took it upon herself to carry her leader's slumbering body back across the Lands Between to the Haligtree. Radahn had survived, albeit barely standing, and his mind was riddled by the Scarlet Rot. He was now little more than a howling beast aimlessly wandering the battlefield, devouring the corpses of friends and foes alike. [ 36 ]
Following the Battle of Aeonia, [ 37 ] Miquella embedded himself into the Haligtree to progress his ascension, but was kidnapped during his slumber. [ 38 ] Another of Miquella's half-brothers was to blame: Mohg , who served an Outer God known as the Formless Mother . [ 39 ] He took the sleeping Empyrean deep underground to the Mohgwyn Palace , where he aspired to raise Miquella to full godhood himself through blood offerings, and then to take on the role of Miquella's consort instead of Radahn, becoming the new monarch of a Mohgwyn Dynasty. [ 40 ] Mohg urged his followers to render offerings of blood and drench Miquella's cocoon in order to facilitate his awakening. [ 41 ]
Despite all of Mohg's efforts, Miquella remained completely unresponsive. [ 40 ] At some point, Miquella had covertly placed an enchantment on Mohg, wishing to use the Omen to gain access to the Realm of Shadow . Sir Ansbach , a Pureblood Knight in service to Mohg, attempted to free his lord by challenging Miquella, only to succumb to an enchantment of his own. [ 42 ]
Without Miquella's blood offerings, and Malenia no longer protected by her Unalloyed Gold Needle once she was returned, the Haligtree became a misshapen husk. slowly succumbing to the unmitigated Scarlet Rot . [ 30 ] [ 43 ] Malenia and the Haligtree's soliders desperately awaited Miquella's return to save their rotting home. [ 44 ] [ 45 ]
Miquella and his promised consort, Radahn
My loyal blade. And champion of the festival. Both your deeds will ever be praised in song. Now, the vow will be honoured, and my Lord brother's soul will return. So that he may be my consort. - Miquella the Kind
Making use of Mohg, Miquella entered the Realm of Shadow , the location of the Gate of Divinity . As Miquella traveled through the Realm of Shadow, he abandoned parts of himself, including his flesh, his eye, his doubt and vacillation, his love, and his fears. Golden Miquella's Crosses resembling a Great Rune appeared at each location where he abandoned something, akin to Miquella's footprints. [ 46 ] Miquella's followers, who pursued him into the Realm of Shadow, used these crosses to trace his path through the realm. [ 47 ] Miquella also discarded his other half, St. Trina , [ 48 ] in the Stone Coffin Fissure . St. Trina, whose love for Miquella was boundless despite her abandonment, [ 1 ] recognized that godhood would be a prison for the Empyrean, [ 49 ] and desired for him to be killed out of mercy. [ 50 ]
Eventually, a Tarnished champion broke into Mohg's palace and slew the Lord of Blood for his great rune. Sir Gideon Ofnir suggested it might be safer to destroy the cocoon that Miquella remains asleep in. [ 51 ] Instead, the Tarnished met Needle Knight Leda , a loyal follower of Miquella, who urged them to travel to the Realm of Shadow by touching Miquella's withered arm within the cocoon. [ 52 ]
Within the Realm of Shadow, the Tarnished encounters several more of Miquella's followers , learns of his mission to ascend to godhood via the Gate of Divinity, [ 53 ] and of the powerful charm that he had placed upon his disciples, which is broken when he discards his Great Rune . [ 54 ] After gaining access to the tower of Enir-Ilim , the Tarnished is confronted by a resurrected Radahn, in a vessel made from the remains of Mohg. [ 55 ] It is unclear whether Miquella always intended to use Mohg's body to resurrect Radahn. However, he needed a vessel, likely a hornsent or omen one due to their strong connection to the spiritual world, to bind to Radahn's soul . [ 56 ] [ 55 ] During the ensuing battle, Miquella steps out of the Gate of Divinity and embraces Radahn as his consort. [ 57 ] The Tarnished triumphs over Radahn and Miquella, thus preventing Miquella's age of compassion. [ 58 ]
Welcome, honoured guest. To the birthplace of our dynasty! - Mohg, Lord of Blood
Mohg, Lord of Blood and Mohg, the Omen are Bosses in Elden Ring . Luminary Mohg is a Demigod and a Shardbearer who is encountered in the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds and at the Mohgwyn Palace .
Mohg, also known as the Lord of Blood, was born of the Golden Lineage —the offspring of Queen Marika and Godfrey, First Elden Lord —and was the twin brother of Morgott . [ 1 ] The twins were accursed Omen and, as a result, were confined and shackled to the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds below Leyndell . [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
Unlike his brother, Mohg embraced his Omen blood . Deep underground, Mohg made contact with an Outer God known as the Formless Mother , who ignited his accursed blood with bloodflame , granting him powerful magic. [ 4 ] [ 5 ]
Mohg escaped confinement in the wake of the Shattering , claiming a Great Rune of the Elden Ring . He began establishing his domain from Mohgwyn Palace and recruiting followers, including his Sanguine Nobles [ 6 ] and a murderous Tarnished known as the Bloody Fingers . Among these followers was Sir Ansbach , commander of the Pureblood Knights , and Varré , a war surgeon who was able to successfully tame Mohg's accursed blood. [ 7 ]
Miquella the Unalloyed later embedded himself within his Haligtree in an attempt to shed his affliction. In this vulnerable and unguarded state, Mohg seized the opportunity to abduct him from the tree. [ 8 ] Miquella was an Empyrean , thus having the potential of ascending to godhood ; Mohg intended to raise Miquella to full godhood so that he may rule at his side as consort and take the role of Elden Lord . [ 9 ] At some point during or after the abduction, Mohg was unknowingly enchanted by Miquella. The circumstances and timeline of this enchantment remain unclear.
After abducting Miquella, Mohg hibernated with him within the Cocoon of the Empyrean , and had his followers render offerings of blood, drenching its chamber in order to facilitate Miquella's awakening. [ 10 ] But no matter how much of Miquella's bloody bedchamber Mohg tried to share, he would receive no response from the young empyrean. [ 9 ]
During this time, Mohg largely escaped the notice of the Roundtable Hold , who were searching for clues as to his whereabouts. [ 11 ]
Eventually, the Tarnished came to learn the location of Mohg's palace, where he had hidden alongside the stolen Miquella. When the Tarnished stumbles upon his chambers, Mohg emerges from a pool of blood, holds Miquella's hand and apologizes for leaving him, ready to confront their "guests". Despite unleashing the full power of his accursed blood, Mohg is unable to overcome the Tarnished, falling at their hands.
Ahh, I can see it, as clear as day! The coming of our dynasty! Mohgwyn! - Mohg, Lord of Blood
Following his death, Mohg's corpse was stolen and transported to the Land of Shadow , where Miquella utilized it for an ancient ritual at the Gate of Divinity . Mohg's body became a vessel to house the revived soul of Radahn , Miquella's promised consort .
Mohg, the Omen is projection encountered in the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds , within the Cathedral of the Forsaken that lies beyond the Forsaken Depths Site of Grace. The arena is a fairly small chapel, with pillars on the side that can be used to gain distance. The Dung Eater is available as a summon for this fight, provided he has been released from his cell.
Mohg's trident attacks have long delays, and cover a wide range. He uses a number of bloodflame-based attacks, which deal blood loss as well as fire damage . Mohg's Shackle can be used to stun him for a few seconds, allowing for some additional hits.
Defeating Mohg, the Omen unlocks the Cathedral of the Forsaken Site of Grace and grants Bloodflame Talons and 100,000 runes. He must be defeated in order to access the Frenzied Flame Proscription .
Mohg, Lord of Blood is encountered at the top of the Mohgwyn Dynasty Mausoleum . The arena is reasonably wide and open, with some gravestones on each side that act as obstacles.
This fight plays out much like the Mohg, the Omen fight, until the second phase, when he performs a Bloodboon Ritual and subsequently sprouts enormous black wings. During phase 2, many of Mohg's moveset expands and his attacks will cover large areas in fire.
Mohg, Lord of Blood must be defeated to unlock the Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree expansion, and enter the Realm of Shadow .
Phase 1 is largely the same as the fight against Mohg, the Omen . The key difference is the introduction of a countdown. When his health drops to certain levels, he will thrust his spear into the air and chant, causing a red ring to appear around the player. He will do this three times, and once his health reaches 50% he will perform Bloodboon Ritual, dealing huge amounts of damage for each ring and inflicting blood loss , while simultaneously recovering his own health. The Purifying Crystal Tear can be added to the Flask of Wondrous Physick to significantly decrease the amount of damage dealt by this move.
After performing Bloodboon Ritual and recovering much of his health, Mohg will sprout wings and his spear will be imbued with bloodflame. The majority of his attacks will spray bloodflame on the ground, leaving patches of fire that last for a long time. He also now has abilities that utilize his wings to get out of range or to close distance easily.
Cower. Before Maliketh, Marika’s Black Blade. - Maliketh, the Black Blade
Maliketh, the Black Blade is a boss in Elden Ring , encountered in Crumbling Farum Azula . This is not an optional boss as Maliketh must be defeated to unlock Leyndell, Ashen Capital and reach the endgame of Elden Ring.
Maliketh is the loyal Shadowbound Beast and half-brother of Queen Marika the Eternal , [ 1 ] [ 2 ] an Empyrean of Numen descent, [ 3 ] who would become the vessel of the Elden Ring . [ 4 ]
Maliketh fought and defeated the Gloam-Eyed Queen , the leader of the Godskin Apostles . [ 5 ] On Marika's orders, Maliketh sealed away the Rune of Death , [ 1 ] binding it within his blade, [ 6 ] causing the true power of the god-slaying black flame to be lost. [ 7 ]
When the Rune of Death was plucked from the Elden Ring, [ 8 ] and confined, [ 9 ] the Golden Order was created, with Queen Marika as its one true god. [ 10 ] Marika's offspring were granted a form of immortality owing to the removal of their fated deaths from the Elden Ring, [ 11 ] however there was not one Demigod who did not fear Maliketh and his blade imbued with death. [ 2 ] He was a beast of such terrifying ferocity that his name came to mean "Death of the Demigods". [ 12 ] He also led the Black Blade Kindred , living gargoyles who wielded weapons held together by blackened corpse wax. [ 13 ]
During the Golden Age of the Erdtree , a fragment of the Rune of Death was stolen from Maliketh. [ 14 ] The perpetrator was Ranni the Witch , who used it to forge godslaying black knives, [ 15 ] which were wielded by the Black Knife Assassins during the assassination of Godwyn the Golden on the Night of Black Knives . [ 16 ] Maliketh responded by binding his blade- and the Rune of Death sealed within- into his own flesh, to prevent death from ever being stolen again. [ 6 ] Later, the Rune of Death sprouted from Godwyn's corpse and began to spread through the Lands Between in the form of Deathroot . Maliketh, under the name Gurranq , resolved to track down and devour the Deathroot, [ 17 ] eventually gaining an insatiable hunger for it. [ 18 ]
Maliketh, now Gurranq, eventually came into contact with D, Hunter of the Dead . D entered Gurranq's service and assisted him in weeding Deathroot, the source of Those Who Live in Death . [ 19 ] D would later find a Tarnished , who agreed to take his place in weeding Deathroot. [ 20 ]
The Tarnished encounters Gurranq in the Bestial Sanctum in Caelid . The beast, dressed in the robes of a clergyman, gives them an eye which trembles in the presence of Deathroot, [ 21 ] and instructs them to bring him any Deathroot they find in return for bestial incantations. [ 22 ] Despite consuming all the Deathroot the Tarnished could bring him, Gurranq is not sated. Despondent, he realises that he has done all he can for the land and departs, with his hunger as his only companion. [ 23 ]
When the Tarnished arrives at the foot of the Erdtree, they find the entrance obstructed by thorns. To remove the thorns, the Tarnished and their companion, Melina , set the Erdtree ablaze at the Giant's Forge. [ 24 ] After doing so, the Tarnished finds themselves in Crumbling Farum Azula , an ancient city in the sky, where they seek the Rune of Death. [ 25 ] The Tarnished finally comes upon Gurranq, who attempts to stop them from stealing the Rune of Death from him. [ 26 ] Despite his best efforts, Gurranq struggles to overcome the Tarnished. As a last resort, he unbinds his death-imbued blade from his flesh and reveals his true identity to the Tarnished. [ 27 ] Nevertheless, Maliketh falls to the Tarnished, and with his dying breath cries out to Marika for forgiveness. [ 28 ] The Rune of Death is unbound, and enshrouds the Lands Between. However, this allows the impenetrable thorns to finally burn away, [ 29 ] allowing the Tarnished to finally gain access to the Erdtree.
Phase 1 is much like combat against Gurranq. During this phase, the Beast Clergyman will make use of his Cinquedea as well as a variety of bestial incantations. His attacks are very fast, leaving few obvious spaces for the player to attack. He may use an earthquake attack, causing area of effect damage in a small circle around him.
At half health, a cutscene will play and phase 2 will begin. Maliketh now wields his Black Blade, and all of his attacks will cause rapid health loss overtime as well as temporary reduction of maximum health. Maliketh is a fast and acrobatic fighter, relying on quick slashes, spins and leaps. He will sometimes jump up and cling to the pillars around the arena, before either jumping at the player or jumping away and firing a ranged attack.
During this phase, the Blasphemous Claw can be used to deflect Maliketh's Black Blade attack, as well as the spin attack he performs after plunging his sword into the ground. Deflecting his attacks will stun him for a few seconds, creating a window during which to attack.
The arena is a wide, circular room. It is possible to fall off the edges all around the perimeter of the room. There are several pillars around the centre of the room, which Maliketh may jump onto to perform certain attacks. These pillars can also be used to create distance between oneself and Maliketh, or to avoid his ranged attacks.
The Dragonlord whose seat lies at the heart of the storm beyond time is said to have been Elden Lord in the age before the Erdtree. Once his god was fled, the lord continued to await its return. - Remembrance of the Dragonlord
Dragonlord Placidusax is a Remembrance Boss in Elden Ring , encountered in Crumbling Farum Azula .
Dragonlord Placidusax is a quadrupedal dragon with two wizened heads and a grievously wounded gravel stone body. [ 1 ] The scales protecting his head and back are drained of color, [ 2 ] while those on his underbelly are vibrant gold . [ 3 ] Each of his craggy, horn -strewn faces has yellow eyes , paired crown horns, and a large horn on the snout. They both have long strands of white hair that continue down the full length of their necks. In his prime, Dragonlord Placidusax had five heads, each emerging from the vortex-like swirl at the base of his neck, though now only two remain. He also had two pairs of wings in the past, but has since lost the rear set. His exposed flesh is red and gold.
Placidusax summons Red Lightning and can assume the form of a storming thundercloud. [ 4 ] He can fire beams of golden flame from his both mouths. [ 5 ]
Placidusax had four heads after his god fled
In the prehistoric era, eons before the age of the Erdtree , the Lands Between were ruled from Farum Azula by Dragonlord Placidusax, the Elden Lord and many-headed king of the beastmen and undying Ancient Dragons . [ 6 ] [ 7 ] However, after he lost a head and his god fled, but likely before the meteorite struck his flying royal city, Placidusax retreated to the storm beyond time to dream in eternal anticipation of his god's return. [ 8 ] [ 9 ] He required his followers to render up their sleep and remain ever-awake, so that he might find solace in slumber. [ 10 ] [ 11 ] The timeless ancient dragons, to whom the passing of many lifetimes had rendered notions of ambition, hunger, and fierceness of spirit as utterly unfathomable, received his blessings and grace in return. [ 12 ] [ 13 ]
In time, the drake dragons —paltry, mortal offspring of the ancient dragons—rebelled, [ 14 ] and Placidusax was betrayed by one of his own: Bayle the Dread . The old dragons formed a living wall of rock to protect their Dragonlord, but not before Bayle inflicted mutual, dire wounds upon the Dragonlord, claiming two of his heads and fleeing to the Jagged Peak . In retaliation, the Dragonlord marked Bayle and his bloodline for death. [ 15 ] He reportedly slew the colossal drake and devoured its Dragon Heart , consummating the first Dragon Communion . He sent his followers to introduce Dragon Communion to mankind, within whom he recognized the mad hunger and fiery drive necessary to destroy Bayle. [ 13 ] [ 16 ]
Farum Azula became a mausoleum enshrining Placidusax, guarded by his chosen beasts. Despite his severely weakened condition, Placidusax continued to grant blessings to his followers. [ 12 ] Several of Placidusax's Gravel Stone scales were disseminated throughout the world. They were used as smithing stones , said to allow for the creation of god-slaying weapons by lightly twisting time. [ 3 ]
Dragonlord Placidusax can be found in the storm beyond time at Crumbling Farum Azula . The nearest site of grace is Beside the Great Bridge , from which it can be reached by traveling north and down the slope. The player needs to jump down from a broken section of the bridge to reach his mausoleum complex. Once inside, activate the empty beastman to lie down. The storm rewinds time, and the Dragonlord appears.
The arena is a large, circular platform with pillars around its perimeter. These can be destroyed by Placidusax's attacks. The size of the arena gives ample room to avoid his area of effect or dodge his divebomb attacks.
Defeating Dragonlord Placidusax unlocks the Dragonlord Placidusax site of grace, which appears inside the arena.
Placidusax will begin the fight by summoning a storm of red lightning bolts which rain down on the arena for a few seconds. During his first phase, he will primarily use lightning claw attacks if the player is in front, a slam attack with his wings if they are to either side, and a tail sweep if they get behind him. He also has fire breath attacks which cover a large area in front of or around him. He has an area of effect attack which involves summoning a large lightning bolt and thrusting it into the ground, creating a massive explosion after a short delay. When he performs this attack, the music will briefly get quieter and red waves will emanate from where the lightning bolt hits, providing an indicator for the range of the explosion.
Placidusax now gains the ability to disappear in a cloud of fog. If he floats into the air before doing so, he will reappear in a stationary or moving thundercloud above the arena, before emerging and diving down at the player. He also gains the ability to disappear and reappear in quick succession, unleashing attacks with his lightning claws in between.
Lichdragon Fortissax is a boss in Elden Ring .
Fortissax is an Ancient Dragon who was once known as the "mightiest boulderstone", known for its use of twin red lightning stakes [ 1 ] , and the sibling of Ancient Dragon Lansseax . [ 2 ]
During the Age of the Erdtree , the Ancient Dragons warred against the forces of Leyndell , after an assault on the royal capital by the great Ancient Dragon Gransax . [ 3 ] Fortissax was challenged by Godwyn the Golden , who fought to the last [ 4 ] . Godwyn defeated Fortissax, but he befriended his fallen foe, and their bond gave rise to the Ancient Dragon Cult of the Royal Capital. [ 5 ] Through this friendship, Godwyn gained the ability to wield golden lightning, while the dragons gained acceptance as part of the Golden Order . [ 6 ]
On the Night of Black Knives , Godwyn was slain by assassins. [ 7 ] Godwyn would die in soul alone, with his body condemned to undeath, as it mutated beyond recognition. [ 8 ] Fortissax fought long and hard against the death within its companion, becoming corrupted by death in the process. [ 9 ] The Lichdragon is encountered within the Deathbed Dream after securing the Cursemark of Death and giving it to Fia , another companion of Godwyn's. Following Fortissax's defeat, Fia gestates the Mending Rune of the Death-Prince , which may usher in an age of death restored. [ 10 ]
As well as being able to breathe fire like other Ancient Dragons, Fortissax possesses the ability to summon a storm of gold and black lightning bolts which cover a wide area and inflict Death Blight . It can also summon a bolt of red lightning, which it slams into the ground, releasing waves of red lightning in multiple directions. After its health has been reduced to 60%, it gains the ability to summon two lightning spears at once, as well as a divebomb ability which is followed by a spinning attack using a lightning glaive.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
A malformed star born in the lightless void far away. Once destroyed an Eternal City and took away their sky. A falling star of ill omen. - Remembrance of the Naturalborn
Astel, Naturalborn of the Void is an optional Boss in Elden Ring .
Far beyond the Lands Between , within the Greater Will 's lightless abyss , the many-colored debris of ancient stars coalesced into a malformed creature. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ] A falling star of ill omen, Astel arrived long ago. [ 4 ] It assailed the Eternal Cities with a barrage of meteors, [ 5 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ] sealing them deep underground, away from the true night sky. [ 8 ] It destroyed the Nameless Eternal City and Noklateo, the Shrouded City . [ 9 ] [ 10 ] [ 11 ]
A procession of multi-colored orbs, Astel is an aberrant, cosmic entity that resembles a Great Dragonfly . [ 12 ] It has a humanoid skull with large mandibles and a large blue eye emerging from a crack in its forehead. It has four translucent insect wings and six skeletal arms that end in human-like hands, the forelimbs each possessing six fingers . Its long tail ends in a spiny scorpion stinger, wielded as a flail . It also casts gravity -based magic and can warp to other parts of the arena.
Astel, Naturalborn of the Void, is encountered within a secluded, starlit cavern somewhere along the underground Ainsel River , beyond the Lake of Rot . This area is accessed by entering the Transportation Coffin overlooking a chasm at the Grand Cloister . The elevator Astel blocks is the only path to the hidden Moonlight Altar , a necessary step for Ranni the Witch 's questline.
The Fire Giant is a survivor of the War against the Giants. Upon realizing the flames of their forge would never die, Queen Marika marked him with a curse. "O trifling giant, mayest thou tend thy flame for eternity." - Remembrance of the Fire Giant
The Fire Giant ( 火の巨人 , Hi no Kyojin ) is a boss in Elden Ring . He is encountered at Flame Peak on the Mountaintops of the Giants . This encounter is not optional as it must be completed to unlock Crumbling Farum Azula and advance the main storyline.
The Fire Giant is a gargantuan, red-haired humanoid with a slumbering, bearded face on its front torso. Its flame-red hair is worn in many braids, each with at least one beard bead. They worshipped the Fell God of Flame , and could borrow from it to achieve near- godlike power. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] The Fire Giants viewed smithing as a divine rite, and even their descendants, the Trolls , wielded hammers patterned after the fell god's eye . [ 3 ] The association between smithing and divinity reaches back to the Ancient Ruins of Rauh , whose anvils were shaped like altars and used in sacred forges . [ 4 ] -->
Long before the Erdtree , the Giants claimed the inhospitable northern mountains after driving away the Ice Dragons that once ruled them. [ 5 ] They worshipped their Fell God and tended its Flame within the Great Forge . Their astrologer neighbors dwelled among the high peaks, while the Zamor Knights were their eternal enemies. [ 6 ] [ 7 ]
When Queen Marika the Eternal ushered in the Age of the Erdtree , she ordered her consort Godfrey , the first Elden Lord , to wage the War Against the Giants , [ 8 ] fearing that their flame could burn her Erdtree . [ 9 ] [ 10 ] [ 11 ] Despite their might, the Giants were said to have been slain by Godfrey and his Crucible Knights , [ 12 ] [ 13 ] while Marika herself was rumored to have struck down the fell god. [ 14 ] They were punished by the Briars of Sin , yet their inextinguishable Flame endured. Marika sealed it away, [ 15 ] reducing its once-roaring blaze to embers and cursing the last Fire Giant to tend it for eternity. [ 16 ]
After untold ages, the last Fire Giant's labor was interrupted by a Tarnished seeking to harness the flame to burn the Erdtree. In battle, the Giant's leg brace was shattered, and in agony he tore off his own foot to sacrifice it to the fell god. Even empowered by divine flame, he was finally struck down—his death releasing him from the eternal curse. [ 17 ]
Alexander, Warrior Jar is available as a summon for this fight, provided he has been met at Mt. Gelmir . His summon sign is just inside the western boss gate. Torrent can also be used during this fight.
The arena is a large snowfield with craggy, uneven terrain. The field slops upwards from the entrance, and the Giant begins the fight at the top of the slope. Torrent can be called during this fight, and is useful for covering distance and avoiding the avalanche by jumping.
Fire Giant Phase 1
During phase 1, the Fire Giant will fight using a large, circular dish. Although he is fairly slow-moving, he is able to cover distance using his roll. He also possesses the ability to launch an avalanche straight towards the player. Initially, the majority of his attacks involve slamming the dish into the ground.
The objective initially is to attack the red braids wrapped around his left leg. After enough damage has been dealt, the braids will fall off, uncovering his injured ankle. At this point he will roll three times in succession, and then reach into the mouth on his abdomen, coating his hand in flames. He now gains the ability to use two fire-based abilities- a fast-moving fireball, and a large, slow-moving fire orb that homes in on the player.
Fire Giant Phase 2
Once his health drops below 47%, a cutscene plays and phase 2 begins. The Fire Giant has now lost the large dish as well as his left leg, and is forced to kneel on the ground. He is less mobile during this phase, however he can still roll. He now has a greater variety of fire spells. He may summon pillars of fire that erupt from the ground around him, breathe fire, or spew molten rocks that rain down on the arena. His weak spot is now on his left forearm.
It is said that long ago, the Greater Will sent a golden star bearing a beast into the Lands Between, which would later become the Elden Ring. - Elden Stars
The Elden Beast is the final Boss of Elden Ring , encountered on the Stone Platform inside the Erdtree at Leyndell, Ashen Capital , fought directly after Radagon of the Golden Order .
A long-necked, aquatic creature, the Elden Beast is a living constellation of shimmering Amber Starlight suspended in a translucent silhouette. Its narrow head lacks a traditional face, instead containing a single ball of glowing white light. It has a golden spine, an elongated body, and, along its back, long, tapering fins flare outward like fingers of radiant gold. Behind the torso trails a long, tapering tail that ends in a rich golden rootstock. The Elden Beast has two arms and two legs, with five-fingered hands. A glowing crack like shattered glass graces its chest.
Sent upon a golden star by the Greater Will , the arrival of the Elden Beast was one of the earliest events known to have occurred in the Lands Between . It was the vassal beast of the Greater Will and the living incarnation of the concept of Order . [ 1 ] At some later point in the primordial past, the Elden Beast was forged into the great Elden Ring . [ 2 ] The Empyrean consort of Dragonlord Placidusax became its vessel, becoming a god and making the ancient dragon the first known Elden Lord . [ 3 ] [ 4 ]
After untold ages , the Numen Marika , an Empyrean, became the new goddess and the vessel of the Elden Ring. [ 5 ] Her Golden Order established her as the one true god to rule over the Lands Between. [ 6 ] However, Marika eventually shattered the Elden Ring , leading to her imprisonment at the Stone Platform within the Erdtree . [ 7 ]
The Tarnished enters the Erdtree where they find the shackled Marika, and face Radagon , Marika's male other self [ 8 ] and the reigning Elden Lord, the two of them sharing the same body. After his defeat, the Elden Beast emerges from Radagon, transforming his defeated body into a large sword . [ 9 ] The Elden Beast reverts to the Elden Ring upon defeat.
The Elden Beast appears immediately after Radagon of the Golden Order is defeated. If you die to the Elden Beast, you are required to fight Radagon again before rechallenging it.
Elden Beast is the second half of the final boss fight with Radagon of the Golden Order . The Elden Beast uses a combination of physical sword attacks and golden Holy attacks.
The arena is a large, flat body of shallow water. Although it appears endless, the arena does have invisible walls surrounding it. The Elden Beast will regularly swim away from the player, or disappear underwater before emerging, meaning that the fight often requires one to chase or wait for it. Unlike the previous fight, it is possible to summon Torrent .
When its health reaches around 80% it will fly up into the air and create a golden ring which closes in on the player before exploding. This can be avoided by jumping over the ring as it closes in. It will also begin to use additional attacks, such as Elden Stars or Spear Showers. At around 30% health, it will perform the Golden Ring attack again, but this time it will generate three rings that each close in on the player.
Its normal sword attacks are fairly easy to dodge, with perhaps the repeating stabs being an exception. The Golden Rings can be jumped over to preserve your momentum and get out of them quicker, while the Spear Showers can be avoid by running while zig-zagging.
Elden Stars, if it cannot be interrupted by a stagger, is quite dangerous due to the consistent damage over time it can inflict and because it will gain speed to chase if allowed to travel with minimal turning. A way to fairly easily dodge it is to circle the Elden Beast counter-clockwise (that is, heading around it to your right before circling left to run out the duration.
Those stripped of the Grace of Gold shall all meet death. In the embrace of Messmer's flame. - Messmer the Impaler
Messmer the Impaler (串刺し公、メスメル, Kushizashi Kō, Mesumeru ), later known as Base Serpent Messmer (邪な蛇、メスメル, Yokoshimana Hebi, Mesumeru ), is a mandatory remembrance boss in Shadow of the Erdtree .
Messmer is a Demigod who is encountered in the Shadow Keep . He is the source of Messmerfire and the Messmer's Flame incantations .
Messmer is not an optional boss as he must be defeated in order to acquire Messmer's Kindling that would allow the burning of the Sealing Tree at the Church of the Bud .
Messmer was born to Queen Marika the Eternal prior to the Second Liurnian War . [ 5 ] His birth was cursed by a dark entity, an evil serpent coiled within that threatened to subsume him. [ 7 ] Known to Messmer as the Abyssal Serpent , [ 8 ] this force was restrained only through Marika's intervention—she removed her son's right eye and replaced it with a seal of her Grace . [ 2 ] Ever since his accursed birth, Messmer was in constant company of the winged serpents , friends who suppressed the base serpent. [ 4 ]
Much like his younger sister , Messmer bore a vision of fire . [ 7 ] and he despised the flame inside himself, and time and time again hoped to rid himself of it, but found that it ever burned. [ 9 ]
At some point, Messmer befriended Commander Gaius , an Albinauric who, like him, was cursed from birth and akin to an older brother to General Radahn , Gaius' fellow student in the art of gravitational sorcery. [ 5 ] Gaius would go on to command Messmer's armies during the crusade.
Messmer conquered the hornsent
Toward the end of the Age of Plenty , [ 10 ] [ 11 ] Messmer was charged by his mother with carrying out a purge of the tower -dwelling hornsent of the Land of Shadow , who did not bear the light of grace. [ 12 ] At some point during his Crusade , Messmer was abandoned in the Land of Shadow , but continued to zealously enforce the purge even though Marika used him as a scapegoat and ceased all contact with him. [ 1 ] Messmer came to reside in a fort known as the Shadow Keep .
Key in his army were the Black Knights , commanded by Black Knight Commander Andreas and his son and second-in-command Black Knight Captain Huw . Although they remained devoutly loyal to Messmer despite his abandonment by Marika, they ultimately rebelled upon learning of his serpentine nature. The pair were imprisoned in an underground tomb , and despite his betrayal, Messmer mourned the loss of Huw, whom he had considered a brother-in-arms. [ 13 ] [ 14 ] His Fire Knights would also refuse to follow the orders of burning the Ancient Ruins of Rauh and the destruction of the specimens in the Specimen Storehouse . [ 15 ] [ 16 ]
Eventually, an intruder invaded Messmer's stronghold, the Shadow Keep, and was noticed by the demigod's serpents, who identified them as a Tarnished Champion and a pretender to the title of Elden Lord . Though surprised that a Tarnished had come to the Land of Shadow, Messmer nonetheless attacked them to continue enforcing the purge. However, the serpentine demigod struggled overcome the Tarnished. Unwilling to accept "a Lord devoid of light" and desperate to regain the upper hand, Messmer ripped out Marika's seal and unleashed the power of the Abyssal Serpent, allowing him to frequently transform into a massive serpent. Nonetheless, the Tarnished was able to land a fatal blow upon Messmer. Realizing that his mother had indeed forsaken him, Messmer used his dying breath to curse Marika.
Hornsent can be summoned for this boss. His summon sign is found inside of the boss room, and will appear if the player decides to side with him against Leda or ignore this part of Leda's quest.
When he's finished with the first 3, he can follow up with the first and third move, especially if you're close to him when he finishes the first string of attacks.
Another version is you can see him in the center of the pool of red liquid while three Serpent heads are visible. The Serpent heads will strike successively and after the third strike, Messmer will follow up with a Flaming Spear Lunge attack, where he flies up, pauses mid-air, and slams his spear onto the ground to create an explosive area around him.
The attacks of Messmer the Impaler are imbued with fire damage, making him a formidable opponent who relies heavily on his spear's reach and agility. To proceed in this boss fight, readiness for his swift movements is important. When fighting Messmer at a close range, you will have more chances of retaliating and chipping away at his health while he recovers. Engaging Messmer patiently is the best strategy to effectively take him down. When he finishes a string of attacks, focus on breaking his poise by pulling off heavy attacks for a chance to deal significant damage.
Because of his speed, Messmer can quickly transition between offense and defense by quickly disengaging with a leap after he finishes a move. Be aware that Messmer counters swiftly after sustaining damage, too. As his speed and precision in combat are his biggest asset, observation is required to avoid being overwhelmed. Once Messmer's health is half-depleted, a cutscene will trigger, which will start Messmer's second phase.
During the second phase, Base Serpent Messmer remains at 50% HP and not only retains his original attacks, but also introduces a set of new and more lethal attacks with the help of the Abyssal Serpent . Among the fresh additions to his move set is the ability to transform into a large red serpent that rises up to the ground to throw a fireball or do bite attacks.
St. Trina is an enigmatic figure. Some say she is a comely young girl, others are sure he is a boy. The only certainty is that their appearance was as sudden as their disappearance. - Sword of St. Trina
St. Trina , also known as the saint of sleep , [ 1 ] is an NPC character in Elden Ring : Shadow of the Erdtree .
A pale young girl, delicately swaddled within the nurturing petals of a motherly deep-purple flower, rests her cherubic head on folded arms as she slumbers within her tranquil garden. Purple blood seeps from an unhealed wound on the left side of St. Trina's head, and her plant-like lower body twists into a dark stalk that roots her to the earth. A silvery-white streak graces her flowing purple hair, and the sweet, poisonous nectar she secretes grants eternal rest to those who partake of it. [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
Her earlier form was that of an alluring young woman with two long braids, [ 4 ] yet her destined adult form was considered unsettling. Crowned by a flower with eight petals, this cyclopean deity was expected to a awaken a third eye and eight wild braids of hair that coiled into eddy-like spirals . [ 5 ]
St. Trina is found in a small cave within the Garden of Deep Purple at the bottom of the Stone Coffin Fissure .
An enigmatic and fleeting individual who held dominion over sleep , some say she is a comely young girl, others are sure he is a boy. The only certainty is that their appearance was as sudden as their disappearance. [ 5 ] [ 6 ] She was the other half of Miquella , the aspect of his love thanks to his Empyrean nature. [ 7 ] The Empyrean and aspect inhabit the same body, much like Queen Marika and Lord Radagon . [ 8 ] [ 9 ] [ 10 ] As Miquella they appeared a small, golden-haired boy; as Trina, a prepossessing young woman with silver , light-purple hair. [ 6 ] [ 11 ]
St. Trina's love was boundless, [ 12 ] [ 13 ] offering gentle, intoxicating rest to those she visited in dreams. Some inhabitants of the Lands Between were so enamored that they formed a cult. Light-purple water lilies on the verge of wilting numbed the senses and prevented agitation, symbolizing faith in Trina. [ 14 ] Seeking to find her again in their sleep, [ 15 ] Trina's followers developed poisonous concoctions to elicit deeper slumber, [ 16 ] [ 17 ] and some priests were rumored to use sleep-inducing arrows for ritual purposes. [ 18 ] Dolores the Sleeping Arrow and Thiollier were among her greatest devotees. [ 2 ]
In the final act of the Shattering , Miquella and Malenia mustered an army of Cleanrot Knights and departed the Haligtree for Caelid to confront General Radahn regarding the vow. [ 19 ] The ensuing Battle of Aeonia culminated in a duel between Radahn and Malenia, who snapped Miquella's Needle to break the stalemate, unleashing her first scarlet rot bloom. [ 20 ] Although she gained wings of strength, fierce Malenia, Blade of Miquella, soon fell into a deep slumber. [ 21 ] [ 22 ]
During Miquella's pilgrimage through the Realm of Shadow , he stopped at the Cerulean Coast and traveled downward into the Stone Coffin Fissure . [ 23 ] Deep underground, the Empyrean stood atop the largest stone coffin and divested himself of his love and adoring other self, [ 13 ] casting Trina into the chasm's darkest depths. [ 24 ] [ 9 ] [ 25 ] Liberated from his fate and eternal childhood, [ 24 ] [ 26 ] he sealed the Fissure and resumed his injurious path to godhood. [ 27 ]
St. Trina survived her fall; [ 28 ] wounded, flowers burgeoned where her nectar-like blood pooled. [ 29 ] Her faint, light-purple slumber mists concentrated into an intoxicating deep-purple fog. [ 30 ] [ 31 ] Trina blossomed, manifesting deep-purple water lilies and forming her Garden of Deep Purple . [ 32 ] The congealed, arcane putrescence of ancient heroes imbibed her poisonous nectar, [ 33 ] received velvety eternal rest , and became her gallant Putrescent Knight . [ 34 ] [ 35 ]
Trina's love for Miquella never wavered, even after her abandonment. [ 12 ] Unable to speak directly, [ 36 ] her singular wish was to grant Miquella forgiveness in death, [ 37 ] knowing that godhood would become his prison. [ 38 ] [ 39 ] If her wish is granted, [ 40 ] Trina withers and dies, leaving behind a single harmless water lily. [ 41 ]
The cult of St. Trina had a presence at Summonwater Village , [ 42 ] Forsaken Ruins , [ 43 ] and Academy Gate Town . [ 44 ] Trina's Lilies grow in abundance at these locations.
St. Trina and Thiollier 's quests progress together.
I was born a champion's cub. Now I am the Lord of the Battlefield's lion. - Radahn's Redmane Helm
Starscourge Radahn ( 星砕きのラダーン , Hoshikudaki no Radān ) , also known as General Radahn , the Red Lion General , and later as Promised Consort Radahn and Radahn, Consort of Miquella , is an optional Demigod boss in Elden Ring and a mandatory God boss in Elden Ring : ; Shadow of the Erdtree .
General Radahn was feared as the strongest Demigod during the Shattering . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ] [ 4 ] This Shardbearer must be defeated to access the Realm of Shadow and achieve the " Age of the Stars " ending.
Red-maned Radahn was the son of Radagon , a champion of the Erdtree , and Queen Rennala of the Full Moon , head of both the Carian royal family and Academy of Raya Lucaria , born after the Second Liurnian War . He had two siblings, Rykard and Ranni . Radahn inherited his father's flaming red hair and was fond of its heroic implications. [ 5 ] From a young age, he was enamored with the Elden Lord Godfrey . Attempting to emulate his idol, Radahn adorned his armor with lions, the symbol of Godfrey and Serosh . [ 6 ]
At some point, the first Elden Lord , Godfrey, was robbed of grace and hounded from the Lands Between . Radahn's father, Radagon, left Rennala to become Queen Marika's new consort and the second Elden Lord. [ 7 ] Radahn and his siblings were thus raised to demigod status by their new step-mother, Marika. [ 8 ]
In their youth, Radahn's Empyrean half-brother Miquella deeply admired him for his kindness and strength, seeing in him the qualities of a lord . When he decided to pursue godhood , he made a vow with Radahn that, [ 9 ] upon his deific return, he would take Radahn as his consort. [ 10 ] In return, Miquella would uphold some unspecified part of the vow. [ 11 ]
Not wanting to abandon his scrawny but beloved steed, Leonard , [ 12 ] [ 13 ] Radahn studied gravitational magic in Sellia under a master who was an Alabaster Lord . [ 14 ] Radahn befriended the Albinauric Gaius , a senior disciple of his teacher, and the two formed a competitive yet friendly rivalry. Radahn's step-brother Messmer the Impaler was also friends with Gaius, and the two became as elder brothers to Radahn. [ 15 ]
Mastering gravitational magic allowed Radahn to manipulate the forces of gravity and challenge the stars themselves. [ 16 ] During the Starscourge Conflict , Radahn saved Sellia by conquering the stars and arrested their cycles, delaying fate . Having earned himself the moniker "Starscourge," he engraved the gravity crest upon his blades. [ 4 ] [ 17 ]
Radahn's soldiers were known as the Redmanes for the red-maned lion raising a sword in the image of Radahn on their surcoats. [ 18 ] The longest serving of the Redmane Knights was Ogha , who studied gravitational techniques alongside Radahn in Sellia. [ 19 ] It was popularly said that the Redmanes knew no weakness. [ 20 ] At an unknown period in time, Jerren , a guest of the Carian royals, became a guest commander for Radahn's armies, and they swore a mutual oath of honorable death. [ 21 ] [ 22 ] During his youth, Radahn witnessed the valor of a gladiator called Freyja , who he asked to become another member of his knights; an offer Freyja accepted. [ 23 ]
Radahn duels Malenia at the Battle of Aeonia
At some point following the Night of Black Knives , Queen Marika shattered the Elden Ring , and her offspring acquired the Great Runes. The maddening taint of their newfound strength led to the Shattering , a war between Marika's demigod descendants, each seeking to become the new ruler of the Lands Between. [ 24 ]
From his stronghold of Redmane Castle in the Caelid Wilds , Radahn led his armies against the forces of the other demigods. Radahn tried to challenge Godrick the Grafted in Limgrave , but the latter hid in Stormveil Castle . [ 25 ]
By the end of the Shattering, only Radahn and his half-sister Malenia, Blade of Miquella were left standing. The two fought to a stalemate in the Battle of Aeonia , their duel ending inconclusively when Malenia unleashed her Scarlet Rot . [ 26 ] As the Scarlet Aeonia flower blossomed, Malenia whispered in Radahn's ear, "Miquella awaits thee, O promised consort." [ 27 ]
The Scarlet Rot ravaged Caelid and consumed Radahn from the inside, eating away at his psyche but failing to kill him. Following the Battle of Aeonia, Radahn roams the Wailing Dunes as a mindless beast who devours the flesh of friend and foe alike, howling at the sky. [ 28 ] Without their commander, the Redmane Knights burned the crest on the left breast of their armor to indicate their resolve not to return home, and to serve as a bulwark against the spread of the rot in Caelid using fire . [ 29 ] [ 30 ]
Despite his madness, Radahn continues to ride his scrawny steed, as well as halt the motions of the stars. The Radahn Festival has been organized by his men in Castle Redmane to celebrate his last battle. It is a gathering of mighty warriors who might finally put the General out of his misery and claim his Great Rune for themselves. The festival serves as Jerren 's way of fulfilling his oath of honorable death to Radahn. [ 31 ] [ 32 ]
Upon the participation of a Tarnished Champion , the Radahn Festival is a success, and Radahn is freed from his tortured existence. His death causes the stars to resume their cycles, some of which come crashing down upon the Lands Between. One such falling star lands in Limgrave, opening the path to Nokron, Eternal City , and allowing the fate of Ranni the Witch to progress. [ 33 ] [ 34 ]
Following Radahn's defeat, his soul met its end. However, Miquella sought to revive it, [ 35 ] still desiring for Radahn to be his lord consort. Miquella successfully revived Radahn, placing his soul into a vessel made from the remains of Mohg, Lord of Blood , another Demigod slain by the same Tarnished who had defeated Radahn. [ 36 ] The Tarnished encounters the newly-resurrected Radahn at the Gate of Divinity at the top of Enir-Ilim . Radahn stands guard as Miquella completes his ascension to godhood and battles the Tarnished once more. During the ensuing battle, Miquella steps out of the Gate of Divinity and embraces Radahn as his consort and fights the Tarnished with Radahn. [ 37 ] The Tarnished triumphs over Radahn and Miquella, thus preventing Miquella's age of compassion. [ 38 ]
Radahn's Great Rune
Torrent can be called during this fight and is useful for closing distance and evading Radahn's ranged attacks.
Multiple NPCs are available to be summoned during the fight, and their summons can be located throughout the arena. Six can be summoned at a time, and once a summon sign is used it will vanish, however each NPC has multiple summon signs that can be used.
The following eight champions are available:
The player will spawn some distance away from Radahn, with the boss visible at the top of a dune in the distance. Immediately, Radahn will begin firing volleys of arrows which rain down from above, homing in on the player, as well as gravity arrows. The latter can be avoided by hiding behind the clusters of weapons dug into the ground, however the weapons will break when struck. Riding Torrent will make it easier to avoid the volleys. Summon signs can be found in clusters all around the arena, and can be used to summon NPCs to assist in the fight.
Once the player is close enough, Radahn will begin attacking using his swords. He is very mobile, using his horse to cover distance easily. He also uses a number of gravity-based attacks, such as Cragblade, gravity waves, and Collapsing Stars.
Once his health is below 50%, Radahn will launch himself into the sky, disappearing for several seconds. He will then come crashing down in a ball of fire, dealing devastating damage to anyone caught in the impact. Radahn now gains the ability to raise four floating rocks, which will hover beside him and then launch at the player or their summons. He also gains the ability to float into the air and spin rapidly while charging.
The Wailing Dunes is a very large arena consisting of many tall dunes, with Radahn initially standing at the top of the largest dune close to the centre of the area. Clusters of weapons can be found stuck in the sand, and can be used to hide from Radahn's arrows. Summon signs can be found throughout the arena, often in clusters of two or three.
The second encounter with Radahn serves as the final boss of the Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree expansion. The first phase is Promised Consort Radahn and the second is Radahn, Consort of Miquella .
Just like in the base game, players will spawn a distance away from Radahn. While retaining his gravity magic, and as his soul now possessed Mohg's remains, Radahn now employs Bloodflame, and seamlessly switches between the two elemental magics while in combat. To defeat him, it is always important to time your attacks in between Radahn's string of attacks or pull off counters at the very end of a combo. Because of his recovery time, this makes his boss battle complicated, as he can launch other attacks almost instantly after finishing a heavy attack. As a result, it is important to note that patience and appropriate timing are the keys to defeating Radahn. The optimal moment to attack is when he finished his basic sword combos, and would take a brief pause to recover.
At the start of his boss battle, he will nearly always use a gravity attack to prevent players from summoning or buffs upon entry into the boss battle. Because of this, players are recommended to use buffs before accessing the boss and cast summons right after dodging the initial attack. During his first phase, Radahn will use a flurry of combos aside from special abilities such as a Bloodflame Slash and his Gravity attacks. After being reduced to 65% of his health, this will trigger a cutscene leading to Phase 2.
In this phase, Radahn's previous attacks are improved and he gains new powerful abilities. Most of them are Holy-powered and have a wider AoE. Overall, while his attacks become more lethal, Radahn is now faster in speed, now capable of creating mirror images to attack and using strong Holy-based abilities, making the boss battle more difficult and challenging. However, despite gaining immense power, Radahn's health has already been reduced to 75%, allowing players to gain a slight edge. It is important to capitalize on the pauses of Radahn's combo attacks, as there are opportunities to strike. Constantly taking advantage of them can deplete his health and because Radahn's attacks can be very punishing if caught off-guard, you have to be prepared to switch between offensive and defensive at times.
While Radahn can still perform similar combos from Phase 1, they have an additional Holy damage explosion at the end. As Miquella is now mounted on his back, he can do a grab attack where he will glow and jump at the player in order to grab them. If successful, Radahn will bring them close to Miquella, who will then place the player under a charm. While this doesn't deal any damage, if Radahn successfully grabs the player a second time while they are charmed, this will ultimately result in instant death. Using Miquella's Great Rune will undo the charm.
The arena consists of a very wide area, with a rough white surface filled with gray-white decomposed corpses, which can be found sticking from the ground. At the other end of the arena, stands the Gate of Divinity itself, where Miquella will step out in divine aspect in the second phase.
Curse you, Bayle! I hereby vow you will rue this day! Behold, a true drake warrior and I, Igon! Your fears made flesh! Solid of scale you might be, foul dragon, but I will riddle with holes your rotten hide! With a hail of harpoons! With every last drop of my being! Bayle the Dread…you shall haunt me no longer! - [[ Igon ]]
Bayle the Dread is an optional boss in Shadow of the Erdtree .
Bayle the Dread was a legendary black dragon who is said to be the ancestor of the drakes or lesser dragons. Long ago, Bayle betrayed the Ancient dragons and clashed with Dragonlord Placidusax . [ 1 ] Their vicious battle ended in stalemate and left both dragons with grievous injuries and loss of body parts, with Bayle losing his two winged arms, his pair of wings on his back and his left leg, with the dreaded dragon fleeing to the Jagged Peak soon afterwards. [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
As punishment for his betrayal, Placidusax created the art of Dragon Communion , sending his followers to shepherd humanity into hunting Bayle and his descendants. [ 4 ] As reward for felling the drakes, the dragon hunters consumed their hearts in order to gain their power. Bayle was pursued by Florissax , a servant of Placidusax who sought to recruit mortals in the hunt for Bayle. [ 5 ] [ 6 ]
Dragonslayer Igon , a particularly obsessive drake warrior, was one such mortal. Igon faced Bayle, but was left broken in both body and spirit by their battle. [ 7 ] [ 8 ]
The gravelstone heart of Bayle
Igon was stumbled upon by a Tarnished champion , and begged them to summon his spirit to face Bayle once more. Together, the pair succeed in slaying Bayle. [ 9 ] [ 10 ]
If Bayle's heart is eaten at the Grand Altar of Dragon Communion , his willpower will one day consume the body and soul of the drake warrior. [ 11 ]
Bayle is weakest against piercing damage, Dragon Communion Grease , and Igon's Harpoons .
Bayle is stuck on the ground. He commands a unique power that combines fire and lightning damage. He is a
Bayle summons an extra set of wings made from red lightning. He is able to fly.
After the church was burned to the ground, Romina discovered a twisted divine element, which she weaved into the baleful scarlet rot. Perhaps then, the buds might find somewhere to gain purchase once more, within the scorched remains. - Remembrance of the Saint of the Bud
Romina, Saint of the Bud is a mandatory Boss in Shadow of the Erdtree .
An attendant of the Church of the Bud in the Ancient Ruins of Rauh , Romina's way of life was destroyed when the crusade came to the Land of Shadow . As Messmer the Impaler 's forces razed her church to the ground, she clutched its ceremonial Bud in speechless silence. [ 1 ] In the ashes, she discovered a twisted divine element, reforming it into the dreaded Scarlet Rot . [ 2 ] The Bud became her poleblade and, over time, her body was corrupted, adopting aspects of flowers , centipedes , scorpions , ants , and butterflies . [ 3 ] After the Battle of Aeonia , Romina reached out to and soothed some of the Aeonia Butterflies disowned by Malenia . [ 4 ] They enabled her to perform a lost sacred rite of purification. [ 5 ] Likewise, the Kindred of Rot turned scarlet red after they were accepted into the motherly embrace of Romina, Saint of the Bud. [ 6 ]
Romina is not an optional boss as it must be defeated to burn the Sealing Tree and reach Enir-Ilim .
Romina is a distinctive opponent whose weaponry is her poleblade, centipede head, and scorpion stinger. It is essential to have a balanced strategy of both offense and defense, but it is advantageous to be more aggressive in battle.
Focus on her central human body as well as her centipede fangs and scorpion tail, which functionally serve as her arms. These parts move independently, allowing her to launch multiple simultaneous attacks, such as swinging her spear while her stinger strikes from another direction. Her attacks include Heavy Spear Thrusts, Sweeping Stinger strikes, and Biting Fangs.
Her most common opening move is her Centipede Sweep , where the centipede part of her body will swing from right to left. It can be dodged by rolling forward. This will let you get close to Romina to deliver a full heavy attack. However, you have to be aware that she may follow up by dashing and swinging her poleblade, which can be avoided by rolling to the left or backwards.
Stay as close as possible to Romina, as some of her sweep attacks won't hit you at point-blank range. Being near her also makes her attack pattern more predictable. For instance, after her usual opening attack, closing the distance with a dodge roll will cause her follow-up attack to miss if you are right beside her.
It is important to always look at Romina's poleblade, as when it glows red, this shows that it has become enchanted with Scarlet Rot. If hit with the enchanted weapon, it will cause a Scarlet Rot build-up. Always be wary of her weapon status. One of the combos that she does with her enchanted weapon is the Leap Combo where she starts with a poleblade sweep, an overhead attack, and then she jumps high in the air, and then plunges her weapon down. To dodge this, you can either:
When the leap combo is timed correctly, you can deliver a couple of free hits while she recovers. This combo also has a variation where Romina skips the 3rd part of the attack and does an enchanted weapon combo instead. She also has another basic move where she makes 3 quick sweeping movements with her poleblade without enchantments. Finally, she can also do the Rolling Attack where she will curl up into a ball, and then roll around the arena. After she finishes rolling, she will slam the ground and then swing her pole blade. This can be initially avoided by getting out of her way, either by dodging or sprinting away. Lock the camera onto her to see where she is going. At the end of the roll, roll to the right to dodge both of her attacks. Then, you can retaliate with a heavy attack.
After she finishes a combo, quickly counterattack to take advantage of the time when she will be briefly vulnerable. While powerful, her attacks have high recovery times, allowing you to dodge and immediately counter. When she begins a combo, dodge her attacks by rolling to the side or towards her to close the distance. Immediately after dodging, counter with heavy attacks to break her poise. Frequent usage of jumping and heavy attacks is recommended as it can stagger her, leaving her open to further attacks.
One of her special moves is the Double Spin 360 Combo , where she will lift up her human body as her weapon glows red, and will do two full spins while swinging her poleblade. After performing this move, she will pause to recover. This move can be dodged by rolling to the left, then dodging to the left again after a slight delay. This move usually causes Romina to end up at a far position from you, but she will take time to recover, and you can do at least one light attack or a jump attack if you sprint up to her.
After her health drops to 50%, she will immediately transition to her second phase; her attacks remain the same, but she can now conjure Rotten Butterflies that will explode like bombs after a short period. She will be seen with pink butterflies circling her, and after a brief period, she will cause a whirlwind in the small arena. Romina then follows up this move with more butterflies in the outer area of the whirlwind that will randomly explode throughout the arena. To dodge this move, start sprinting away as her body lights up with a pink hue. Then, if you can outrun the AoE, you can stand at the edge, and you will not get hit. If you get caught, you can spam roll until you get out of the AoE. As the fight goes on, Romina will likely redo this move again, but with shorter preparation. So you will need to react quicker to get out of the exploding butterflies.
Romina at first seems like you must wait and punish with a typical melee build. She has a glaring weakness: she is vulnerable to animations that shift the player's hurt box down, particularly to low-profile common moves like her double glowing spear lunge and swipe. A perfect example I found was using Dryleaf Arts, where the Heavy attack naturally has low profiles for many of her spear-swiping moves. During my run, I found it more beneficial to be aggressive rather than defensive. Staying on her inner right side up front will negate a lot of her attacks with a dodge as needed. I ran Frost to add the slow to her animations, which was a plus, but not required in fighting her. The low profiling and staying on the offensive to break stance to heal as needed or deal significant damage was enough.
Enough... I have endured... more than enough... I ask you forgive me, dearest Nanaya... Ahhhhhh... - Sage Midra
Midra, Lord of Frenzied Flame , also known as Sage Midra , is an optional boss in the Elden Ring add-on Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree .
Long ago, the great Sage Midra attempted to become a Lord of Frenzied Flame . However, he was too weak and failed. [ 1 ] Pierced by the branching thorns of the Greatsword of Damnation , his power was suppressed by the hornsent . [ 2 ] [ 3 ] [ 4 ] Midra's Manse and the dark lands of the Abyssal Woods were forbidden by the Hornsent. [ 5 ] It is said the eyes of those who served the sage were burned by the Frenzied Flame of madness . [ 6 ] [ 7 ] Midra lingered on in perpetual suffering at the behest of his beloved Nanaya . [ 8 ] [ 9 ]
Eventually, a Tarnished Champion entered Midra's manse to explore and loot it. Midra repeatedly tried to warn the Tarnished to leave, but his pleas went unheeded. Upon the Tarnished coming upon Midra's chambers, Midra chastised the Tarnished for their foolishness before attacking them, only to be brutally beaten and subdued. Finally, Midra could endure his pain no more. He pulls the sword out through his head and decapitates himself. Then, he manifests as the Lord of Frenzied Flame. The branching arms of the sword coil tightly around its central needle. [ 4 ]
A feeble man wearing a yellow or gold robe with a large clasp with green gems. A golden stake is driven through his eye that continues into his body. Its barbs emerge from his torso in the shape of an evergreen . He unseals the Frenzied Flame by removing the rod through his eye, decapitating himself to reveal a gazing fireball of Frenzied Flame. The barbs coil around the weapon to form his sword.
Crucible Knight is a non-respawnable enemy in Elden Ring .
The Crucible Knights served Godfrey, the First Elden Lord. [ 1 ] They were led by Crucible Knight Ordovis and Crucible Knight Siluria , two honored as the foremost amongst the Crucible Knights. [ 2 ] Their armor holds the power of the crucible of life. In time, their strength, even their appearance, was seen as chaotic and deserving of scorn. [ 3 ]

Crucible Knights led by Siluria. Their armor adorned with the great tree ornamentation that is her mark. Elemer of the Briar is a reoccurring boss in Elden Ring .
Elemer of the Briar, also known as the Bell Bearing Hunter , originally hailed from Eochaid , a land of proudly solitary ascetics. [ 1 ] He wears iron armor wrapped in iron thorns, which are a mark of the guilty and of those sentenced to death. [ 2 ] He was slated for execution at the Shaded Castle , home of the family of House Marais, however he evaded death by snatching the sword from the site of his looming execution and furnished it with battle skills from his homeland. [ 3 ] He gained the moniker "Bell Bearing Hunter" by killing numerous merchants and instructors [ 4 ] , and taking their Bell Bearings.
Elemer can be encountered in the Castellan's Hall of the Shaded Castle, the site of his failed execution. He can also appear in various locations throughout the Lands Between , typically in places where merchants can be found.
The Bell-Bearing Hunter will only appear when resting at night; to make him reappear after being defeated yourself, rest at the grace and set the time to night and then rest again.
