Briar Greatshield
Elemer is encountered in the hall at the top of the Shaded Castle. He can channel energy through his sword, allowing him to send it towards the player and control it at a distance, or fire a red beam by rotating it quickly.
The Bell Bearing Hunter appears at night, in the Hermit Merchant's Shack in the Capital Outskirts . The Hermit Merchant (Capital Outskirts) will disappear for the duration of the fight, but will reappear if the player dies or if they defeat the boss.
The Bell Bearing Hunter appears at night, outside the Isolated Merchant's Shack in Greyoll's Dragonbarrow . The Isolated Merchant (Dragonbarrow) will disappear for the duration of the fight, but will reappear if the player dies or if they defeat the boss.
Godskin Apostles are Bosses in Elden Ring and Elden Ring Nightreign .
Lanky humanoids clad in robes sewn together from patches of smooth skin. [ 1 ] The Godskin Apostles were led by the Gloam-Eyed Queen [ 2 ] , who cradled them as newborns in a swaddling cloth made from skin much like their robes [ 3 ] . They served Destined Death [ 1 ] , and wielded god-slaying black flame. However, when Maliketh, the Black Blade , sealed away the Rune of Death, the flame's true power was lost. [ 4 ]
A duo consisting of a Godskin Apostle and Godskin Noble , encountered in the Dragon Temple within Crumbling Farum Azula . They share a health bar and have their own individual health. If one is killed, the other will resurrect them shortly. If both are killed before the shared health bar reaches 0, the Noble will respawn and summon the Apostle shortly.
Nobles are the most ancient apostles who are said to have assimilated inhuman physiology. Not unlike the crucible, the Erdtree in its primordial form. - Godskin Noble Robe
Godskin Nobles are a reoccurring enemy and boss in Elden Ring .
The Godskin Nobles are stout humanoids who wear robes sewn together from patches of soft skin, featuring seven-faced aprons. They are the most ancient of the apostles who once served the Gloam-Eyed Queen , [ 1 ] incorporating inhuman physiology, not unlike the primordial crucible . [ 2 ] They wield elegant thrusting swords with skill unmatched by lowborns, [ 3 ] and wield black flame like the Godskin Apostles .
A duo consisting of a Godskin Apostle and Godskin Noble, encountered in the Dragon Temple within Crumbling Farum Azula . They share a health bar, as well as having their own individual health. If one is killed, the other will resurrect them after a short amount of time. If both are killed before the shared health bar reaches 0, the Noble will respawn and summon the Apostle after a short amount of time.
The Godskin Duo share one health bar of around 24000 HP (NG), but also still have their own HP. If one is killed, it will either respawn automatically after ~15 seconds or the other Godskin will reanimate them. They will also still enter phase 2 if dropping close to 50% in individual HP.
The pillars within the arena are an effective way to separate them, although their phase 2 attacks will demolish the upper portion of them. In addition, both of them can be parried.
Sleep Pots can serve as a way to buy time as both bosses can be rendered temporarily paralyzed by sleep status.
The living rampart of the Erdtree, the Tree Sentinels are the standard to which all defenders of the Erdtree aspire. - Erdtree Greatshield
Tree Sentinels ( ツリーガード , Tsurīgādo , lit. "Tree Guard") are Bosses in Elden Ring and Elden Ring Nightreign .
Possessed of great strength and abundant Grace , Queen Marika 's mounted Tree Sentinels met little resistance as they charged down her enemies. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] Heavily-equipped and blessed with old Erdtree incantations , [ 3 ] very few were permitted to join their nigh unbreakable ranks. [ 4 ] [ 5 ] They were resolute in their commitment toward protecting that which deserved protection, becoming the gold standard to which all defenders of the Erdtree measured themselves. [ 6 ] Their gallantry influenced the practices of the Leyndell Knights , who similarly put the shield before the sword. [ 7 ]
After the Ancient Dragon Gransax attacked Leyndell , some of the Tree Sentinels adopted characteristics of the Ancient Dragons . These knights became Draconic Tree Sentinels to better protect the Erdtree. [ 8 ]
A few Tree Sentinels embarked on Messmer 's crusade , later safeguarding the path to the Shaman Village , Queen Marika's former home. [ 9 ]
King Morgott distributed special, invisibility-revealing torches to the Tree Sentinels following his rise to power, hoping to prevent a second Night of Black Knives . [ 10 ]
An imposingly sturdy knight chained to the saddle of a large horse. The Tree Sentinel wears golden filigreed plate with intricate vine and floral motifs, inlaid with crimson and viridian jewels, and a dark ochre cape depicting a sacred tree . Their helm features red false eyeslits and a small, decorative tree with yellow-green growth in place of a plume. The knight carries a massive golden halberd imbued with Holy energy. Their steed is covered head-to-hoof in barding of golden plate over layered black armor. Its ornate chamfron (faceplate) has vented blinkers and a spiral unicorn horn embellishment.
A duo of Tree Sentinels found in the Hinterlands of Scaduview , guarding the path to the Minor Erdtree incantation.
The shield bearer starts out on to the left, on the path to riding across the nearby bridge, while the torch-wielder is riding down the path from Shaman Village . This means they are quite easy to fight separately.
As with the Altus duo both of these must be defeated to get their runes, but their respective Blessings are dropped the first time each is killed.
After the great ancient dragon Gransax attacked, the sentinels had an epiphany. The only way to truly protect the Erdtree was to become dragons themselves. - Malformed Dragon Armor
Draconic Tree Sentinel is a recurring field boss in Elden Ring .
Misshapen Tree Sentinels using a malformed golden armor adorned with various dragon imagery. They adopted draconic features to protect the Erdtree after Ancient Dragon Gransax attacked Leyndell, Royal Capital . [ 1 ]
The Night's Cavalry, who now wander the dim roads of night, were once led by the Fell Omen and were deliverers of death for great warriors, knights, and champions. - Night's Cavalry Greaves
The Night's Cavalry , also known as Nightriders , [ 1 ] are recurring bosses in Elden Ring and end-of-night bosses in Elden Ring Nightreign .
Night's Cavalrymen were once led by Margit, the Fell Omen , delivering death to great warriors, knights, and champions . [ 2 ] [ 3 ] Their fond remembrances inspired the Phantom Slash battle art, which manifests an apparition of their former teacher. [ 4 ] Presently, they can be found across the Lands Between , appearing only at night. [ 5 ]
The Night's Cavalry are knights in black armor with flowing black hair that only appear at night , riding atop funeral steeds . [ 6 ] They fight using flails , which can inflict blood loss , [ 7 ] or glaives , which allow them to perform wide, sweeping attacks. [ 1 ]
The Night's Cavalry and its Funeral Steed have separate health bars. Defeating the horse dismounts the rider. The knight summons a new horse from a purple portal after a while, or after the player runs away.
There are ten Night's Cavalry across nine locations :
Nightrider Flail
Nightrider Glaive
Black Blade Kindred is a reoccurring boss in Elden Ring .
The Black Blade Kindred are Valiant Gargoyles who serve Maliketh, the Black Blade . [ 1 ] These golems wield bronze weapons mended with blackened corpse wax , and are able to harness the power of the Rune of Death , with attacks that drain one's health .
Gargoyle's Black Halberd
A Black Blade Kindred who stands guard outside the Bestial Sanctum in Caelid . It wields a halberd and a greatsword.
It is possible to avoid this boss by using the sending gate north of the Third Church of Marika , which will teleport the player to the door to the Bestial Sanctum, behind the boss.
Gargoyle's Black Axe
A Black Blade Kindred who appears in the Forbidden Lands as the player approaches the Grand Lift of Rold on the way to the Mountaintops of the Giants . It wields a twinblade and an axe.
Millicent is available as a summon for this fight, provided she has been given the Valkyrie's Prosthesis and has been spoken to in Dominula, Windmill Village .
The dead gazed at the skies over the lakes of Limgrave, praying that the dragons' flames would burn them to ash. - Agheel's Flame
Flying Dragon Agheel is an optional boss in Elden Ring .
Flying Dragon Agheel is encountered in Agheel Lake in southern Limgrave , northwest of the Dragon-Burnt Ruins . Wandering Nobles in the ruins around the lake chant Agheel's name, praying that it will burn them to ash. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] The drake appears by flying down from above, torching a congregation of Wandering Nobles with dragonfire.
Flying Dragon Agheel the standard Dragon movepool.
Smarag was a devourer of sorcerers, and over time, his body became corrupted by their glintstones. - Smarag's Glintstone Breath
Glintstone Dragon Smarag is an optional boss in Elden Ring .
A devourer of sorcerers , whose body gradually became corrupted by the glintstones of those he ate. [ 1 ] Smarag is encountered near an island west of the Academy of Raya Lucaria and north of the Temple Quarter , guarding a Glintstone Sorcerer corpse that holds the first Academy Glintstone Key .
Glintstone Dragon Smarag uses the Glintstone Dragon movepool.
Glintstone Dragon Smarag is encountered in Liurnia of the Lakes , near Crystalline Woods and Temple Quarter .

Ulcerated Tree Spirits ( 爛れた樹霊 , Tadareta Jurei , lit. "Rotten Tree Spirit") and Putrid Tree Spirits are Enemies and Bosses in Elden Ring . Most information about this enemy is conjectural, based on its visual details and contextual clues. This enemy functions like an unmarked boss and does not respawn once defeated. There are three bosses and eight non-boss Ulcerated Tree Spirits to find.
Ulcerated Tree Spirits are giant, serpentine entities with white, bark-like skin that resembles branches or roots, covered in large red pustules. They slam their claws and tails in combat and can generate searing golden fire . Commonly found near the Erdtree and its roots, they usually drop Golden Seeds .

Erdtree Avatar is a non-respawnable enemy and field boss in Elden Ring .
Beings with bodies resembling hollow tree stumps. The avatars emerged in the wake of the shattering of the Elden Ring in order to protect the Minor Erdtrees . [ 1 ] They wield large staffs depicting the Erdtree , and are capable of utilising offensive incantations.

The ancestral followers keep their distance from the Erdtree, awaiting new buds. - Great Horned Headband
The Ancestral Follower Warriors are enemies in Elden Ring .
Having abandoned steel, the weapons they wield consist of repurposed animal parts.
The horned folk rejected writing and metalworking in all its forms, living in primitive hunter-gatherer communities among dynastic ruins and ancient bowers . They worshipped the spirits of herbivorous beasts , a deeply-rooted faith that operated beyond the purview of Marika 's Golden Order . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] They distanced themselves from the Erdtree , waiting for new buds to sprout in the Lands Between . [ 3 ]
The most common are those that wield the Jawbone Axe and are capable of performing swift attacks with both the weapon and their free hand.
The most dangerous and notable of these warriors are the hunters that wield the Horn Bow , capable of firing Dwelling Arrows with near-perfect precision, even over great distances. If the player is spotted, they will relentlessly fire arrows, but if they are approached, they will switch to an axe for melee combat.
A spectral variant of the Ancestral Followers. Like similar phantom variants, they can briefly appear and disappear.
Magma Wyrm is a reoccurring boss and non-respawning enemy in Elden Ring and Elden Ring Nightreign .
Magma Wyrms are quadrupedal draconic beings with torn, vestigial wings and broad heads. They were once human heroes who partook in Dragon Communion , for which they were cursed to crawl the earth as flightless imitations of Dragons , [ 1 ] losing their humanity in the process. [ 2 ] They wield scaly greatswords that resemble the jawbones of dragons, [ 1 ] [ 3 ] and can spew magma from their mouths. [ 2 ]
There are two non-boss Magma Wyrms that can be encountered. One is found in the lower part of Volcano Manor , accessible via an elevator near the Temple of Eiglay Site of Grace . The second is found in the Dragon's Pit minor dungeon in Gravesite Plain , found by progressing normally through the dungeon, and going up the stairs through a cave opening.
Magma Wyrm Makar resides in ancient ruins at the top of the Ruin-Strewn Precipice , blocking the secret path from Liurnia of the Lakes to Altus Plateau . Makar was likely a human hero who became a wyrm after partaking in Dragon Communion.
A Magma Wyrm is encountered in a lava pool near Fort Laiedd , southwest of the Seethewater Terminus Site of Grace. It can be lured out of the lava for an easier fight.
Great Wyrm Theodorix is encountered at the eastern end of the frozen river in the Consecrated Snowfield , northeast of the Inner Consecrated Snowfield Site of Grace. He was once an ancient troll warrior and hero of the war against the Giants , [ 4 ] who became a Magma Wyrm after partaking in Dragon Communion.
His attacks can inflict damage on the Crabs and Land Octopus nearby, which will cause them to aggro against it.
Unalloyed Gold Needle
Commander O'Neil is a boss in Elden Ring .
A veteran of a battle that took place in the Swamp of Aeonia in Caelid . He continued to brandish his flag in the rot-eaten battlefield even after his lord fled. [ 1 ] He wears the same armor and wields the same standard as Commander Niall , the leader of an army of no nation situated in Castle Sol .
In battle, Commander O'Neil summons the spirits of Exile Soldiers . Initially, he will summon five regular soldiers, and will summon three large soldiers after his health has been reduced to half. His attacks inflict Scarlet Rot .
O'Neil is in possession of the Unalloyed Gold Needle, which is required by Sage Gowry to stanch Millicent 's Rot.
Polyanna, Adopted Daughter can be summoned for this fight.
Commander Niall, a veteran general of Castle Sol , offered his prosthesis in exchange for the lives of imprisoned knights , forming an army of no nation. [ 1 ] A lone survivor, Niall commands the spirits of deceased knights to defend his master, who has long passed. [ 2 ] Niall guards a chest containing the Haligtree Secret Medallion (Left) , one-half of the Medallion required to gain access to the Consecrated Snowfield , the land of Miquella's Haligtree .
At the beginning of the fight, Niall summons the spirits of two Banished Knights , one with a sword and shield, and the other wielding dual swords. Niall will be relatively passive while the knights are alive, instead buffing them until they have both been defeated or his health has been reduced to half. Both Banished Knights will inflict Frostbite with their attacks. Niall himself uses a mixture of lightning and frost -based attacks. He can imbue his prosthesis with lightning and perform kicks and stomps, and he can use his halberd to generate frost.
Elemer of the Briar is a reoccurring boss in Elden Ring .
Elemer of the Briar, also known as the Bell Bearing Hunter , originally hailed from Eochaid , a land of proudly solitary ascetics. [ 1 ] He wears iron armor wrapped in iron thorns, which are a mark of the guilty and of those sentenced to death. [ 2 ] He was slated for execution at the Shaded Castle , home of the family of House Marais, however he evaded death by snatching the sword from the site of his looming execution and furnished it with battle skills from his homeland. [ 3 ] He gained the moniker "Bell Bearing Hunter" by killing numerous merchants and instructors [ 4 ] , and taking their Bell Bearings.
Elemer can be encountered in the Castellan's Hall of the Shaded Castle, the site of his failed execution. He can also appear in various locations throughout the Lands Between , typically in places where merchants can be found.
The Bell-Bearing Hunter will only appear when resting at night; to make him reappear after being defeated yourself, rest at the grace and set the time to night and then rest again.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
Briar Greatshield
Elemer is encountered in the hall at the top of the Shaded Castle. He can channel energy through his sword, allowing him to send it towards the player and control it at a distance, or fire a red beam by rotating it quickly.
The Bell Bearing Hunter appears at night, in the Hermit Merchant's Shack in the Capital Outskirts . The Hermit Merchant (Capital Outskirts) will disappear for the duration of the fight, but will reappear if the player dies or if they defeat the boss.
The Bell Bearing Hunter appears at night, outside the Isolated Merchant's Shack in Greyoll's Dragonbarrow . The Isolated Merchant (Dragonbarrow) will disappear for the duration of the fight, but will reappear if the player dies or if they defeat the boss.
Loretta is the boss of two locations : Caria Manor and Miquella's Haligtree . Her oath-sworn spectral form—Royal Knight Loretta—is found at the former, while her corporeal body defends the latter. Loretta is mechanically similar to the Tree Sentinels and Draconic Tree Sentinels and cannot be separated from her steed .
Loretta was once a royal Carian knight , [ 1 ] and served as a personal guard for Carian royalty . [ 2 ] Loretta's favored weapon was said to be the bow, and she developed sorceries imitating the power of a greatbow . [ 3 ] [ 4 ]
Loretta eventually became concerned with the plight of the Albinaurics and embarked on a long and bloody journey searching for a haven for the Albinauric people. She determined that the Haligtree was their best chance for eventual salvation. [ 5 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ] It was rumored she was actually an Albinauric herself, due to the shape and symbolism associated with her Silver Mirrorshield . [ 8 ] She would eventually find it at the Haligtree , in service to demigod Miquella , where she now remains.
Loretta appears to have entered into Miquella's service, replacing the blue glintstone that once adorned her war sickle with unalloyed gold . [ 2 ] Now she stands guard within the Haligtree, refusing to abandon her post although Miquella himself is long gone. Her lapis-lazuli blue cape is the emblem of the knightly pride that continues to guide her. [ 1 ]
Royal Knight Loretta is a boss in Elden Ring . She can be found at Caria Manor in the Royal Moongazing Grounds .
She appears to be an apparition of Loretta summoned to guard Caria Manor, just as the real Loretta presumably used to do before leaving her duty to help find sanctuary for the mistreated Albinaurics .
Loretta, Knight of the Haligtree is a mini-boss in Elden Ring found in Miquella's Haligtree and is required to progress to Elphael, Brace of the Haligtree . This boss is a stronger version of Royal Knight Loretta , found in Caria Manor.
O Horn-deck'd beast, from higher sphere deliver'd. Take root inside the tower's sculpted keepers. We beg of thee to dance and cavort. And perch'd within, we beg of thee; rise. - Hornsent Grandam
The Divine Beast Dancing Lion is an optional boss in Shadow of the Erdtree . The Remembrace variant may be encountered in the Belurat, Tower Settlement . The lion dancer at the Ancient Ruins of Rauh may be fought on Horseback.
The divine beasts were messengers of the heavens. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] The sculpted keepers are representations used to perform the ritual of the lion dance during the tower festival in Belurat, Tower Settlement . Only the greatest of horned warriors became divine beast warriors, and few became sculpted keepers. [ 3 ] [ 4 ]
When Messmer the Impaler 's army assailed the tower, the lion dance was turned towards martial ends. [ 2 ] [ 5 ] . By the end of Messmer's Crusade , only two divine beasts remained: one inside of Belurat, and another in the Ancient Ruins of Rauh . The one in Belurat was under the control of Hornsent Grandam , who directed the divine beast to rest until the Impaler's forces returned so it could exact vengeance for her people. When a Tarnished Champion happened upon the divine beast's resting place, Grandam assumed them to be one of Messmer's prodigies and ordered the divine beast to slay the Tarnished. It failed to do so, however, and was slain. The Tarnished can also encounter and slay the other divine beasts while exploring Rauh, thereby putting an end to them.
The Divine Beast will fight normally in its first phase. Around 70% health, it will switch between three storm -based elements on a timed basis: Lightning , Frost , and Wind.
The Divine Beast Dancing Lion at the Ancient Ruins of Rauh also has access to Death Blight .
In her childhood, she and her elder sister Rennala met these moons. Overlapping, as though nestled against one another. - Rellana's Twin Moons
Rellana, Twin Moon Knight is a Boss in Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree . She is encountered in Castle Ensis .
A scion of the moon -worshipping Carian royal family , Lunar Princess Rellana was the younger sister of Rennala, the Full Moon Witch . As young girls, the sisters encountered the twin moons , which overlapped, as if nestled against one another. [ 1 ] Taught sorcery by the illustrious Count Ymir , [ 2 ] Rellana later became an enchanted Carian Knight . [ 3 ]
Rellana was drawn to Messmer . In the days leading up to the crusade , the gallant Twin Moon Knight disavowed her birthright, entering ritual combat at the colosseum to demonstrate her fidelity to the Erdtree . [ 4 ] Her sister, by then Carian Queen, accepted her abdication and sanctioned her quest, bequeathing a length of her lustrous black hair. [ 5 ] Rellana and a group of her Carian Knights joined Messmer's crusade , [ 6 ] knowing full well that not even the brilliance of the moon could grant him succor. [ 7 ]
After claiming Castle Ensis in the Realm of Shadow , Rellana's lunar sorcery shattered a linchpin stone at Moorth Ruins , triggering a landslide that sank much of the hornsent settlement into the earth. [ 8 ] Before long, Rellana was known as the Sword of Messmer. [ 7 ] [ 9 ] [ 10 ]
Rellana is an optional boss as she can be bypassed via the sealed Spiritspring in Gravesite Plain to enter Scadu Altus . [ 11 ]
Needle Knight Leda can be summoned to fight this boss. However, her summon sign will not be available after entering Shadow Keep Castle for the first time.
During phase 2, both moves summon more glintblades.
Much like the Scadutree itself in appearance, a second stalk winds tightly around the first, almost as if in a tender embrace. - Shadow Sunflower Blossom
Scadutree Avatar is an optional Legend boss in Shadow of the Erdtree .
The Scadutree Avatar is encountered at the Scadutree Base in the lower section of Scaduview . It is accessible through the Shadow Keep , past the Tree-Worship Sanctum Site of Grace . The brittle Shadow Sunflower emerges from a pool of thick sap that covers the ground. [ 1 ] It is blackened and covered in thorny briars. Like the Scadutree , its towering form is gently embraced by a second stalk. [ 2 ]
The Scadutree Avatar is a dark manifestation of the Scadutree that contrasts the Erdtree Avatars of the Golden Order . [ 2 ] [ 1 ] It claimed Miquella's Great Rune after Miquella the Kind discarded it. [ 3 ]
Gaius and Radahn were good rivals in their youth, and this sorcery is a product of their friendly competition. - Blades of Stone
Commander Gaius is an optional boss in Shadow of the Erdtree encountered outside the backdoor of the Shadow Keep .
Commander Gaius was a noted warrior and military strategist who rode a giant boar as his steed. Gaius studied gravitational magic from an Alabaster Lord . [ 1 ] He was a fellow student of Radahn , a future demigod . He also befriended Messmer the Impaler , as both had in common that they were cursed from birth. The pair were as elder brothers to Radahn, with whom Gaius had formed a friendly rivalry. [ 2 ] [ 3 ] When Messmer embarked on the purge of the Land of Shadow on Queen Marika the Eternal 's orders, Gaius would join him and serve as the commander of his soldiers. He was never without his boar. [ 4 ] Even when Marika abandoned Messmer, Gaius remained steadfast, guarding the backdoor of Shadow Keep . It was here that he would meet his end at the hands of a Tarnished champion .
Commander Gaius is an albinauric without legs who rides a heavily armored, great-tusked boar. Gaius wears black iron armor patterned to represent fallen seeds and wields the Sword Lance . [ 1 ] He was cursed by his Albinauric heritage and as such was doomed to lose the use of his legs. [ 5 ]
Commander Gaius will charge with his boar to try to run you over. This can be dodge by jumping over with torrent or dodging at a very exact moment. He also uses gravity magic to attack enemies that are too far away.
All tainted flesh eventually becomes putrescence, and this clump of it imbibed St. Trina's nectar, which granted it eternal rest. And so it was that putrescence became her knight. - Remembrance of Putrescence
The Putrescent Knight ( 泥濘の騎士 , Nukarumi no Kishi , lit. "Mud Knight") is a Boss in Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree .
Interred within stone coffins and buried at sea in an age long past, the stagnant, congealed remains of tainted heroes eventually drifted toward the Gravesite Plain of the Lands Between , where all Death converges. [ 1 ] Though putrescence was once incinerated in ghostflame by Deathbirds , the contents of the vessels leaked and pooled at the bottom of the Stone Coffin Fissure , where they lingered in endless wait for true Death. [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
When St. Trina fell into the depths of the Fissure, her gentle sleep intensified into a deadly poison. Her nectar-like blood pooled, sprouting flowers , creating the Garden of Deep Purple . [ 4 ] [ 5 ] A mass of putrescence imbibed this nectar, finding salvation in her velvet, eternal sleep . From this, the putrescence reformed into a Putrescent Knight sworn to Trina. [ 2 ]
The Knight is both rider and mount , each lacking functional legs. It wields a vast, crescent -shaped cleaver of human bone and hardened putrescence, its strength drawn from the Knight's arcane power. [ 6 ] It conjures putrescence-born Death Sorceries , transmuting liquor into spiritual explosions of bruise-colored ghostflame . [ 3 ]
The Mother received signs from the Greater Will from the beyond of the microcosm. Despite being broken and abandoned, she kept waiting for another message to come. - Staff of the Great Beyond
Metyr, Mother of Fingers is an optional Remembrance Boss in Elden Ring , introduced in the Shadow of the Erdtree expansion.
Metyr, the brilliant daughter of the Greater Will , was the first of all stars to fall upon the Lands Between . [ 1 ] She possessed a microcosm which allowed her to receive messages from the Greater Will. [ 2 ] Metyr gave birth to the Two Fingers that guided the empyreans and the Tarnished . [ 1 ]
Long ago, Metyr was damaged and her Ringed Finger was removed. [ 3 ] She would never again receive a signal from the Greater Will. [ 2 ] The wisdom received by the Two Fingers was severed, and Metyr began birthing the aberrant Fingercreepers . [ 1 ] Metyr concealed herself within the Finger Ruins of Miyr, below the Cathedral of Manus Metyr, and waited for an eternity in vain for another signal from her lord. [ 2 ]
Although Metyr was broken, her Two Fingers continued guiding the empyreans without a word from the Greater Will. [ 4 ] It is said they presided over the birth of Marika ’s Erdtree as she created it from the primordial matter of the Crucible . [ 5 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ]
Metyr is a monstrous being made from fingers. Her head resembles an elongated thumb, and her face a pronounced thumbprint. At its center is a small, wart-like eye from which she blasts pink energy beams. [ 8 ] Ridge-like wrinkles, forming fingerprint-like patterns, cover Metyr's head and neck. She moves about on four sets of four-fingered hands, 16 coordinated finger legs in total. Metyr has two long-reaching arms that terminate in four-fingered hands tipped with sharp nails painted red. She may use these to pry open her abdominal cavity when birthing new Fingercreepers. Her tail forks into two tail fingers which wrap each other like a spiral. Between them rests an orb containing a microcosm. [ 2 ] [ 9 ]
Metyr's body festers with unhealed wounds. Upon her right chest is a deep laceration, and her belly has been split wide open, revealing gore and the stillborn remains of malformed fingers. Several more protrude from large lesions on her neck and tail fingers, and her microcosm appears clouded like an eye with cataracts. The iris of her bloodshot eye is quartered into a quatrefoil. [ 9 ]
Metyr is encountered at the Finger Birthing Grounds after ringing the hanging bell at the Finger Ruins of Miyr , located beneath the Cathedral of Manus Metyr on the Scadu Altus .
This area becomes accessible after advancing Count Ymir 's questline. To reach it, the player must ring the two hanging bells at the other Finger Ruins , return to the cathedral, examine Ymir's throne, and descend the newly revealed ladder to the ruins below. There, they must defeat Swordhand of Night Anna before ringing the final bell.
Metyr crawls around and can fire a laser beam from her eye. Try fighting her head-on. She punishes flanking during this phase.
Metyr summons her damaged microcosm and uses it to channel gravity magic. Be wary that she can fly during this stage, which can be troubling for some melee players.
I am the witch Ranni. I stole Death long ago, and search now for the dark path. That I might one day upend the whole of it, and rid the world of all that came before. - Ranni the Witch
Ranni the Witch , also known as Lunar Princess Ranni and Renna the Witch , is a character in Elden Ring . She is one of the Demigods , and the focus of one of the game's most elaborate questlines.
Ranni and her Dark Moon
A child born of the union between Rennala, Queen of the Full Moon and red-haired Radagon during the age of the Erdtree , Ranni embodied an alliance between Raya Lucaria and Leyndell . [ 1 ] She had two older [verification needed] brothers, Radahn and Rykard . [ 2 ] As a daughter of Carian royalty , she was a Lunar Princess, and raised in accordance with tradition. Led by the hand of her mother, young Ranni encountered her Dark Moon —cold, dark, and veiled in occult mystery. [ 3 ]
The Two Fingers named Ranni as an Empyrean , one with the potential to one day succeed Queen Marika as the divine ruler of the Lands Between , [ 4 ] and granted her a Shadowbound Beast named Blaidd to be her vassal. [ 5 ] He was approved of by Rennala and was raised as her foster brother. Ranni grew up playing with Blaidd, and they were often accompanied by Iji , a troll blacksmith who served the Carian royals. [ 6 ]
At some point, Ranni's father abandoned her mother to marry Queen Marika and assume the title of second Elden Lord . Although Ranni and her siblings were raised to Demigod status by their new stepmother, [ 7 ] their heartbroken mother was left indisposed, cradling her Amber Egg in all-consuming grief.
Ranni later [verification needed] ventured deep in woods, where she encountered a snowy crone who became her secret mentor. [ 8 ] She was an old witch well versed in cold-based sorceries , and she taught Ranni to fear the Dark Moon as she imparted her magic. [ 9 ] [ 10 ] The full Dark Moon, cold and leaden, would become Ranni's sigil and symbol of her power and authority. [ 11 ] [ 12 ] [ 13 ]
Ranni slew her body to evade the Two Fingers
Although the Two Fingers had chosen her as Marika's successor, Ranni did not wish to be a puppet for the Greater Will and resented her Empyrean fate. In order to escape it, Ranni stole a fragment of the Rune of Death from Maliketh, the Black Blade and, through a fearsome rite, imbued it into the blades of Numen assassins, who were said to be close to Queen Marika herself. She also gave a fragment to her brother Rykard as a last resort, so he could kill Maliketh if necessary. [ 14 ] Ranni plotted for the assassins to kill another individual while she simultaneously killed herself, slaying her own body while the other person died in spirit, thus freeing herself from being an Empyrean. [ 15 ]
In what would become known as the Night of Black Knives , the assassins murdered Godwyn the Golden , killing him in spirit, while Ranni killed herself in body, transferring her spirit into a doll said to be modeled after the image of her mentor, the Snow Witch. [ 8 ] This marked the step-siblings as the first demigod casualties in history. [ 16 ] Ranni's fate and her involvement in the plot remained largely unknown by the denizens of the Lands Between. [ 17 ]
At some point after the Night of Black Knives, Queen Marika shattered the Elden Ring . Ranni claimed a Great Rune , but appears to have discarded it, [ 18 ] and largely remained outside of the conflict that followed. As a consequence of her doll body, Ranni required extended periods of hibernation and withdrew from the world, hiding in the Carian Manor while her agents worked to bring about her plan of ridding the Lands Between of the influence of the Greater Will , allowing her to pursue her divine ascension on her own terms.
Ranni initially introduces herself as "Renna the Witch"
After the Shattering , Ranni learned of a recently arrived Tarnished riding the spectral steed, Torrent . She approached them at the Church of Elleh , inquiring whether they possess the steed that once accompanied Melina . [ 19 ] Upon confirming her suspicions, she bestowed upon them a Spirit Calling Bell and Lone Wolf Ashes , explaining that Torrent’s former master had entrusted her with delivering these items to its next owner. [ 20 ]
Ranni later reunited with the Tarnished at her Rise in the Three Sisters , where she invited them into her service. [ 21 ] She tasked the Tarnished with aiding Blaidd in uncovering a path into Nokron, Eternal City , to claim its treasure—a weapon capable of slaying the Two Fingers who had chosen her as an Empyrean. [ 22 ] [ 23 ] However, the path to Nokron would only reveal itself with the death of her brother, Starscourge Radahn , who had long held the stars —and thus Ranni's fate—in stasis with gravity magic . [ 24 ]
After Radahn's defeat and the acquisition of the Fingerslayer Blade , Ranni descended to the Ainsel River Main , leading to Nokstella, Eternal City . [ 25 ] There, she commanded her champion to rid her of the Baleful Shadows sent by the Two Fingers to assassinate her. [ 26 ] [ 27 ] Upon their victory, Ranni rewarded the Tarnished with a key to a Carian chest containing the Dark Moon Ring . [ 28 ] [ 29 ] Then, Ranni departed to fulfill her dark purpose. [ 30 ] [ 31 ] She traveled to the Cathedral of Manus Celes on the Moonlight Altar , where she slew the great Two Fingers beneath it and abandoned her doll body. [ 23 ] [ 32 ]
If the Tarnished retrieved the Dark Moon Ring and presented it to Ranni's doll, she accepted them as her consort, granting them the Dark Moon Greatsword as a symbol of their union. [ 33 ] [ 34 ] She revealed the full extent of her plan: to succeed Queen Marika as god and bring about the Age of the Stars . Ranni intends to remove the Elden Ring from the Lands Between and journey into the cosmos, [ 35 ] freeing its inhabitants from the influence of the Greater Will and granting them true autonomy over their lives. [citation needed]
After defeating the Elden Beast , the Tarnished may summon Ranni, who ushers in the Dark Moon and her Age of the Stars, realizing her vision for a new Order. [ 36 ]
Ranni's disembodied spirit inhabits the woven puppet of a four-armed maiden with pallid blue skin and long, flowing blue hair. Her left eye—the doll's right—is sealed shut by an azure sigil, while both open eyes glow cyan. She wears an elegant white gown beneath a voluminous fur cloak, lined with two long brown braids. A massive, floppy-brimmed witch’s hat rests atop her head, crowned with a delicate silver filigree. Luminious blue veinwork runs throughout the frozen brim's cold underside.

I can play the role of maiden. Turning rune fragments into strength. To aid you in your search for the Elden Ring. You need only take me with you. To the foot of the Erdtree. - Melina
Melina is a deuteragonist character in Elden Ring . She is a mysterious, spectral woman who offers an alliance with the Tarnished to help them on their journey to become Elden Lord. She may only be encountered when resting at specific Sites of Grace , though she may be summoned to help fight Morgott, the Omen King at the Elden Throne .
Melina has healed burns on her hands
Melina has long observed the Lands Between . [ 1 ] She was born at the foot of the Erdtree . [ 2 ] [ 3 ] She is a secret child of Queen Marika . Unlike Messmer or Morgott , Melina does not recall Marika with fondness. [ 4 ]
At some point long ago, Melina bore a vision of fire. [ 5 ] She was burned, leaving her bodiless; [ 6 ] a drifting spirit bound to Grace . [ 7 ] . Like her brother Messmer, [ 8 ] she was assigned a purpose by Marika. [ 3 ] However, she was unable to remember it. [ 9 ] And so, Melina traveled with the spectral steed Torrent in search of the Tarnished who would lead her back to the foot of the Erdtree. There, she may ascertain her given purpose.
Melina offers an accord
Torrent identifies and selects a maidenless Tarnished , [ 10 ] who recently washed up in the Stranded Graveyard , as one capable of brandishing the Elden Ring. [ 11 ] [ 12 ] Melina descends the spectral steed to grant the fallen champion a set of Sacred Flasks , choosing to aid them in violation of the Golden Order . [ 13 ]
Sometime later, Melina approaches the Tarnished to offer them an accord: She could play the role of the missing Finger Maiden in return for a ride to the foot of the Erdtree. [ 14 ] If the player desires the strength of runes , and, if they accept the accord, Melina entrusts them with the Spectral Steed Whistle and, therefore, Torrent. [ 10 ] Melina advises them to follow the guidance of Grace and seek the shardbearer at Stormveil Castle . [ 15 ]
Once the Tarnished defeats the demigod , Melina confesses that she was testing the Tarnished to see if they truly possessed the guidance of grace and if they were fit for the challenges to come. [ 11 ] Satisfied with her new companion, Melina offers to take them to Roundtable Hold , a gathering place for Tarnished champions. [ 16 ]
Throughout their journey, Melina also provides specks of guidance at certain sites of grace and, at churches dedicated to Queen Marika , she offers to reveal words spoken by Marika herself in the distant past. [ 17 ]
Melina looks for her purpose
Upon arriving at their destination, the Royal Capital at the foot of the Erdtree , Melina thanks the Tarnished for escorting her and leaves to ascertain her purpose, claiming that she can govern her movement more freely there. She entrusts the power of runes and Torrent to the Tarnished. [ 7 ] She will also offer her aid should the Tarnished challenge Morgott, the Omen King , ruler of Leyndell and guardian of the Erdtree.
After defeating Morgott, the Tarnished finds the path into the Erdtree barred by impenetrable thorns refusing entrance to all. Melina, having ascertained her purpose and seeing the Tarnished stuck, rejoins the Tarnished to say that she can burn the Erdtree to gain entrance inside, provided that she can get ahold of the Giants' Flame . And hence, she asks to go on a new journey, this time to the flame of ruin, far above the clouds, upon the snowy Mountaintops of the Giants . [ 18 ] and tells them she will take care of the "kindling" required to set the tree alight. [ 19 ]
Defeating Morgott also unseals a path to the Three Fingers . If the Tarnished rests at the nearest grace from their entombment, Melina will warn against meeting them and insist against inheriting the Frenzied Flame , for it would end all lives and births, which she cherishes. [ 20 ] If the Tarnished heeds her warning, Melina and the protagonist will continue their journey for the flame of ruin .
Melina awakens the flame of ruin
When making their way to the Forge of the Giants , Melina clarifies that she is now acting of her own volition, regardless of the purpose that her mother gave her. [ 21 ] After defeating the guardian of the flame , Melina puts her plan into action. She takes the Tarnished's hand, narcotizing them by doing so, and proceeds to sacrifice herself to channel the flame of ruin, setting the Erdtree aflame. [ 22 ] The Tarnished, maidenless once more, wakes up at Crumbling Farum Azula . There, they must confront the Black Blade Maliketh and recover the Rune of Death . In this, Melina fulfills her purpose: "The one who walks alongside flame, Shall one day meet the road of Destined Death." [ 23 ]
Melina vows to deliver Destined Death
If the player ignores her warnings at the Frenzied Flame Proscription , or just inherits the Frenzied Flame without speaking with her, she will say that The Tarnished is no longer fit, ending her accord, and forever leaving their side but threatening to kill them should they become the Lord of Frenzied Flame . [ 24 ]
If Melina did not fulfil her purpose as Kindling Maiden, an additional cutscene will play after the Lord of Frenzied Flame ending. At the Stone Platform , a chorus of whistling guides a transformed Melina to the Spectral Steed Whistle. [ 25 ] She retrieves the smoldering ring from a pile of ash and holds it in her open palm. As Torrent's final remnants are consumed by the Frenzied Flame, [ 26 ] Melina reveals her unsealed left eye and vows vengeance upon the player in the form of Destined Death . [ 27 ] [ 28 ]
Traveler's Set
Melina's questline runs parallel to the main story and is required to complete the game. It has two possible outcomes.
Roderika the spirit tuner prentice. Pleased to make your acquaintance. - Roderika, Spirit Tuner
Roderika, Spirit Tuner , also known as the Heartbroken Maiden , is a merchant character in Elden Ring .
A Tarnished [ 1 ] noblewoman who, despite having never seen the guidance of grace [ 2 ] , travelled to the Lands Between along with her companions. After arriving, those companions fell victim to Godrick , becoming subjects for his grafting. [ 3 ] Roderika alone survived, taking refuge in Stormhill Shack . It is here that she meets the Tarnished . She beseeches the Tarnished to bring a message to her grafted companions, whom she refers to as chrysalids, assuring them that she loves them and will join them soon. [ 4 ]
Roderika then heads to Roundtable Hold . Here, she becomes acquainted with Smithing Master Hewg , who takes notice of her gift for spirit tuning and is reminded of a spirit tuner he knew long ago, whose eyes were of the same hue as Roderika's. [ 5 ] Reluctantly, Hewg agrees to teach Roderika everything he knows about spirit tuning.
Roderika remains at Roundtable Hold, where she hones her newfound talent and eventually becomes a fully-fledged spirit tuner. [ 6 ] Her ability to sense spirits allows her to notice the Dung Eater's presence, which she warns the Tarnished about. [ 7 ]
After the Erdtree burns, Roderika attempts to convince Hewg to leave Roundtable [ 8 ] , but to no avail. She chooses to respect Hewg's decision, and remains behind with him even after he forgets her. [ 9 ] As the hold burns, she begs the Tarnished to become Elden Lord, and to use the weapons Hewg forged to slay Queen Marika the Eternal . [ 10 ]
Roderika can upgrade Spirit Ashes up to +10 using Grave Glovewort and Ghost Glovewort .
Roderika cannot be harmed or killed.
I'm trapped by the Hold, undying, smithing for you fools. That's all there is to it. - Smithing Master Hewg
Smithing Master Hewg is a character in Elden Ring .
Hewg is a blacksmith at the Roundtable Hold who improves armaments to maximum level and provides other services.
Hewg smiths weapons for the Tarnished
A Scaly Misbegotten bearing aspects of the primordial Crucible , Hewg practiced the once-divine art of smithing . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] A spirit tuner with distinctive eyes helped him out in the distant past, though she died before he could repay her. [ 3 ]
Long ago, Queen Marika cursed Hewg with an impossible task under her Golden Order : to create a weapon capable of slaying a god . [ 4 ] [ 5 ] Chained to the Roundtable Hold for eternity, he maintained the weapons of Tarnished seeking the Elden Ring . [ 6 ] [ 7 ]
When he meets Roderika , he recognizes that her eyes share the same hue as those of his old acquaintance. [ 8 ] Although reluctant at first, Hewg agrees to take Roderika under his wing at the insistence of the the Tarnished .
After the Tarnished sets fire to the Erdtree , the Roundtable Hold also begins to burn. Hewg's chains are broken, yet he insists on remaining in the hold, where he can continue to smith weapons to slay a god, despite Roderika's pleas for him to leave. [ 9 ] As the Roundtable burns, Hewg's mental state deteriorates, causing him to slur his words and, eventually, to forget both Roderika and the Tarnished. [ 10 ] Roderika decides to respect Hewg's decision to stay at the Roundtable, and resolves to remain with him. [ 11 ] Her last request is for the Tarnished to use the weapons Hewg smithed to slay Queen Marika. [ 12 ]
Smithing Master Hewg remains in a fixed location at the Roundtable Hold throughout the entire game.
As a Tarnished who wishes to stand before the Elden Ring and become Elden Lord, I am accumulating knowledge. To be all-knowing. - Sir Gideon Ofnir, the All-Knowing
Sir Gideon Ofnir, the All-Knowing ( 百智卿、ギデオン オーフニール , Hyakuchikyō, Gideon Ōfunīru ) is an NPC and boss in Elden Ring .
Sir Gideon Ofnir laid to rest
Gideon Ofnir is the Tarnished leader of Roundtable Hold and the adoptive father of Nepheli Loux . [ 1 ] Called to the Lands Between by the guidance of Grace, Gideon wishes to become Elden Lord. [ 2 ] To this end he accumulates information on the Shardbearers , employing a network of spies [ 3 ] to aid in his hunt for knowledge. Initially, he is apprehensive of the Tarnished , but after they have claimed a Great Rune he becomes willing to share his knowledge of the remaining shardbearers.
In the past, Gideon took in Nepheli Loux after she lost sight of the guidance of Grace, taking advantage of her youthful credulity. [ 4 ] He promised her that he would not allow the downtrodden to be cheated any longer if he became Elden Lord. [ 5 ] He also became acquainted with Preceptor Seluvis and Dolores the Sleeping Arrow , although he and Seluvis would go their separate ways because of Dolores. [ 6 ]
At some point, Gideon engaged in a long exchange with the Two Fingers , and in doing so learned that everything—including the Erdtree and the Two Fingers themselves—had been broken. [ 7 ] He also glimpsed into the will of Queen Marika the Eternal , shuddering in fear at an end that should not be. [ 8 ] He concluded from this that the queen wished for the Tarnished to struggle eternally. [ 9 ]
When a Tarnished champion makes their way to the Roundtable Hold , the first in a long time, Gideon is initially dismissive of them, welcoming them to the Hold but calling them a mere visitor. Gideon encourages the Tarnished to seek a Great Rune in order to gain audience with the Two Fingers and be welcomed as a proper member of the Roundtable Hold.
True to his word, Gideon inducts them as a true member of the Roundtable upon their meeting with the Two Fingers, and shares with them some of the information he has amassed on the Shardbearers .
Although Gideon had amassed knowledge on many of the shardbearers, he had not ascertained the whereabouts of four demigods: Ranni the Witch ; Mohg, Lord of Blood ; Malenia, Blade of Miquella ; and Miquella of the Haligtree . In his search for the latter, he sends his men to ransack the Village of the Albinaurics in Liurnia of the Lakes , knowing that the Albinaurics possess half of a secret medallion that would open the path to the Haligtree. The slaughter of the Albinaurics causes Nepheli to lose faith in him, which causes him to abandon her. [ 10 ] He also sought Latenna , an Albinauric woman with knowledge of the location of the other half of the medallion. [ 11 ] If the Tarnished claims one half of the medallion, Gideon's underling Ensha will ambush them in Roundtable Hold, apparently of his own volition. [ 12 ] After Ensha is defeated, Gideon compensates the Tarnished by sharing the possible whereabouts of the medallion's other half.
When the Erdtree rejects the Tarnished , forcing them to contemplate journeying to the Forge of the Giants to burn the thorns barring entry into the Erdtree, Gideon encourages them to take no heed of the Fingers' warning that this would be a cardinal sin. He also offers to reward the Tarnished for any information they can deliver on the four great runes whose locations are unknown. If the Tarnished pursues this quest to its ending, finding the cocoon of Miquella within the Mohgwyn Dynasty Mausoleum , Gideon thanks them, declaring that this is one of the last pieces he needs to put everything together.
After the Tarnished burns the Erdtree and unseals the Rune of Death , Gideon makes his way to Leyndell, Ashen Capital , where he confronts the Tarnished in the Erdtree Sanctuary. Upon his defeat, he warns them that a Tarnished could not become a Lord, and that a man cannot kill a god. [ 13 ]
Sir Gideon Ofnir, the All-Knowing is a boss encounter in Leyndell, Ashen Capital. He utilises both sorceries and incantations in combat, and learns new spells depending on whether you have defeated Rykard , Malenia, or Mohg. He only has seven memory slots, and knows six spells by default, meaning that the spells learned by defeating the aforementioned bosses can replace his default spells. If two of these bosses have been defeated, Gideon will lose Comet Azur. If all three have been defeated, he will lose Triple Rings of Light.
Let the scars I carve remind them. I am Nepheli Loux. Warrior. - Nepheli Loux, Warrior
Nepheli Loux, Warrior is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Nepheli Loux is a Tarnished warrior [ 1 ] from the Badlands . In her infancy, Nepheli lived through murder and pillage unchecked. [ 2 ] At some point, she lost the guidance of grace, and was taken in by Gideon Ofnir , who became her foster father. [ 3 ] Gideon promised Nepheli that if he became Elden Lord he would never allow the downtrodden to be cheated again, [ 4 ] earning her loyalty and aid in his pursuit of the title of Elden Lord. [ 5 ]
At the behest of Gideon, Nepheli infiltrates Stormveil Castle , [ 6 ] the home of the demigod Godrick the Grafted . Here, she encounters a Tarnished , who aids her in defeating the decrepit demigod. With Godrick slain, she returns to Roundtable Hold , where she awards them with an Arsenal Charm she found in Stormveil, and encourages them to speak to her foster father.
Travelling to Liurnia of the Lakes , Nepheli comes upon the Village of the Albinaurics , where she witnesses the slaughter of the Albinauric inhabitants at the hands of her father's men. [ 7 ] Reminded of the brutality she witnessed as a child, Nepheli vows to deliver justice to the oppressors, [ 8 ] assisting the Tarnished in defeating the Omenkiller responsible for the slaughter.
For giving into her emotions and abandoning the mission, Nepheli is cast aside by Gideon. [ 9 ] Without her estranged father's guidance, she becomes crestfallen, resigning to the lower levels of Roundtable Hold where she questions the faith she had in Gideon. [ 10 ]
The Tarnished obtains the ashes of The Stormhawk King in the Chapel of Anticipation , which they may choose to give to Nepheli. She can smell the ancient storm within the ash, [ 11 ] and is reminded of her first hawk. [ 12 ] Despite her inability to sense spirits within ash, [ 13 ] she gladly receives them.
After claiming the Stormhawk King's ashes, Nepheli encounters Kenneth Haight , who recognises her as a worthy heir of Limgrave . [ 14 ] Nepheli accepts the role, having been reminded by Limgrave of her own home. [ 15 ] As the new lord of Limgrave , Nepheli pledges to aid the Tarnished should they become Elden Lord, [ 16 ] pledging to call upon the storm to drive away the foulness that has settled on the winds. [ 17 ]

I was created to be a warrior vessel. Many great warriors reside within me, ever dreaming of becoming a great champion. - Alexander, Warrior Jar
Alexander, Warrior Jar is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Alexander is a living jar who travels the Lands Between , honing his strength to become a great warrior. [ 1 ] Alexander was created to be a warrior vessel, and the remains of many great warriors reside within him. [ 2 ] He originally came from Jarburg , a hidden village of living jars in Liurnia of the Lakes ; however, he vowed never to return, [ 3 ] claiming that "the path of champions must be trod alone". [ 4 ]
On his journey to become a grand champion, he seeks out Redmane Castle in Caelid , following rumours of a festival of combat. [ 5 ] On his way to the festival, he crosses paths with the Tarnished multiple times, often requiring their assistance to get out of unfortunate situations such as being stuck in potholes.
Alexander finally participates in the Radahn Festival , a brawl between several champions and Starscourge Radahn . Alexander survives the ordeal, however, he suffers damage to his body and is forced to hide for the remainder of the battle. [ 6 ] Undeterred, he replenishes himself with the bodies of mighty warriors littering the battlefield, vowing to grow even stronger. [ 7 ]
Next, Alexander travels to Mt. Gelmir , hoping to temper his body in the sea of fire, [ 8 ] such that it would never crack again. Finding the lava to be lukewarm and insufficient to strengthen his vessel, he sets his sights upon the Mountaintops of the Giants , seeking out the flame of ruin. [ 9 ]
Alexander travels to the mountaintops, where he witnesses the Tarnished's fight with the Fire Giant . [ 10 ] He then finds himself in Farum Azula , where he encounters the Tarnished for a final time. Impressed by his companion's feats of strength, he requests a duel. [ 11 ] The Tarnished emerges victorious and Alexander accepts his defeat, asking the Tarnished to take his innards with his final words. [ 12 ]
The Tarnished may present these innards to Alexander's nephew, the Jar-Bairn , who vows to become strong like his uncle Alexander. [ 13 ]

Blaidd, who served as Ranni's shadow, was a loyal ally who would defy destiny itself if it would have him turn upon his Lady. - Blaidd's Armor (Altered)
Blaidd the Half-Wolf is an NPC character in Elden Ring .
A guarded and boorish yet fiercely loyal half- wolf , [ 2 ] Blaidd was a shadowbound beast , created by the Two Fingers to serve Lunar Princess Ranni when she was chosen as an Empyrean . [ 3 ] [ 4 ] The wolf was the beast of the Carian royal covenant and irrefutably symbolized the moon 's pride, [ 5 ] and so he was approved and raised by Rennala, Queen of the Full Moon as Ranni's stepbrother. [ 6 ]
Blaidd was Ranni's unwavering blade. Like all shadowbound beasts, he could not truly die and was incapable of treachery against his master, compelled to enact her will. [ 7 ] Unbeknownst to him, however, an accursed failsafe within shadows overrode this directive should their master turn against the Two Fingers; should Ranni rebel against her prescribed fate , Blaidd’s unwavering loyalty would twist into madness, becoming a Baleful Shadow —a dire threat to Ranni herself. [ 8 ]
When Blaidd swore an oath to serve no master other than Ranni the Witch and her Dark Moon , [ 4 ] [ 9 ] a cold frost magic graced his Royal Greatsword . [ 10 ] The cold bothered him, nonetheless. [ 3 ]
Blaidd searched the Mistwood Ruins for a traitor named Darriwil , and the passage to Nokron, Eternal City , a long-lost ruin said to be banished underground by the Greater Will . [ 11 ] He travels to Redmane Castle to participate in the Radahn Festival . [ 12 ]
I am Seluvis, preceptor in the sorcerous arts. I don't know what it is the mistress sees in a provincial Tarnished like you... - Preceptor Seluvis
Preceptor Seluvis is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Seluvis is a preceptor in service of Ranni the Witch , the last princess of Caria . [ 1 ] He resides within a rise in the Three Sisters , openly expresses disdain towards the Tarnished [ 2 ] speaking to them with an air of superiority and hostility.
Seluvis is a collector of " puppets "—living beings transformed into thralls through the administration of a special draught brewed using Starlight Shards . [ 3 ] The physical bodies of these puppets are stored in a hidden cellar in the Three Sisters. [ 4 ] In the past, Seluvis was acquainted with Gideon Ofnir , however they parted ways after he turned Dolores the Sleeping Arrow ] into a puppet. [ 5 ] He was also familiar with Sellen , a sorceress who owes him a favour for assisting her when she was expelled from the Academy of Raya Lucaria . [ 6 ] Among his collection is the body of a sorceress wearing a Witch's Glintstone Crown , into which Sellen's Primal Glintstone can be inserted to provide her with a new body full of vigor. [ 7 ]
After becoming acquainted with the Tarnished, Seluvis asks them to give a potion to Nepheli Loux . If Nepheli drinks the potion, she will fall into a deep slumber and become a puppet , with her body residing in Seluvis' basement. Alternatively, if the Tarnished shows the potion to Gideon, he will dispose of it himself and suggest that the Tarnished tell Seluvis that they gave Nepheli the potion. [ 8 ] The potion can also be fed to the Dung Eater , resulting in him becoming a Dung Eater Puppet instead.
When the Tarnished confronts Seluvis about his collection of puppets, he offers to brew them their own puppet in exchange for Starlight Shards. [ 9 ] If they accept, Seluvis will later task them with retrieving an Amber Starlight , with which he brews an Amber Draught intended to turn Ranni into his puppet. [ 10 ] Ranni sees through this treachery, however, and bids the Tarnished leave, killing them if they do not.
Whether the Tarnished aids Seluvis in his betrayal or not, he can later be found dead in his tower, in the same kneeling position as his puppets.
Pidia's questline becomes locked after giving Ranni the Fingerslayer Blade , regardless of any steps already completed.
My eyesight has been weak since birth, you see. I can't tell which way I'm supposed to go next. But when I eat one of those grapes, I can feel a distant light in the back of my eyes. - Lightseeker Hyetta
Lightseeker Hyetta , later known as Finger Maiden Hyetta , is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Hyetta is a blind woman who travels the Lands Between in pursuit of a distant light that she believes to lead her to her duty as a Finger Maiden . [ 1 ] To this end, she begs for donations of Shabriri Grapes , which allow her to see the distant light in the back of her eyes . Hyetta requests grapes from The Tarnished at various points across Liurnia of the Lakes , eventually learning that the grapes she has been eating are human eyeballs , vomiting in repulsion. [ 2 ] [ 3 ] However, her resolve returns, and she becomes more determined than ever to become a Finger Maiden, realizing that with everyone's eyes together, the distant light is clearer. [ 4 ] With the light seeming closer than ever, Hyetta asks the Tarnished for a Fingerprint Grape , the eye of one who has been clasped by the burned Fingers . [ 5 ] The Tarnished fights and defeats Festering Fingerprint Vyke , a Tarnished who was scorched by the Flame of Frenzy , and offers his eyeball to Hyetta, who eats it. [ 6 ] [ 7 ]
If her questline has been advanced, the light guides Hyetta to the Frenzied Flame Proscription , far below the capital , where it is revealed that all along she had been guided by Three Fingers . She waits patiently on the side of the hall opposite the Site of Grace, urging the Tarnished to seek an audience with the Three Fingers, whose sanctum lies beyond a large stone door that was partially melted by searing fingerprints. [ 8 ] Should the Tarnished allow themselves to be burned by the Flame of Frenzy and touch Hyetta's forehead, she becomes a Finger Maiden and relay the words of the Three Fingers. She reveals that all that there is came from the One Great , and that every sin and every curse was born of a mistake of the Greater Will . She states the purpose of the Flame of Frenzy: to melt everything away until all is One again. Her body then becomes engulfed in Frenzied Flames, and she burns away, leaving behind the Frenzied Flame Seal . [ 9 ] [ 10 ]
Traveling Maiden Set (Altered)
For Lightseeker Hyetta to appear, you must have completed Irina of Morne 's questline, meaning Irina must be dead.
Burn the Erdtree to the ground, and incinerate all that divides and distinguishes. Ahhh, may chaos take the world! May chaos take the world! - Shabriri
Shabriri is an NPC in Elden Ring . He is a spirit that possesses the body of Bloody Finger Hunter Yura , [ 1 ] appearing after the player ascends the Grand Lift of Rold . Note that once Shabriri appears, Yura's questline will end regardless of how much progress has been made in it. It is not necessary to have started or completed Yura's questline for Shabriri to appear. If player visits the Three Fingers before reaching Shabriri, he will not appear. The Ronin's Set can be found on the ground where he would otherwise stand.
The most reviled man in all history, [ 2 ] Shabriri was found guilty of slander long ago and sentenced to blindness. With his eyeballs completely gouged out, it is said that, in time, the Frenzied Flame came to dwell within his empty sockets. [ 3 ] He believed that chaos should take the world and was regarded to be the origin of the sickness of Frenzied Flame. [ 2 ] Following his death, Shabriri endured as a spirit capable of inhabiting the bodies of others. [ 1 ] [ 4 ]
The Tarnished encounters Shabriri in the Mountaintops of the Giants , where he is inhabiting the body of Bloody Finger Hunter Yura . [ 1 ] The Tarnished, at the behest of Melina , is bound for the Forge of the Giants so she may set the Erdtree aflame. [ 5 ] However, Shabriri advises the Tarnished to seek out the Three Fingers in the depths below Leyndell , revealing that their ascendency to the throne of Elden Lord would otherwise require Melina's sacrifice. [ 6 ] He proposes an alternative path: the Tarnished may spare the life of Melina by inheriting the flame of frenzy and using their own body as kindling. [ 7 ] Shabriri bids the Tarnished become the Lord of Chaos , burning the Erdtree to the ground and incinerating all that divides and distinguishes. [ 8 ]
Shabriri is found near the Zamor Ruins Site of Grace on the Mountaintops of the Giants .
Shabriri is a summonable cooperator for the Godfrey, First Elden Lord / Hoarah Loux, Warrior boss fight if the player has visited the Three Fingers and has not used Miquella's Needle .

I am Yura, hunter of Bloody Fingers. - Bloody Finger Hunter Yura
Bloody Finger Hunter Yura is an NPC character in Elden Ring .
A ronin warrior in an iron kasa reminiscent of the straw hats worn in the Land of Reeds , [ 1 ] Yura was a hunter of Mohg 's Bloody Fingers . [ 2 ] He understood the hidden dangers of Dragon Communion and was once close to Eleonora, Violet Bloody Finger , a former Drake Knight for whom he harbored deep feelings. [ 3 ] [ 4 ] He wielded the unblockable Piercing Fang technique with deadly precision. [ 5 ]
Yura can first be found resting beneath a fallen ruin south of the Dragon-Burnt Ruins in Limgrave . He warns the Tarnished to stay away from Agheel Lake , where Flying Dragon Agheel roosts. [ 6 ] However, he offers his aid if the player is brave enough to hunt the mighty dragon . If the Tarnished slays Agheel, Yura speaks of the island Church of Dragon Communion , [ 7 ] and cautions against Dragon Communion's corrupting influence. [ 8 ]
When the Tarnished is ambushed by Bloody Finger Nerijus on the Murkwater River , Yura intervenes to thwart the invasion . [ 9 ] Later, Yura travels to the Academy of Raya Lucaria , where the Tarnished may repay his aid by assisting him against a Ravenmount Assassin . [ 10 ] There, Yura urges them to avoid Eleonora, the deadliest of all Bloody Fingers. [ 11 ]
Yura ultimately tracks Eleonora to the Second Church of Marika on the Altus Plateau . In their final battle, he suffers a mortal wound to sever the Bloody Finger from her hand. [ 12 ] As the Tarnished arrives too late, Yura implores Eleonora to renounce the cessblood before dying in their presence. [ 13 ]
After his death, Yura's body becomes host to Shabriri , who claims that Yura willingly surrendered his vessel. [ 3 ] [ 14 ]
Tell whoever put you up to this. That if I am to flower into something other than myself, I would rather rot into nothingness as I am. - Millicent
Millicent is an NPC cooperator in Elden Ring .
Millicent is a red-haired woman afflicted by Scarlet Rot . She and her sisters were found in the Swamp of Aeonia in Caelid by Sage Gowry , who raised them as his daughters. [ 1 ] Her four sisters travelled to Miquella's Haligtree under Gowry's guidance [ 2 ] , however Millicent alone remained behind.
At Gowry's behest, [ 3 ] the Tarnished obtains an Unalloyed Gold Needle and brings it to the Church of the Plague , where Millicent is slowly succumbing to the Rot. She inserts the needle to stall the Rot, regaining her strength. [ 4 ] However, her memories appear to have been affected by her sickness, as when she struggles to remember Gowry upon returning to his shack to find it abandoned. [ 5 ]
Millicent sets off on a journey across the Lands Between , retracing the route taken by Malenia, Blade of Miquella after the battle of Aeonia. [ 6 ] She once again meets the Tarnished on the Altus Plateau , where they present her with a Valkyrie's Prosthesis to replace her missing sword arm. [ 7 ]
Millicent's journey takes her to the Mountaintops of the Giants , in search of a fort containing a medallion which will allow her to access the Haligtree. [ 8 ] After the Tarnished claims the medallion and travels to the Consecrated Snowfield , Millicent makes her way to the Haligtree, and to Elphael , the city at its base. Here, she reveals to the Tarnished that she is of Malenia's blood, although she is unsure whether she is a sister, daughter, or offshoot of the Demigod. [ 9 ] Unbeknownst to Millicent, however, the Tarnished has been advised by Gowry to assist his remaining four daughters in killing Millicent, so that she can be reborn as a scarlet valkyrie when Malenia ascends to godhood. [ 10 ]
The Tarnished may then make a choice: kill Millicent alongside her four sisters, or fight alongside her against the attackers. Should the Tarnished kill Millicent, she will become a scarlet aeonia flower , waiting for Malenia's ascension. If the player fights alongside her, she will remove the needle from her body, allowing her to succumb to the Rot.

He's back. The Dung Eater. Again. I can hear them; the spirits as they howl and lament in fear of the curse. And worse than ever, the reverberations of the twisted malison itself. But after all this time, I've started to grasp it now. I can hear, in the malison, another fearsome Order. - Roderika, Spirit Tuner
The Dung Eater is an character in Elden Ring .
A self-described "scourge upon the living," the loathesome Dung Eater is a Tarnished who revels in murder and defilement. [ 1 ] He places the Seedbed Curse on his victims to sever their souls from the Erdtree and its grace , trapping them in eternal torment. [ 2 ]
The Dung Eater has the heart of an Omen without the body to match. He wears a malformed set of hefty red armor with tufts of red hair emerging from the bleeding stumps of its severed Omen horns . His helmet has no opening except for a deep gash over the right eye. His heavy, sun -shaped medallion represents the guidance he once saw, and the ring to which it will one day lead. [ 3 ] [ 4 ] He wields an accursed sword forged from the saw-like spine of the shrieking, [ 5 ] malformed giant Milos , whose perceived deformity mirrored his own. [ 6 ] This is his ideal form, and a reflection of the landscape of his mind. [ 7 ]
The Dung Eater received Grace
The Dung Eater envisioned an Order that would place a "pox upon life itself." [ 3 ] [ 7 ] [ 8 ] He murdered and defiled countless victims in a reviled ritual that produced Seedbed Curses, severing the dead souls from the Erdtree and binding them to his own flesh. [ 9 ] [ 10 ] [ 11 ] Those cursed in this way were doomed to be reborn as Omen, passing the curse to their descendants for all eternity. [ 12 ] With each pox, the Dung Eater nourished and grew his own Seedbed Curse. [ 13 ] He personally cultivated thousands of these horn-strewn tumors across the realm. [ 14 ] The art was among the most vile things in the entire Lands Between . [ 2 ]
The Dung Eater was caught and imprisoned for his unspeakable crimes, but his work continued unperturbed, much to the horror of fellow inmate Blackguard Big Boggart . [ 15 ] Then, he was publicly hanged in front of an angry crowd beneath the sun . Upon his death, the Dung Eater received Queen Marika 's grace. [ 16 ] The Dung Eater visited Elphael, Brace of the Haligtree , the Volcano Manor and Leyndell, Royal Capital after his revival. [verification needed] He was jailed with the noble Omen in the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds and eventually lost sight of his guiding grace. [ 3 ]
The Dung Eater at the Roundtable
The Dung Eater's red phantom appears at the Roundtable Hold when the Tarnished reaches the Altus Plateau . He sits on the floor among a pile of bodies in the room adjacent to Sir Gideon Ofnir 's study. Though he does not respect his fellow Tarnished , he abides by the pact of non-aggression. [ 17 ] [ 18 ] Roderika, Spirit Tuner senses the spirits trapped by the Dung Eater and warns the Tarnished of the curse. [ 9 ] [ 4 ]
If the player collects a Seedbed Curse and speaks to the Dung Eater, the Dung Eater detects its presence. He produces a Sewer-Gaol Key and asks the Tarnished to release his corporeal body from the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds. [ 19 ] If he is released, the Dung Eater attacks and defiles Blackguard Big Boggart. When the player discovers the evidence, the Dung Eater invades them as well. [ 20 ] If repelled, Dung Eater exclaims something unexpected happened. Despite the curse stirring within, his blessing was warded off by the protagonist—a feat none had succeeded in before. [ 21 ]
The Dung Eater has a revelation: he was not the one who could curse the world as in his vision. He was just the means to get there; his flesh is the one that must receive the blessing. [ 22 ] He asks to be killed and defiled by the Seedbed Curse until his gestated Mending Rune of the Fell Curse coalesces. [ 23 ] If this Rune is added to the Elden Ring , it curses Order itself and ushers in the Blessing of Despair . [ 24 ]
The Tarnished may also choose to simply kill him, leave him in his jail, or turn him into a puppet with Seluvis's Potion . [ 14 ]
"Do you know of the Noble Goldmask? Though he was but a Tarnished, living outside the Lands Between, he was a great scholar, who foresaw the coming guidance of Grace." - Brother Corhyn
Goldmask is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Goldmask is a Tarnished scholar and staunch Golden Order fundamentalist. [ 1 ] He predicted the guidance of Grace, and upon being beckoned by it he came to the Lands Between to contemplate the Golden Order. [ 2 ]
Although a Golden Order fundamentalist himself, Goldmask was critical of the hunters of Those Who Live in Death, lamenting that their learnedness had been reduced to fanatical raving and an obsession with finding a great evil to contend with, a concept which he did not believe existed within the Golden Order. [ 3 ]
While contemplating the Erdtree in the Altus Plateau Goldmask is approached by Brother Corhyn , a man of the cloth who wished to travel alongside him as a scholar. In Leyndell , Goldmask becomes perplexed by the identity of Radagon , whose existence calls into question the principle that Queen Marika the Eternal is the one true god. [ 4 ] With the help of the The Tarnished , Goldmask learns that Radagon is Marika.
Goldmask and Corhyn then travel to the Mountaintops of the Giants , where Corhyn becomes aware of Goldmask's suspicions regarding the holism of the Golden Order. [ 5 ] Corhyn begins to doubt Goldmask's faith, questioning his decision to travel to the Mountaintops. [ 6 ]
Goldmask had come to the revelation that the imperfection of the Golden Order and the instability of ideology was due to the fickleness of the gods. [ 7 ] After the Erdtree burns, Goldmask returns to Leyndell and dies on the hill near the Erdtree Sanctuary, leaving behind the Mending Rune of Perfect Order , which would allow the Golden Order to be perfected.
Goldmask cannot be made hostile, and will disappear if attacked, giving no Runes or item drops. He will reappear in his last location after resting at a Site of Grace.
Goldmask's Rags Gold Bracelets Gold Waistwrap
I, Boc the seamster, am forever in your service. May the throne of Elden Lord be yours. - Boc
Boc the Seamster or Demi-Human Boc is an NPC in Elden Ring . He offers the player the ability to modify their garments , free of charge.
Boc is a demi-human seamster from Limgrave . He was very close to his mother , a seamstress, until her passing. Inspired by her, Boc aspired to follow in her footsteps and inherited her sewing kit . He lived with a demi-human tribe in a Coastal Cave on the western coast of Limgrave, but at some point, he was cast out by his kin . Lost and isolated, Boc was transformed into a bush by a spell .
A Tarnished came across Boc and broke the spell, freeing him. Grateful, Boc offered to sneak back into the cave where he had been exiled to retrieve something precious with which to repay his champion. However, his former tribe discovered him and beat him mercilessly. When the champion found Boc again, he warned them not to enter the cave. Ignoring his warning, the champion avenged Boc and recovered his mother's cherished sewing needle . Moved by their kindness, Boc vowed to become a seamster like his mother.
Boc next encounters the champion in Liurnia of the Lakes , where he humbly offers his services as the champion's personal seamster. He will trace the champion's footsteps, following them to the Altus Plateau and the Royal Capital . Boc remains in awe of his master, and as the Tarnished champion draws closer to the throne of the Elden Lord , Boc will begin to refer to them as a lord.
Even though Boc is given a golden needle worthy of a master seamster, allowing him to perform modifications to the grab of the demigods themselves, Boc remains terribly self-conscious and bothered by his appearance. He asks his master whether they think he is ugly and expresses an interest in being reborn by Queen Rennala . Should the Tarnished champion aid Boc in fulfilling his wish to be reborn, Boc will travel to the Academy of Raya Lucaria and will be reborn a human through her powers. However, like many of those reborn by Rennala, the process goes awry, and Boc dies shortly thereafter.
Instead, the Tarnished champion may find a Prattling Pate which speaks with the voice of Boc's deceased mother, and tells him he's beautiful. Upon hearing this, Boc will be contented and will continue faithfully serving his lord.
Note: This dialogue includes variations for Boc calling the player master (ご主人さま) and lord (わが王よ).
Well, well, well? Thought you'd just help yourself to a man's personal belongings? You scheming little thief. The gods demand repentance! Cough up your coin, all of it! - Patches
Patches is an NPC and boss in Elden Ring . He surrenders if you reduce his HP to 50% or less. From then on, he acts as a merchant and gives helpful advice to players.
Patches is a Tarnished who leads a group of bandits , operating out of Murkwater Cave in Limgrave . He is a nomadic and free-spirited individual with a proclivity for tricking people and robbing them of their possessions.
If the Tarnished opens the treasure chest in Murkwater Cave, Patches accosts them with accusations of theft. After a brief fight, Patches surrenders and offers his services as a merchant . He reveals that the bandits he leads are former foot soldiers from a defeated army.
Later, Patches moves to Liurnia of the Lakes , setting up camp on the Scenic Isle . Here, he encounters the Tarnished again and imparts knowledge about the Abductor Virgin below the Academy of Raya Lucaria , which he claims is enchanted with a spell of transportation that will send one straight to the base of the Erdtree . In reality, the Virgin's spell sends unwitting adventurers to the Subterranean Inquisition Chamber on Mt. Gelmir . Patches also informs the Tarnished about Rya , advising them to assist her.
Patches later travels to Mt. Gelmir. The Tarnished may encounter him here, where he will kick them into a ravine, warning them to steer clear of Volcano Manor . Despite these warnings, the Tarnished encounters Patches in the Manor, where he reveals himself to be a member of the Recusants who serve Tanith, Volcano Manor Proprietress . Patches' latest target is Great Horned Tragoth , and he quickly offloads this difficult task onto a newbie.
After the Tarnished defeats Rykard, Lord of Blasphemy , Patches leaves Volcano Manor. He is next found in the Shaded Castle nursing a serious injury. He gives the Tarnished a set of Dancer's Castanets , which he beseeches them to return to Tanith, who is presently feasting upon Rykard's corpse. Patches then returns to Murkwater Cave, where he once again opens up his shop, following a brief rematch with the Tarnished.

O Greater Will, hear my voice. I am the recusant Bernahl, inheritor of my brother's will, and you will fall to my blade. - Knight Bernahl
Knight Bernahl is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Residing in the Warmaster's Shack of Limgrave , Knight Bernahl (騎士ベルナール) is a tarnished merchant who sells a number of Ashes of War . Bernahl was once a Tarnished champion worthy of becoming a lord, until his Finger Maiden cast herself into the flames. [ 1 ]
Should the Tarnished join the Volcano Manor , they'll meet again with Bernahl, but this time he'll introduce himself as "Recusant Bernahl" (背律者ベルナール). After assassinating the first targets commissioned by Tanith , Bernahl will invite the Tarnished to join him in his hunt of Vargram the Raging Wolf and Errant Sorcerer Wilhelm at the Fortified Manor of Leyndell, Royal Capital .
He will become as a summon against the Godskin Duo in Crumbling Farum Azula .
The Tarnished will come face to face with Bernahl one last time to the north of the Great Bridge in Crumbling Farum Azula , where the recusant will invade his former comrade.
