Academy Gate Town Volcano Manor Jarburg
Diallos Hoslow is a scion of House Hoslow and the younger brother of Juno Hoslow . From a young age, Diallos was all talk and no trousers, with an inability to commit to action. As a result, Juno inherited the Hoslow legacy without resistance. Juno loved his brother dearly and showered him with adoration. Diallos, in turn, admired his brother, a mighty warrior who lived up to the bloody legacy of House Hoslow. Diallos aspired to be like his older brother, knowing that pursuing the bloody legacy of their house would break his brother's heart.
Diallos had a servant by the name of Lanya and the two were companions since childhood. At some point, the two set out on a journey in the Lands Between , but Diallos lost track of the fickle Lanya, and the two became separated. He made his way to Roundtable Hold where he implored the Hold's visitors to keep an eye out for Lanya.
Diallos eventually managed to track Lanya down to Liurnia of the Lakes , where he found her dead. He deduced that the recusants of the Volcano Manor were behind her death and swore vengeance upon them. He tracked them down to their hideout on Mt. Gelmir , but when the proprietor of the manor, Lady Tanith , offered him a place among them, flattering him by telling him he had the stuff of champions, Diallos abandoned his vengeance and decided to join the manor as a recusant.
Diallos pursued the path of a recusant, dirtying his hands time and again, but soon came to realize his folly. Having achieved nothing, he declared himself a complete fool, just as his brother had said, for abandoning the path of revenge and sullying the name of his house.
Diallos left the Volcano Manor and travelled to Jarburg , a settlement for Living Jars . Diallos became Jarburg's new "Potentate" and devoted himself to caring for the jars. Diallos was at peace with his new calling, feeling for the first time in his life that he was on the straight and narrow. The jars enjoyed his soft, silky hands, but they were disappointed by his apparent lack of strength and courage.
When Jarburg was invaded by jar-poachers, Diallos took up arms to defend his charges. He was mortally wounded in the battle, but managed to drive off the poachers and saved most of the jars. Diallos died at peace, having finally proven his worth to his dear jars and to himself.

I'm Latenna. An Albinauric, the same as Old Albus. My apologies for my coarse words earlier. I presumed the worst, seeing that you were another Tarnished, like that all-hearing brute. - Latenna
Latenna the Albinauric is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Latenna is an Albinauric woman and a deft archer. She and her wolf companion , Lobo , began their journey in the lands of the Haligtree , a sanctuary for Albinaurics. [ 1 ] She journeyed to the far south, eventually coming to Liurnia of the Lakes .
Here, Latenna was accosted by the servants of Sir Gideon Ofnir, the All-Knowing , [ 2 ] a Tarnished wishing to gain access to the hidden lands of the Haligtree. Believing Latenna had a secret medallion that opened the way to the Haligtree, [ 3 ] Ofnir's servants attacked her and killed her wolf, leaving her crippled, but Latenna still refused to divulge the location of the medallion, feigning ignorance.
After the Tarnished receives a half of the secret medallion from the elderly Albinauric Albus , Latenna tells them the location of the other half, [ 4 ] and asks them to bring her along to the lands of the Haligtree, where she might fulfill her duty. [ 5 ] The Tarnished agrees, and Latenna voluntarily becomes Spirit Ash , [ 6 ] so they might carry her with them.
In the Mountaintops of the Giants , Latenna alerts the Tarnished that the medallion is near when they approach Castle Sol . [ 7 ] With the second half retrieved, the path to the Haligtree is opened. She urges them to bring her to the liturgical town of Ordina . [ 8 ] Here, a towering young Albinauric known as Phillia slumbers. [ 9 ] Latenna grants her the birthing droplet, allowing her to create new life for all the Albinaurics. [ 10 ] She thanks the Tarnished for their aid, promising to fight alongside them until the bitter end, requesting that they lay her to rest by Lobo once the fighting is done. [ 11 ]
Death... My sin... Should not be touched...by the hand of man... - Gurranq, Beast Clergyman
Gurranq, Beast Clergyman , also known as Beast Clergyman and Maliketh, the Black Blade , is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Gurranq is a hulking, bestial high clergyman from Farum Azula who resides in the Bestial Sanctum in north-eastern Caelid . [ 1 ] Long ago, his terrifying ferocity earned him the name "Death of the Demigods. [ 2 ] [ 3 ] [ 4 ] [ 5 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ] Presently, he seeks Deathroot , a product of the Rune of Death which spread through the Lands Between following the murder of Godwyn the Golden on the Night of Black Knives . [ 8 ] Gurranq consumes Deathroot, although it does not appear to sate him. [ 9 ]
Gurranq was assisted in his eradication of the Deathroot by D, Hunter of the Dead , a hunter of Those Who Live in Death . [ 10 ] However, D passes this duty onto a Tarnished after noticing their prowess for weeding Deathroot. [ 11 ] The Tarnished brings the Deathroot they find throughout the world to Gurranq, and is given access to bestial incantations in exchange. [ 12 ] Once they have fed Gurranq all the Deathroot they can find, Gurranq leaves the sanctum. Although still not sated, he realises that he can do no more, and that his appetite will be his sole companion. [ 13 ]
When the Tarnished travels to Crumbling Farum Azula to claim the Rune of Death, they encounter Gurranq once more. If the Tarnished had given Gurranq all the Deathroots, he is saddened by his friend's betrayal, but nonetheless attacks the Tarnished to protect the Rune of Death from them. Gurranq is overwhelmed, forcing him to use the Rune of Death to empower himself and reveal his true form as Maliketh, the Black Blade , [ 14 ] shadowbound beast of Queen Marika the Eternal . [ 15 ] The Tarnished defeats Maliketh, and unleashes the Rune of Death.
I am Iji. The Carian royal family's dedicated blacksmith, and Lady Ranni's war counsellor. - War Counselor Iji
War Counselor Iji , also known as Smithing Master Iji , is a character in Elden Ring .
War Counselor Iji is a wise and kind-hearted Troll who smithed weapons for the Carian royal family and their enchanted knights . He has known Ranni and Blaidd since they were children, and they would let him join in when they played. [ 1 ] Along with Blaidd, he swore allegiance to Ranni when she renounced her flesh and chose the dark path of the Empyrean . [ 2 ]
He made weapons for Radahn during the Shattering but now counsels and aids Ranni the Witch in her opposition to the Greater Will .
Iji maintains a smithing post near the Kingsrealm Ruins and warns the player to beware Caria Manor . If the played joins Ranni's followers, Iji welcomes them with open arms.
Jerren recalls that the weapons Iji smithed were blunt, yet did not decay when faced with Scarlet Rot . [ 3 ] Jerren may also offer a vital clue regarding Ranni's fate, which helps Iji to come to the realisation that General Radahn must be killed in order to release the stars and Ranni's own fate. [ 4 ]
Iji is also shown to care for Blaidd [ 5 ] , however he also harbours some reservations. Fearing that, as her sworn shadow , Blaidd will go mad and become a curse for Ranni for resisting the Two Fingers [ 6 ] , Iji imprisons Blaidd in the Forlorn Hound Evergaol . [ 7 ] Later, after Blaidd breaks free of his imprisonment and gives his life in defence of Ranni, Iji admits that he misjudged Blaidd's loyalty, and senses that he will soon join Blaidd in death. [ 8 ] Later, he can be found dead, his body ablaze with black flame , with the corpses of Black Knife Assassins nearby.
My name is Thops. Presuming you're interested, I can teach you sorceries, as promised. Only, none of them are particularly great... - Sorcerer Thops
Sorcerer Thops is an NPC in Elden Ring .
A former student of the Academy of Raya Lucaria , Thops was considered a "bluntstone" [ 1 ] , lacking any talent for sorcery, yet he looked up to Sorceress Sellen [ 2 ] prior to her expulsion from the Academy.
When the Shattering broke out, the Academy declared that they would not interfere with the conflict, and the scholars cast repelling seals on the gates. [ 3 ] Thops was outside the Academy's grounds when the seals were cast [ 4 ] , and thus found himself unable to return.
Thops encounters the Tarnished at the Church of Irith in Liurnia of the Lakes , just beyond Stormveil Castle . He offers to share his limited knowledge of sorceries with them in return for a small donation [ 5 ] , and advises them to seek out an Academy Glintstone Key so that they can access the Academy of Raya Lucaria. Should the Tarnished find a second Glintstone Key, they may offer it to Thops, allowing him to finally return to the Academy. Shortly after returning, he passes away hunched over a desk, however he leaves behind a sorcery which may one day form the basis of a new Conspectus . [ 6 ]
Tarnished, are we? A wonder you should turn up here. I am Sellen, a sorcerer, quite plainly. - Sorceress Sellen
Sorceress Sellen is a merchant NPC in Elden Ring . She is initially found in Waypoint Ruins in Limgrave and is eager to share her glintstone sorceries .
Sellen was considered to be the most promising glintstone sorceress to ever attend the Academy of Raya Lucaria . [ 1 ] Her first teacher at the academy was the sorcerer Azur , one of the founding glintstone sorcerers and originator of the Karolos Conspectus . [ 2 ] [ 3 ] Azur, along with Lusat , was banished from the academy due to their study of the Primeval Current [ 4 ] , a study Sellen wished to pursue. However, following accusations of unspeakable treatment of her fellow scholars under the name of the Graven Witch, Sellen too was expelled from the academy. [ 5 ] Sellen had sought to restore the Primeval Current, desiring glintstone sorceries unbound by terrestrial taboos and the pedantry of the Carian Royal Family . [ 6 ]
Sellen was also an acquaintance of Preceptor Seluvis , and a frequent visitor to his underground cellar [ 7 ] , where he kept his collection of puppets. When Sellen was expelled, Seluvis helped her in some capacity, for which she owes him. [ 8 ]
At some point following her banishment, Sellen was imprisoned in Witchbane Ruins on the Weeping Peninsula , bound by the Academy's shackles. [ 9 ] She managed to manifest a projection of herself [ 10 ] in the Waypoint Ruins in Limgrave . It is here that she meets the Tarnished , who becomes her apprentice [ 11 ] , learning glintstone sorceries from her. When she learns that the Tarnished has found Master Azur on Mt. Gelmir , she requests that they seek out Master Lusat, speculating that he returned to his home of Sellia, Town of Sorcery . [ 12 ] The Tarnished discovers Lusat, in a near-inorganic state [ 13 ] much like Azur, in Sellia Hideaway , and reports back to Sellen.
Witch-Hunter Jerren locates Sellen
Much like Ranni the Witch , Sellen's fate is tied to the stars, and with the defeat of Starscourge Radahn , Sellen becomes dispossessed of her immortality. [ 14 ] This makes her a target of Jerren , a friend of the Carian Royal Family who once made a promise to exterminate the witch. Sellen reveals to the Tarnished that the form they have been speaking to is a projection [ 10 ] , and that her true body resides in Witchbane Ruins. [ 15 ] The Tarnished meets with Sellen's true body, shackled in the ruin's cellar, and she asks them to remove her Primal Glintstone , beseeching them to look after it. [ 16 ] Jerren arrives to find Sellen's previous body already perished. [ 17 ] The Tarnished later places Sellen's Primal Glintstone into a puppet in Seluvis's basement, which bears a striking resemblance to Sellen's old body.
Sellen, now in her new, more youthful body [ 18 ] , returns to the Academy and displaces Rennala, Queen of the Full Moon . [ 19 ] She has the bodies of Azur and Lusat moved back to the Academy, so that she can finally hone the Primeval Current. [ 20 ] She offers her support to the Tarnished in their mission to become Elden Lord , and requests that when the time comes, they illuminate her about the secrets of life which course the Elden Ring [ 21 ] Before long, however, Jerren finally catches up to her. [ 22 ] Should the Tarnished aid her in beating back Jerren, she will continue her research. When the Tarnished next sees her, she has transformed into a Graven Mass .
I teach incantations, the strength granted us by the Two Fingers, and explore the secrets of the Golden Order. - Brother Corhyn
Brother Corhyn is a merchant NPC in Elden Ring . He can be given prayerbooks to access an array of Incantations .
Brother Corhyn is a cleric of the Golden Order . At some point, Corhyn made his way to Roundtable Hold , where he teaches the incantations of the Two Fingers to Tarnished of the Roundtable, hoping that one of them might one day claim the title of Elden Lord , so that Corhyn might council them. [ 1 ] When a Tarnished champion makes their way to the Roundtable, Corhyn introduces himself to them, and offers his tutelage. Corhyn will even teach the champion heretical incantations, from outside the line of the Erdtree , though he does so reluctantly.
After the Tarnished champion opens the way to the Altus Plateau , Corhyn announces that he is departing the Roundtable to search for the legendary Goldmask , an eminent scholar of the Golden Order . While searching for Goldmask, Corhyn continues his own investigations into the nature of the Golden Order, and while he makes some advancements, he also becomes aware of how little he truly knows. [ 2 ] With guidance from the Tarnished champion, Corhyn is united with Goldmask.
Corhyn takes it upon himself to become Goldmask's disciple and to chronicle his wisdom, deciphering the meaning behind every minute movement made by the mute Goldmask. The process goes well, until Goldmask's movements suddenly cease, as he is confounded by the nature of Radagon . The Tarnished champion may solve the riddle, revealing to Goldmask that Radagon and Queen Marika the Eternal are in fact one and the same, allowing Corhyn to continue his work. [ 3 ]
Goldmask leads his disciple to the Forbidden Lands and the Mountaintops of the Giants , where none may tread. Corhyn continues his duty, but begins to doubt his master. He detects in his movements that Goldmask has begun to suspect the holism of the Golden Order , an unacceptable heresy in Corhyn's mind. [ 4 ] Corhyn continues to serve his master, but is tormented by doubt.
After the Tarnished champion unleashes the flame of the giants to burn the Erdtree , Corhyn is found in the ashen ruins of Leyndell, Royal Capital . Corhyn denounces his master as nothing more than a madman, who rejected the perfection of the Golden Order and sought to replace it with his own "perfected" order. [ 5 ] As the Erdtree burns above him, Corhyn loses his mind. Alternatively, Corhyn may be offered the Tonic of Forgetfulness, causing him to remain in the Mountaintops, seemingly unaware that Goldmask has returned to Leyndell. [ 6 ]

He is also possible to summon as a cooperator in Black Knife Catacombs .
Darian, more commonly known as D, Hunter of the Dead is an undead hunter and an ally of Gurranq, the Beast Clergyman . Darian has a twin brother by the name of Devin , who was also called D. While Darian and Devin had different minds and bodies, they shared a single soul, and were reviled as cursed beings. The twins found sanctuary in the Golden Order , the only institution to accept them. [ 1 ]
Darian befriended the spellblade Rogier , with whom he shared an interest in Those Who Live in Death . The two friends eventually parted ways [ 2 ] , each coming to their own conclusion about the undead.
Darian became a proponent of Golden Order fundamentalism and a hunter of Those Who Live in Death , seeking to stamp out defilement and preserve the perfection of the Golden Order. Darian encountered and became an ally of Gurranq, who bid him to weed out Deathroot , a plant which caused the emergence of Those Who Live in Death, so that he might feed it to him.
Following the traces of death, Darian came upon Summonwater Village , where a Tibia Mariner had set up shop. In the outskirts of the village, he encounters a Tarnished champion and warns them to stay away from the village. After the champion defeats the Mariner and weeds out the Deathroot, Darian offers them a deal; to take his place as Gurranq's servant, in exchange for Gurranq sharing with them the strength of beasts.
With other matters to attend to, Darian relocates to Roundtable Hold . After the Tarnished takes him up on his offer, he declares them brothers-in-arms and teaches them the fundamentalist techniques wielded by the hunters of the dead. Another resident of Roundtable Hold and associate of the Tarnished champion is Fia , a deathbed companion and servant of the Prince of Death . Fia gives the Tarnished a dagger, asking them to find its rightful owner. After the Tarnished shows Darian the dagger, he offers to return it to its owner.
Shortly thereafter, Darian is murdered by Fia. The Tarnished champion may retrieve Darian's armor and find his twin . Devin will don the armor, and avenge his brother, finding Fia at the foot of the Prince of Death and murdering her.
Twinned Set
I am the guardian of Those Who Live in Death. They call me a foul and rotten witch. Yet you still wish to be held by me? - Fia, Deathbed Companion
Fia, Deathbed Companion is an NPC character in Elden Ring .
Fia is initially located at the Roundtable Hold in the room adjacent to Smithing Master Hewg . She may be hugged to gain a Baldachin's Blessing . At a certain point during her questline, she moves to the Prince of Death's Throne at the Deeproot Depths .
Fia's quest intersects with the questlines of D, Hunter of the Dead ; D, Beholder of Death ; Ranni the Witch ; and Sorcerer Rogier .
Fia was once a Deathbed Companion. She would receive the warmth and vigor from champions, and then lay with the remains of an exalted noble, to grant him another chance at life. [ 1 ] This was the sole purpose of Fia's existence, and was considered a sacred act in her homeland. [ 2 ]
However, before Fia could bear the noble into new life, she was awakened by the guidance of grace, and chased from her birthplace, travelling to the Lands Between . [ 3 ] At some point she met a chivalrous knight by the name of Lionel the Lionhearted . Upon meeting the exiled Fia, Lionel declared himself to be her father, and became her loyal companion. [ 4 ]
Fia found herself in Roundtable Hold , where she continued to perform her role as a Deathbed Companion. Here, she encountered Rogier , a spellblade obsessed with Those Who Live in Death, and a Tarnished champion seeking to become Elden Lord . Rogier began an investigation into the events surrounding the Night of Black Knives , which had led to the death of Godwyn, aided by the Tarnished champion. Fia subtly aided the pair in their investigation, pointing them towards the Black Knifeprint , [ 5 ] and granted her services to the Tarnished champion, taking their warmth and vigor in exchange for her blessings.
Unbeknownst to the other Tarnished of Roundtable Hold, Fia was the companion of Godwyn , the Prince of Death, and wished to become a mother to Those Who Live in Death. [ 6 ] After asking the Tarnished to return a Weathered Dagger to D, Hunter of the Dead , Fia kills D, who was in possession of one half of the Cursemark of Death , [ 7 ] and returns the Cursemark to the malformed corpse of Godwyn in Deeproot Depths . She then solicits the assistance of the Tarnished in retrieving the other half of the Cursemark, which she uses to gestate a Mending Rune that can embed the principle of Life in Death into Order. [ 8 ]
D, Beholder of Death , seeking revenge for his brother, D, kills Fia after she creates her Mending Rune.
Fia's questline ties into the questlines of several other NPCs, and is required in order to achieve the Age of the Duskborn ending.
One day, I'll be just like Uncle Alexander. And I'll have to leave the village to become a champion. - Jar-Bairn
Jar-Bairn is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Jar-Bairn is a young Living Jar who lives in the secluded village of Jarburg in Liurnia of the Lakes . Like his uncle Alexander , he is a warrior jar [ 1 ] , and strives to become a champion just like Alexander. [ 2 ]
Presently, however, he is on the lookout for a new Potentate for the village. He meets the Tarnished when they pay a visit to Jarburg, but determines that they are not suited to be the new Potentate due to their rough hands. [ 3 ] Nevertheless, he welcomes them to the village and invites them to come back and pick the flowers growing in the village whenever they want. [ 4 ] He also warns the Tarnished of poachers who hunt and destroy other living jars. [ 5 ]
Eventually, Jar-Bairn finds a new Potentate in Diallos Hoslow , a former Recusant who abandoned Volcano Manor after giving up on his path of revenge. [ 6 ] Despite his disappointment that Diallos is not as strong as the Tarnished, he admires his smooth hands. [ 7 ]
Not long after Diallos becomes Potentate, Jarburg is beset by poachers. Diallos defends the village and fights off the attackers, but many of the jars are broken [ 8 ] and Diallos himself succumbs to his wounds. Jar-Bairn vows to become a warrior like Diallos, so that he can protect everybody. [ 9 ] The Tarnished, having fought and defeated Alexander, offers the young jar his innards , which he uses to become even stronger, deciding to leave the village in search of glory, like his uncle. [ 10 ]
Jar-Bairn uses お兄ちゃん (older brother) when talking to male characters and お姉ちゃん (older sister) when talking to female characters. Both variations will be included on this page, written as お兄ちゃん / お姉ちゃん
Oh, a pleasure to see you, a pleasure indeed. I am Gowry. A great sage, in my day, anyway. - Sage Gowry
Sage Gowry is a merchant NPC in Elden Ring .
Gowry is an elderly sage dwelling in the blighted Caelid Wilds . When the Empyrean Malenia unleashed the Scarlet Rot during her battle with General Radahn , she permanently blighted Caelid. Since that day, Gowry has dedicated himself to her and the Order of Rot he hopes she will usher in. [ 1 ]
Gowry found Millicent and her sisters in the Swamp of Aeonia and raised them as his daughters. [ 2 ] Seeing them as buds [ 3 ] , he sent each of Millicent's sisters to the Haligtree in the hopes that they would bloom into scarlet valkyries. [ 4 ] [ 5 ]
Millicent became consumed by the Scarlet Rot, and was housed in a church, where she was worshipped by the Pests [ 6 ] . Gowry sought the aid of a Tarnished , offering to reveal to them the secret of the magical town of Sellia in exchange for their aid. [ 7 ] Gowry bids the Tarnished to journey deep into the Swamp of Aeonia to retrieve a needle of unalloyed gold, which could stem the effects of the Scarlet Rot. After the Tarnished retrieves the needle, Gowry shares the secret of the town, and asks them for another favor; to find Millicent and give her the needle.
Gowry avoids Millicent when she comes to visit his shack, later telling the Tarnished that she has no need of him anymore, and must embark on her fated journey. The Tarnished may aid Millicent on her journey, even giving her a prosthetic arm . Doing so will earn them Gowry's good will, who will offer to teach them a rot incantation, and reveal to them his allegiance to Malenia. [ 8 ]
As Millicent travels to the Haligtree , where Malenia awaits, she draws ever closer to her "sisters", who made the same journey as her. Gowry bids the Tarnished to aid the sisters in murdering Millicent, believing that a betrayal by someone she trusts so dearly will cause her to blossom into a flower [ 9 ] , which will be reborn as a scarlet valkyrie when Malenia ascends to godhood.
Should the Tarnished kill Millicent, they will return to Gowry's shack to find him seemingly dead. Should they instead aid Millicent against her sisters, she will prevail, but will remove the golden needle, willfully allowing herself to succumb to the Scarlet Rot. [ 10 ] The Tarnished may then find Gowry lamenting Millicent's decision, questioning whether she and Malenia detests him and the other children of rot so utterly. [ 11 ]
If the Tarnished attempts to kill Gowry, his body will transform into that of a Kindred of Rot . Upon returning to his shack, he will once again resume his human form, revealing that he can inhabit other pests to avoid death. [ 12 ]
Gowry's Bell Bearing
Ensha of the Royal Remains is an NPC in Elden Ring .
Ensha is the unspeaking adherent of Sir Gideon Ofnir , typically found leaning on the wall outside his master's study in Roundtable Hold . Ensha wears armour graced with golden human bones, which are said to have belonged to a soulless king, the lord of the lost and desperate, known as Ensha. [ 1 ]
After the Tarnished obtains one half of the Haligtree Secret Medallion, Ensha invades them in Roundtable Hold. After killing Ensha, the Tarnished confronts Gideon, who claims that Ensha got ahead of himself. [ 2 ] As an apology, Gideon furnishes the Tarnished with advice regarding the whereabouts of the medallion's other half. [ 3 ]
The stars are dark tonight. But rest assured, this is no ill omen. On the contrary. I believe that this portends a magnificent starry cascade. - Count Ymir
Count Ymir, High Priest , later known as the boss Ymir, Mother of Fingers , is a character in Shadow of the Erdtree .
Count Ymir is located at the Cathedral of Manus Metyr on the eastern Scadu Altus in the Realm of Shadow . He may be found sitting on his throne during the day but spends his nights in the attached graveyard visiting his son Yuri . Ymir offers cryptic guidance and items to aid those who seek their purpose. [ 1 ] He provides the player with a map to a hallowed ruin, claiming it holds the key to fate guided by the stars. [ 2 ]
Count Ymir is protected by his loyal Swordhands of Night : Jolán and her sister, Anna . [ 3 ]
Count Ymir was a master glintstone sorcerer renowned for his understanding of the cosmos. During the time of Elden Lord Godfrey , [ 4 ] [ 5 ] he served the Carian Royals and taught glintstone sorcery to Rellana, Twin Moon Knight . With a wizened hand gently gripping a glintstone , he often inspired his students, saying, "One need only envision the romance of the stars above with adoration for stardust in one's heart to become a great sorcerer. Do so, and you will know love." [ 6 ] [ 7 ] Although he originally held allegiance to the moons , he eventually dismissed them in his pursuit of deeper cosmic truths . [ 8 ] [ 9 ] [ 10 ]
Ymir uncovered secrets of the Greater Will during expedition into the hallowed Finger Ruins in the eastern Realm of Shadow . He studied the lamprey that dwelled within and mastered their Finger Sorcery , becoming a Finger-Weaver . [ 11 ] Below the Cathedral of Manus Metyr , he found the Finger Ruins of Miyr concealed the Finger Birthing Grounds , where Metyr waited in vain. [ 12 ]
Ymir learned that Metyr's true power and the guidance of the Two Fingers had been broken long ago. [ 12 ] [ 13 ] He became the high priest of Manus Metyr and acquired the service of the Swordhands of Night. After his child, Yuri , died at a tender age, Ymir's grief drove him to find a way to bring him back. [ 14 ] [ 15 ] He decided he would succeed Metyr as the next mother of Fingers. [ 16 ] He began ingesting Fingerprint Nostrum and birthing Fingercreepers of his own. [ 17 ] [ 18 ]
Ymir shares the wisdom of the cosmos and a Hole-Laden Necklace with the Tarnished champion . He directs them to sound the ominous hanging bells at the Finger Ruins of Dheo and Rhia . Once both bells are rung, Ymir reveals the location of the Ruins of Miyr. Ringing the third and final bell will leave one's fate guided by the stars—and face-to-face with Metyr. If the Mother of Fingers is defeated, Ymir's hope is rekindled but the prospect of achieving his dream drives him mad. [ 19 ] He achieves a partial transformation and fails to birth Yuri anew, instead creating more Fingercreepers. [ 20 ]
Count Ymir's questline is tied to that of Jolán, Swordhand of Night . Proceeding with certain quest stages may lock you out of any rewards.
Needle Knight Leda is an NPC in Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree .
The last member of the Needle Knights, an order devoted to Miquella of the Haligtree . [ 1 ] Leda was guided by Miquella to the Realm of Shadow alongside her compatriots [ 2 ] , all of whom were under the influence of a powerful charm which compelled them to follow the Empyrean. [ 3 ] While in the Realm of Shadow, Leda followed the trail of crosses left by Miquella, discovering in the process that he sought the Gate of Divinity, which was sealed away by a tree. [ 4 ]
The Tarnished encounters Leda in Mohgwyn Palace , where she urges them to touch the withered arm in Miquella's cocoon to enter the Realm of Shadow. Within the Land of Shadow, the Tarnished meets Leda and her various compatriots on their search for Miquella, seeking out the crosses to ascertain his route. However, the charm inflicted upon the compatriots is broken when Miquella's Great Rune is shattered. [ 5 ] Leda's devotion to Miquella is unshaken, but she begins to suspect her compatriots of disloyalty. [ 6 ] Leda sets about ferreting out those she believes undeserving of a place at Miquella's side [ 7 ] , with her potential targets being the Hornsent and Sir Ansbach . The Tarnished may assist her in her hunt, or side with her opponents.
After gaining access to Enir-Ilim , the Tarnished encounters Leda for a final time on the way to the Gate of Divinity. Leda deduces that the Tarnished was never guided by Miquella, and concludes that they were instead following the guidance of the Erdtree . [ 8 ] Viewing the Tarnished as a threat to Miquella's ascension, she challenges them. [ 9 ] The Tarnished triumphs over Leda and her remaining allies, and continues to the top of the tower.
Leda's Armor Oathseeker Knight Gauntlets Oathseeker Knight Greaves
Multilayered Ring of Light
1. Defeat both Starscourge Radahn and Mohg, Lord of Blood . Then rest on the nearest Site of Grace . Leda will appear in front of Miquella's cocoon at Mohgywn Dynasty Mausoleum and urge to interact with it.
2. Defeat the Divine Beast Dancing Lion , climb up the stairs in the adjacent room and collect the item on the top; a letter from Leda.
3. Defeat Rellana, Twin Moon Knight , Leda can be summoned for this fight. After the fight, you can find Leda again in the next Site of Grace.
4. Return to the same place and speak to Leda after visiting the entrance of the Shadow Keep .
5. Speaking with Leda and choose an option:
Rest on the site of grace and speak with Leda again after choosing an option.
6. (If she goes after Hornsent) you can find a summon signs in the Shadow Keep.
If Leda is helped, Hornsent will perish and reward the player with:
If Hornsent is helped, he can be summoned against Messmer and rewards you:
If nothing is done and Hornsent is summoned against Messmer, Leda will go after Ansbach.
7. She can be found at the Storehouse, First Floor where Sir Ansbach is.
If Leda is helped, Ansbach will perish and reward the player with:
If Ansbach is helped, he can be summoned on another fight and his questline contiunues.
If nothing is done, Ansbach can be summoned in future boss fights.
8. Regardless of any choices made, Leda will be finally found at Enir Ilim , where she will be waiting for a quick chat with the player.
He insists that he's nothing but a worn-down, over-the-hill soldier. But in his day, he was the feared commander of the Pureblood Knights, who cleaved open Miquella the Kind with his blood blade. - Needle Knight Leda
Sir Ansbach , also known as Pureblood Knight Ansbach , is a character in Shadow of the Erdtree
Formerly the feared commander of the Pureblood Knights [ 2 ] in service of Lord Mohg , Ansbach is one of the compatriots of Needle Knight Leda who followed Miquella into the Realm of Shadow . A wise old man, Ansbach has dedicated himself to investigating Miquella's purpose [ 3 ] by following the trail of crosses he left behind. [ 4 ]
As with the rest who followed Miquella into the Shadow Realm , Ansbach was under the influence of a charm , which breaks when the Empyrean abandons his Miquella's Great Rune . [ 5 ] With his mind free of the charm, Ansbach recalls that he once challenged Miquella in an attempt to free Mohg of his enchantment, which resulted in him falling under the enchantment himself. [ 6 ]
With his faculties restored, Ansbach makes his way to the Specimen Storehouse within the Shadow Keep . There, he learns that Mohg's body has been taken to Miquella [ 7 ] , and with the assistance of the Tarnished , discovers that Miquella intends to use Mohg's corpse as a vessel for his king consort. [ 8 ]
Ansbach becomes one of Needle Knight Leda 's possible targets [ 9 ] , resulting in a duel in which the Tarnished may intervene on either side. Should Ansbach survive Leda's attack, he will aid the Tarnished against Leda, Dryleaf Dane , and their allies in Enir-Ilim . Ansbach will then be available to assist the Tarnished in their battle against Promised Consort Radahn , before which he admits that he knows the Tarnished was responsible for killing Mohg, but bears no grudge against them, viewing Mohg's death as an honorable one. [ 10 ] After defeating Miquella and his consort, Ansbach dies before the Gate of Divinity .
Ansbach can be summoned for the following encounters:
Ansbach's Set is looted from [his body after completing his quest Enir-Ilim . It may also be obtained by helping Needle Knight Leda defeat Sir Ansbach at the Specimen Storehouse .

I am afraid I underestimated the lad. Appearing frail in both body and mind, I presumed he'd be like to stumble upon the field of battle... What a fool I was. - Sir Ansbach
Thiollier is an NPC merchant in Shadow of the Erdtree .
A Tarnished , [ 1 ] Thiollier was an isolated young man who encountered St. Trina , just once, and was granted the sweet repose of velvety sleep . The remainder of his days would be spent in search of the means to recapture it, despite Miquella 's enchantment . [ 2 ] [ 3 ] He views himself as utterly weak and useless, though he is, in secret, an expert in the realm of mixing poisons . [ 4 ] [ 5 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ] [ 8 ] He wears a mask with a tranquil sleeping face carved on it, its silver hair is arranged in the same style as St. Trina's, increasing arcane . [ 9 ] Additionally, he has sewn countless needles onto the exterior of his garb for a talismanic effect. [ 10 ] [ 11 ] [ 12 ]
Thiollier touched Miquella's withered arm at the Cocoon of the Empyrean and, alongside other followers of Miquella , entered the Realm of Shadow after the death of Mohg, Lord of Blood . [ 13 ] The player Tarnished can help Thiollier create a condensed, somniferous elixir, purported to be capable of putting even an ancient dragon to sleep, although fatal for any mortal. [ 14 ] [ 15 ] [ 16 ] [ 17 ] [ 18 ] Should his questline be completed, Thiollier can see St. Trina once more in the Garden of Deep Purple . [ 2 ] [ 19 ] [ 20 ] [ 21 ]
Thiollier sits by himself, quite some distance from his compatriots, at the Pillar Path Cross Site of Grace , located on the northeastern border of the Gravesite Plain . He later moves to the Garden of Deep Purple . Thiollier can be summoned as a cooperator against Putrescent Knight , Miquella's Followers , and Promised Consort Radahn .
Thiollier acts as a merchant and sells various items that hint at Trina's origin.
WARNING: Coming too close to the entrance of the Shadow Keep will lock you out of the first step of his quest, and you will miss the Spirit Ash of Ancient Dragon Florissax .
Redmane Freyja is an NPC in Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree .
Formerly one of the most distinguished knights of Starscourge Radahn , who invited her into his ranks after witnessing her valour as a gladiator [ 1 ] , Freyja is one of the compatriots of Needle Knight Leda who followed Miquella into the Realm of Shadow .
In the past, Freyja was stricken by Scarlet Rot in the Swamp of Aeonia . Left behind and resigned to death, she was approached by Miquella, who put his lips to her wound and drained the poison from it. [ 2 ] [ 3 ] Freyja was subsequently charmed by Miquella, and later entered the Realm of Shadow with Leda and her compatriots.
After Miquella's charm is broken, Freyja chooses to strike out on her own, although she remains loyal to Miquella. [ 4 ] She recalls Miquella mentioning a vow he once made with her former lord Radahn, and resolves to learn the nature of the vow. [ 5 ] To this end, she travels to the Shadow Keep , where she has difficulty reading the letters etched into the stone tablets. [ 6 ] With assistance from the The Tarnished and Sir Ansbach , Freyja learns that Miquella wishes to revive the soul of General Radahn. Freyja welcomes this, believing that endless war would suit her former master better than an honourable death. [ 7 ]
Later, Freyja joins Leda and Dryleaf Dane in Enir-Ilim , in their fight against the Tarnished. Upon her defeat, she praises the Tarnished for honoring her with a glorious end. [ 8 ]
I like finding things. For you, Lady Leda, her allies, and the forager brood. Things bring joy to all. - Moore
Sir Moore is a merchant NPC in Shadow of the Erdtree . He likes collecting things and will share and sell goods with the Tarnished and the other followers of Miquella . He is initially located at the Main Gate Cross Site of Grace outside Belurat, Tower Settlement in the Realm of Shadow .
Moore was once a pest who awaited the return of the goddess of the Scarlet Rot . [ 1 ] When her successor, Malenia , disowned and abandoned the pests, Moore and his forager brood were left without a master. He and his kin later allied with Miquella and joined his followers . The brood shared their scavenged items with Moore and his comrades out of kindness. [ 2 ] [ 3 ]

Horns are sublime artifacts to hornsent, and their presence confirms the belief that they are a chosen people. Only the repeated sprouting of fresh horns can create a tangled horn, which is viewed as an irrefutable symbol of primacy. - Clarifying Horn Charm +2
The Hornsent (角人, Tsunobito , lit. "Horned People") are a faction in Shadow of the Erdtree .
The Hornsent were a polytheistic, deeply ascetic people who associated the spiral , the Crucible , and their tangled horns with the divine . [ 1 ] They have lived in Belurat and the Land of the Tower since times of old, and constructed the spiral tower, Enir-Ilim .
The Hornsent held a great knowledge about multiple Outer Gods and seemingly integrated different divine powers into their culture. They were aware of the Formless Mother [ 2 ] and Shadow Undead at the Abandoned Ailing Village cast Swarm of Flies , an incantation associated with the Formless Mother. They used Rot for purification rituals through Romina, Saint of the Bud [ 3 ] and kept Gravebirds inside Belurat and Enir-Ilim, golems crafted as kindreds to the Deathbirds [ 4 ] . They were also aware of the Fell God of fire that was part of their legends [ 5 ] . The hornsent butchered undesirables and stuffed them into jars . They conducted a divine ritual to rebirth the jar contents as better people. [ 6 ] [ 7 ] [ 8 ] [ 9 ]
Queen Marika betrayed hornsent. [ 10 ] [ 11 ] . Their tower and its Divine Gate was sealed by shadow [ 12 ] and their lands hidden in the Realm of Shadow . The hornsent were later attacked by forces of the Erdtree led by Messmer , son of Marika. His flame burned their armies and settlements. [ 13 ] [ 14 ] Those who survived bore a deep grudge or swore vengeance. [ 15 ] [ 16 ]
Dane is a member of the Dryleaf Sect , an order of spiritual seekers who chose to serve a new god after seeing the decline of the Erdtree in the fallen leaves. [ 1 ] Dane fights using an unarmed technique which focuses on kicks. [ 2 ]
Dane is a compatriot of Needle Knight Leda , and has been in the service of Miquella even longer than she has. [ 3 ] He seldom speaks, and even Leda has never heard his voice. [ 4 ] The The Tarnished may challenge him to a duel in Scadu Altus [ 5 ] , after which he will grant them access to Dryleaf Arts .
Dane discovers the sealing tree in the Ancient Ruins of Rauh and deduces that it must be burnt using the flame of Messmer the Impaler . [ 6 ] After it has been burnt, Dane joins Leda in Enir-Ilim , where they face off against the Tarnished. Upon his defeat he finally breaks his silence, offering a plea for Miquella to rise to godhood. [ 7 ]
The demesne of Limgrave, far south of the Erdtree, is bordered to the northwest by the cliffs of Stormveil, and under its ever-clouded skies roll the great steppes of the pale lands. - Map: Limgrave, West
Limgrave is a region of the Lands Between in Elden Ring .
Map of Limgrave
Limgrave is located in the southwestern corner of the Lands Between. A temperate land of green plains and golden trees, with windswept hills to the north and a dense, mist-shrouded woodland to the east. To the south lies the Weeping Peninsula , an isolated region known for its unceasing rain. Godrick the Grafted presides over Limgrave from Stormveil Castle , to the northwest, and to the northeast lies the region of Caelid .
Godrick the Grafted
Upon the cliff, in Castle Stormveil, is a shardbearer. A demigod who inherited a fragment of the shattered Elden Ring. - Melina — [[ Elden Ring ]]
Stormveil Castle is a legacy dungeon located in Limgrave .
Map of Stormveil
Stormveil Castle perches atop a cliff overlooking Limgrave. Currently, it is the stronghold of the Demigod Godrick the Grafted, but long ago it was ruled over by an old king, back when the true storm raged. [ 1 ] The castle is heavily guarded and patrolled by Banished Knights, Exile Soldiers, and warhawks with blades grafted to their talons. [ 2 ] The exterior of the castle is mottled with craters lined with thorns, which have also spread to the soldiers within. It is said that the source may be hidden deep within the castle. [ 3 ]
The majority of Liurnia, known for its vast forests and ever-present fog, is sinking into a lake. - Map: Liurnia, West
Liurnia of the Lakes , also known as Liurnia , is a region in Elden Ring .
Map of Liurnia
Liurnia is the westernmost region of the Lands Between . Characterized by its vast forests, sheer cliffs, and ever-present fog, the majority of the region is sinking into a lake. On the eastern side, the Bellum Highway runs north to south, connecting the area to the regions of Altus Plateau and Limgrave . The western coast is closely associated with the Carian royal family , and this is where their Manor stands. The Academy of Raya Lucaria rises above the lake in the center of the region, at a junction between two highroads, with the Academy Gate Town spreading around it, slowly disappearing into the waters. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
The Moonlight Altar , a high plateau at the southern point, obscures the Village of the Albinaurics and its surrounding poisonous lake on the overworld map . It can only be accessed via an elevator located past the Grand Cloister deep underground, guarded by Astel, Naturalborn of the Void .
The Academy of Raya Lucaria is a both a faction , and a legacy dungeon located in Liurnia of the Lakes .
Map of Raya Lucaria
The Academy of Raya Lucaria sits on a plateau in the middle of the great lake of Liurnia, and is the place of study for glintstone sorcerers of the Lands Between . [ 1 ] This area is accessed by using an Academy Glintstone Key to pass through either of the two gates marked with the blue seal .
The Academy offers everything from basic training in sorcerery to advanced, specialized study. Higher learning is accessible to only noteworthy scholars, who are then permitted to don stone Glintstone Crowns , modeled after notable sorcerers in their chosen conspectus . [ 2 ] Azur and Lusat , regarded as founding glintstone sorcerers, founded the Karolos and Olivinus Conspectuses, respectively. [ 3 ] The majority of Glintstone Crown sorcerers found within the Academy pursue one of these two founding conspectuses.
Bell-shaped glintstone sigil of the academy depicts twin Cuckoos watching a mass of glintstone [ 4 ]
The founding of the Academy of Raya Lucaria was credited to the primeval sorcerers Azur and Lusat. [ 3 ] Their study of the Primeval Current shook the academy when they began to transfigure fledgling sorcerers into Graven Masses —the seeds of stars. [ 5 ]
Long ago, Rennala charmed the Academy with her lunar magic. She became the Academy's master and established the house of Caria as royalty. [ 6 ] When Rennala assumed governorship over the Academy, she heavily limited the study of the primeval current due the dangers it presented and subsequently exiled Azur and Lusat. This change outraged Sorceress Sellen , who began to transform her peers into Graven Schools. [ 7 ] Though the Academy expelled Sellen and denounced her methods, they shared her core sentiment, and their thirst for knowledge would eventually lead to the downfall of the Carians influence over the Academy.
The combined forces of the Knights of the Cuckoo: the Cuckoo Knights , the Raya Lucaria Soldiers and their Foot Soldiers were hired by the Academy at some point. As payment for their service, the Academy taught them martial Glintstone techniques like Scholar's Armament and Scholar's Shield . The design of the Cuckoo bird upon their armor is mused to represent the Cuckoo's refusal to be mere servants of the Academy. The Cuckoo were given free reign to wage war as they pleased by the Academy, and became known for their rapacious ways.
When Rennala's husband Radagon left her to become the second Elden Lord , Rennala's heart went with him. [ 8 ] With Rennala a grieving shell of her former self, the Academy then realised that she was no champion after all. [ 9 ] She still clutches the amber egg given to her by Radagon, which contains the Great Rune of the Unborn . [ 10 ] No longer in any state to defend herself, the Academy took the opportunity to lock Rennala in their Grand Library and staged a rebellion against the Carians, so that they could pursue unlimited study once more. The resulting conflict between the Acadamy's forces, and those of the Carians, waged across Liurnia, becoming an effective Liurnian civil war . Ultimately, the Acadamy would achieve their goals. Without their queen, and her successors absent, the Carians fell into decline, and their influence in the Academy's policies dissipated.
After the Shattering of the Elden Ring , the Academy declared neutrality in the ensuing war and cast repelling seals upon its entrances, blocking outside access to anyone not in possession of a Academy Glintstone Key . [ 11 ] Such a key may be found on an island west of the Academy, guarded by Glintstone Dragon Smarag .
There are four Sites of Grace in the Academy of Raya Lucaria:
Caelid, known as the locale of the last battle between General Radahn and Malenia, Blade of Miquella, is a vast land consummately marred by scarlet rot. - Map: Caelid
Caelid is a region in Elden Ring .
Map of Caelid
A wasteland on the southeastern tip of the Lands Between , plagued by Scarlet Rot and inhabited by all manner of malformed creatures. Caelid was the site of the Battle of Aeonia between General Radahn and Malenia, Blade of Miquella , during which the first flower of Aeonia bloomed and covered the region in Scarlet Rot. Radahn's army, the Redmanes , continue to combat the rot using fire to this day. The region is lined by smoldering walls and dotted with colossal remains .
A fortress on an island to the south of Caelid , connected to the mainland by a heavily fortified greatbridge. The castle is the stronghold of General Radahn 's army, beaten yet unbowed after their defeat at the hands of Malenia and her Cleanrot Knights .
Redmane Castle is also the site of the Radahn Festival; a contest in which great champions attempt to defeat the Rot-maddened Radahn and claim his Great Rune . This event is initiated either by activating a Site of Grace in Altus Plateau or by progressing Ranni the Witch 's questline.
During the Radahn Festival, all of the enemies in the castle (except for the two Elder Lions) will disappear, and the boss (if not defeated already) will not show up in the plaza. Once Starscourge Radahn has been defeated, the enemies will return and the boss can be fought if not defeated already.
Altus Plateau is a region in Elden Ring .
Map of Altus
The Altus Plateau is a northwestern region of the Lands Between . It is a region of great significance, for it is here that the Erdtree can be found, as well as Leyndell , the royal capital of Queen Marika . Altus borders Liurnia of the Lakes to the south, and the Forbidden Lands which lead to the Mountaintops of the Giants to the east. Due to its high elevation, Altus is connected to its neighbouring regions primarily through two lifts; the Grand Lift of Dectus to the south and the Grand Lift of Rold to the east. There is another, more dangerous path to Liurnia that goes through the mountains separating the two regions.
Altus is a lush and verdant land, once over-flowing with the bounty of the Erdtree itself. Most of the vegetation that grows in Altus is tinged with the gold of the Erdtree, and flowers that grow on the plateau are prized reagents by Perfumers. The people of the plateau believed that those born at the foot of the Erdtree, like themselves, were blessed. While still beautiful, the land is marred by scars from the Shattering , left over from the many battles waged here. The land is dotted by ruined battlefields and soldier's camps.
The western parts of Altus are mountainous and dominated by the volcanic Mt. Gelmir . At the top of the mountain lies the Volcano Manor , home to the demigod Praetor Rykard . At the foot of the mountain lies bubbling geysers as well as a village of Demihumans.
In the north of Altus, through a deep canyon, lies the Shaded Castle , ancient manor of the Marais family who served as both executioners and castellans of the Shaded Castle for generations. The castle lies in disrepair, haunted by Wraith-Callers and Revenants, and with most of its courtyard sinking into a poison swamp.
The eastern parts of Altus are dominated by Leyndell , Queen Marika's royal capital, built at the foot of the Erdtree . Two primary paths lead into the capital grounds; one from the southwest and one from the northwest. The southwestern path is the main road, a well-maintained and well-guarded highway gloriously decorated with statues of Queen Marika's soldiers. The capital grounds are defended by double ramparts. Within the outer wall, to the northeast, lies a Minor Erdtree. Just outside the outer wall, on an outcropping north of the southwestern highway, lies the Giant-Conquering Hero's Grave , final resting place of a hero who fought against the Giants.
The inner wall of the capital is surrounded by a moat, which appears to have mostly dried out, as its waters are now shallow. Within the inner walls, the Royal Capital is bounded by a lake, which serves as yet another layer of protection. The capital is ruled by the Demigod Morgott , known also as the Veiled Monarch.
Journey to the capital Leyndell, to the east of the Altus Plateau, at the foot of the Erdtree. The Two Fingers will deny your passage no longer. You may be our best hope. Find your way to the Elden Ring. - Gideon Ofnir
Leyndell, Royal Capital is a legacy dungeon on the Altus Plateau in Elden Ring . This area is revealed on the map by collecting Map: Leyndell, Royal Capital .
Map of Leyndell
Leyndell, Royal Capital sits at the foot of the Erdtree on Altus Plateau . It is connected to the Capital Outskirts , Forbidden Lands , and Subterranean Shunning-Grounds . The city is enclosed by double ramparts, [ 1 ] with the city proper contained within the inner wall. The current lord of Leyndell is Morgott the Grace-Given , [ 2 ] a Demigod of the Golden Lineage, [ 3 ] who took it upon himself to become the Erdtree's protector, despite being born a graceless Omen . [ 4 ]
Long ago, the city was assaulted by the colossal Ancient Dragon Gransax - the only time in recorded history that Leyndell's walls have fallen. This marked the dawn of the War of the Ancient Dragons . [ 5 ] The bloody conflict came to an end when Godwyn the Golden befriended the dread Fortissax , [ 6 ] an event which gave rise to the capital's Ancient Dragon Cult . [ 7 ] Gransax's corpse can still be found towering over much of the city.
The Fortified Manor , in the southwestern portion of the city, is a perfect likeness of the Roundtable Hold . In its heyday, the manor was the headquarters of the Two Fingers and the warriors of Elden Lord Godfrey . [ 8 ] Unlike the Table of Lost Grace , where Tarnished champions gather, the Fortified Manor is completely abandoned.
Far below the city is the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds , a network of sewers and waterways inhabited by the Omen . The Leyndell Catacombs also branch off from this underground realm. Even further below lies the Cathedral of the Forsaken , where the Great Caravan of nomadic merchants were entombed so as to bury the Madness that followed them. [ 9 ] In their underground prison they chanted a curse of despair, summoning the Frenzied Flame . [ 10 ]
The Elden Throne sits beneath the Erdtree, in the south-eastern area of the city. It is here that Morgott stands guard, determined to protect the Erdtree from would-be champions.
Leyndell contains the following Landmarks and Locations :
Mt. Gelmir, which houses the Volcano Manor at its summit, is characterized by sheer cliffs and ominous skies. These qualities only became more pronounced after the Shattering. - Map: Mt. Gelmir
Mt. Gelmir is a subregion in Elden Ring , located on the Altus Plateau .
A volcano in western Altus Plateau , which houses the Volcano Manor at its summit. It is characterized by sheer cliffs and ominous skies, qualities which grew more pronounced in the wake of The Shattering .
The dried-up Seethewater River runs along the base of the volcano, with geysers that spew jets of boiling water. The river terminates on the west side, near Fort Laiedd where the forces of Leyndell are locked in conflict with the Fire Monks . The Hermit Village , inhabited by Demi-Humans and Glintstone Sorcerers , sits on the southeastern edge of the volcano. Primeval Sorcerer Azur , one of the founding Glintstone Sorcerers, settled near the village after his banishment from the Academy of Raya Lucaria .
Mt. Gelmir was the site of the most horrendous conflict of the Shattering, which has left scars that can still be found. Ruined campsites litter the cliffsides. Some Leyndell Soldiers remain, driven to frenzy by the horrors they saw.
The Volcano Manor , which sits atop the mountain, is the home of the Demigod Praetor Rykard , who once led a company of inquisitors. After the Elden Ring was broken, Rykard fed himself to the blasphemous serpent , Great Rune and all, in defiance of the gods . His knights abandoned him when his noble ambitions were reduced to gluttony and depravity, yet his consort, Tanith , remained by his side. Rykard is now served by the Recusants ; a band of Tarnished who hunt their own kind.
The Volcano Manor (火山館, Kazan-kan ) is a subregion in Elden Ring . It is a legacy dungeon located on Mt. Gelmir .
Map of Volcano Manor
During the Shattering , the Volcano Manor was the home of Praetor Rykard and his Recusant , fierce warriors who waged war against the Erdtree . Following Rykard's transformation into the Lord of Blasphemy, the remaining Recusants deserted him and left the Volcano Manor. Afterwards, Rykard's consort, Lady Tanith , continued to maintain the Manor as the base of operations for a new generation of Recusants. After their return to the Lands Between , Tarnished considered strong and merciless towards their kin, were extended invitations to join the Volcano Manor and are given contracts to hunt other Tarnished in service of the Roundtable. Tarnished who prove themselves are offered an audience with what has become of Praetor Rykard, the Lord of Blasphemy, which will inevitably end with the serpentine demigod devouring them for their strength.
Even after the Shattering, the Volcano Manor is still besieged by the forces of the Royal Capital . Camps of Leyndell soliders dot the perilous assent of Mt. Gelmir.
The Volcano Manor is one of the game's most complex locations. It can be reached in multiple ways and you can progress through from different directions.
The fastest, but most gimmicky way to reach it is by letting the Abductor Virgin at the bottom of the Raya Lucaria Academy grapple you to death. You will still drop your runes, but be respawned right within the Volcano Manor area. From here there are two paths that are each a point of no return. One leading to the rest of the manor, the other brings you to the Abductor Virgin duo bossfight and back to the Altus Plateau . For the Abductor Virgin boss, search for the cave with multiple drop-down platforms. To progress deeper into the manor, jump down the lava waterfall. If you die here before reaching a grace, you will be respawned where the Abductor Virgin dropped you within Volcano Manor. From here you can explore the area, defeat the Godskin Noble and either make it back to the manor entrance with Lady Tanith and the other npcs, or skip their quests and head straight to the gateway portal leading to Praetor Rykard .
The regular paths to enter the manor are either on foot/horseback across Mt. Gelmir , or to be teleported right to the Volcano Manor entrance grace by Rya once reaching the Altus Plateau . You won't be able to reach the bosses or explore the rest of the area from here unless you accept Lady Tanith's offer to get the Drawing-Room Key . If you join the manor, a list of NPCs become available there: Bernahl , Patches , Rya , Diallos Hoslow . To get all the content out of the manor, you have to wait with fighting Rykard until reaching the Mountaintops of the Giants , so that you can do all of the following NPC invasions for the manor: Old Knight Istvan , Rileigh the Idle, Great Horned Tragoth , Vargram the Raging Wolf + Errant Sorcerer Wilhelm, Juno Hoslow, Knight of Blood . After defeating Juno Hoslow, Tanith offers to send you to Rykard, where you can then start the boss fight. Remember to complete Rya 's quest before defeating Juno Hoslow, Knight of Blood , otherwise you'll be locked out of Tanith 's dialogue regarding Rya.
Mountaintops of the Giants is a region in Elden Ring .
Map of the Mountaintops
The northern Mountaintops were once the home of the Fire Giants , after they claimed them from the Ice Dragons . At the birth of the Erdtree , the forces of Queen Marika the Eternal and Godfrey, First Elden Lord marched up the mountain and put the Giants to the sword. With the Giants defeated, the Flame of Ruin was confined within the Giants' Forge atop the mount, and the Age of the Erdtree began.
The Fire Monks , who were left behind to watch over the Flame of Ruin, can be found patrolling the region. They are often accompanied by the Guilty : thorn sorcerers who were banished to the north. Their fortress, the Guardians' Garrison , sits on the eastern side of the mountain.
The Zamor Ruins in the southwest are the home of an ancient clan of Zamor Warriors . They were ancient enemies of the Fire Giants, and are regarded as heroes due to their actions in the War Against the Giants .
The Mountaintops were also home to the astrologers , neighbors of the Giants and predecessors to the modern Glintstone Sorcerers . The ruins of their civilization can be found in the central Mountaintops.
The northernmost section of the Mountaintops is dominated by Castle Sol , where the site of an eclipse once inspired dreadful awe. Half of a medallion that will grant access to Miquella's Haligtree can be found here, protected by Commander Niall .
The medallion can be used at the Grand Lift of Rold to gain access to the Consecrated Snowfield , which sprawls to the west of the Mountaintops. The Albinaurics , and others who revere Miquella , seek this sacred land in the hopes of earning the Empyrean 's favour. Ordina, Liturgical Town is the final stop on the way to the Haligtree, and is home to several Albinauric Archers .
It is said that the ancient royal city of Farum Azula has been slowly crumbling since time immemorial. - Old Lord's Talisman
Crumbling Farum Azula is a subregion of the Lands Between in Elden Ring . This legacy dungeon is accessible after burning the Erdtree at the Forge of the Giants found on Flame Peak in the Mountaintops of the Giants .
Map of Farum Azula
Farum Azula is a giant temple in the sky, located above the sea to the east of the Lands Between . Once a royal city of the Ancient Dragons and the seat of the Dragonlord Placidusax , Farum Azula has been crumbling since time immemorial. [ 1 ] Now, all that remains is a mausoleum guarded by chosen Beastmen , who wield weapons clad in Red Lightning . [ 2 ] The storm beyond time rages in the center of the crumbling city, and at its heart is the Dragonlord's seat, where he awaits the return of his god . [ 3 ]
In Farum Azula, many Ancient Dragons can be found buried in the rock, between the catacombs of the Beastmen and the surface of the city, their bodies still filled with gold. [ 4 ] It is said that they formed a living wall of rock to protect the Dragonlord long ago. [ 5 ]
As well as Beastmen, Farum Azula is still home to a number of Ancient Dragons , who roost on the floating fragments of the city. There is also a population of Wormfaces dwelling in one of the lower levels of the city. It appears that Deathroot has spread throughout parts of the city as well.
Farum Azula is the dwelling place of Maliketh, the Black Blade , the protector of the Rune of Death . It is here that the Tarnished finds themselves after the Erdtree is set aflame, and where they finally unbind the Rune of Death, releasing it upon the Lands Between.
Crumbling Farum Azula Sites of Grace
Miquella's Haligtree (ミケラの聖樹, Mikera no Seiju ) is a legacy dungeon located north of the Consecrated Snowfield . It is accessible after solving the puzzle in the Evergaol at Ordina, Liturgical Town and taking the Sending Gate .
Map of the Haligtree
Miquella 's Haligtree is a vast, misshapen tree in the far north of the Lands Between . [ 1 ] Built into the canopy is Haligtree Town , a sanctuary for the unwanted. At the base of the tree is Elphael, Brace of the Haligtree , a city largely inhabited by the Haligtree Knights and Cleanrot Knights who serve Miquella and Malenia . Both areas contain statues of the twin Demigods .
Long ago, the Empyrean Miquella abandoned Golden Order Fundamentalism after realizing it could not treat Malenia 's Scarlet Rot . [ 2 ] He sought to establish an Unalloyed Gold order away from the Erdtree and settled on the Haligtree. [ 1 ] Miquella watered the sapling with his own Empyrean blood, and later wove a cocoon and embedded himself within its trunk to nurture it directly. [ 3 ] However, it would fail to grow into an Erdtree . Before he could finish, Miquella was cut and taken from the tree by Mohg , [ 4 ] who was under his charm. The Lord of Blood zealously wished to raise the Empyrean to godhood and become his consort. [ 5 ] After returning from her battle with Radahn , Malenia awaited her brother's return at the base of the tree, [ 6 ] and over time infected the tree with her Scarlet Rot.
Nevertheless, the Haligtree and its city became a haven for those rejected by society, such as the Misbegotten and the Kindred of Rot . Loretta , a former Knight of Caria , founded a sanctuary for Albinaurics among the boughs of the Haligtree. [ 7 ] [ 8 ] Those who made the pilgrimage presented a secret medallion at the Grand Lift of Rold to gain access to the Consecrated Snowfield. They traveled north and crossed the river to Ordina, Liturgical Town, where they journeyed through a Sending Gate. [ 9 ] [ 10 ]
Category;Subregions
Elphael, Brace of the Haligtree is a legacy dungeon in Elden Ring . It is accessible after defeating Loretta, Knight of the Haligtree in Miquella's Haligtree .
It is an optional endgame locations that can only be reached by descending from Miquella's Haligtree , past Loretta, Knight of the Haligtree . The boss at the end of this area is Malenia, Blade of Miquella .
There are five Sites of Grace in Elphael:
In the lightless depths lies the grave of an ancient civilization. It is here Mohg, the Lord of Blood, is building his palace, to be the seat of his coming dynasty named Mohgwyn. And whatever nightmares that may bring. - Map Mohgwyn Palace
The Mohgwyn Palace is a subregion in Elden Ring . It is located on an island in the Siofra River .
An island in the underground Siofra River, far to the east of Nokron, Eternal City . The grave of an ancient dynasty civilization can be found here, and it is in these ruins that Mohg, Lord of Blood , has chosen to be the seat of his coming Mohgwyn Dynasty . [ 1 ]
A large part of the area is taken up by a blood -red lake, which is the habitat of many abominations. The Mohgwyn Dynasty Mausoleum juts out of the west side of the island, housing the Lord of Blood and his vassals.
There are two possible entrances to this area. The conventional route is via a sending gate on the western edge of Consecrated Snowfield , which leads to a cliff on the southeastern side of the palace. Alternately, by becoming a Pureblood Knight of the Mohgwyn Dynasty, one can obtain a Pureblood Knight's Medal from White Mask Varré , which will teleport the player to the mausoleum entrance at will.
Descend underground where the fallen star struck Limgrave. And make it yours. The precious treasure of Nokron. - War Counselor Iji
Nokron, Eternal City is a subregion in Elden Ring , located along the Siofra River .
Nokron is one of the Eternal Cities of the Nox , who were banished underground after invoking the ire of the Greater Will . [ 1 ] Nokron's chair-crypt houses the Fingerslayer Blade , a blood-drenched fetish made from a corpse that can harm the Greater Will and its vassals, and is proof of the treason of the Nox. [ 2 ]
Nokron is notably difficult to access. Long ago, a band of slaves-turned-soldiers called the Fallen Hawks were ordered to explore the Eternal Cities. [ 3 ] Although they managed to find their way into the subterranean realm, they became trapped after they discovered the Ghostflame . [ 4 ] While the city is visible from the lower portion of Siofra River, the route to it is only opened after Starscourge Radahn is defeated, which causes a star to fall upon Limgrave , opening a deep crater near Fort Haight .
Nokstella, Eternal City is a subregion of the Ainsel River in Elden Ring .
Nokstella is one of the Eternal Cities inhabited by the Nox , who were banished underground after invoking the ire of the Greater Will . [ 1 ] It is located in the Ainsel River Main , on the west side of the underground river, and can only be accessed by using the Sending Gate in Renna's Rise and following the path through the northern Uhl Palace Ruins .
The lost Black Moon of Nokstella was once the guide to countless stars , and a talisman made in its image was regarded as the treasure of the city. [ 2 ]
At the very depths of the Erdtree's majestic roots lies the source of the Ainsel and the Siofra rivers. Here too begins the network of Greattree roots that spread throughout the Lands Between. - Map: Deeproot Depths
The Deeproot Depths is an underground region of the Lands Between in Elden Ring . This area of the map is revealed by collecting Map: Deeproot Depths .
Map of the Deeproot Depths
The Deeproot Depths is an enormous cavern deep below the Altus Plateau . It is the source of the Ainsel and Siofra Rivers , and the furthest downward the Erdtree roots extend. The network of Greattree roots that spread throughout the Lands Between also begins here. [ 1 ]
Below the Prince of Death's Throne , a nameless Eternal City lies in ruins , with many of its buildings sinking into a mire of milky liquid. In the northwestern area, a Wandering Mausoleum prowls, surrounded by Mausoleum Soldiers and Knights . To the far west, Siluria , one of the two leaders of the Crucible Knights, awaits at the hollowed-out trunk of a dead oak tree.
The Nameless Eternal City was destroyed by Astel, Naturalborn of the Void long ago. [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
After Godwyn the Golden was murdered on the Night of Black Knives , his body was buried in the Erdtree's roots. [ 4 ] His malformed body, corrupted by Death, can be found to the north of the cavern. It is here that Fia resides after fleeing Roundtable Hold .
This area can be reached by either defeating the Valiant Gargoyle duo boss in Siofra Aqueduct or by finding an illusory wall at the bottom of the Frenzied Flame Proscription , found behind a movable wall guarded by Mohg, the Omen at the bottom of the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds .
An abandoned coffin found along the southwestern shore of the shallow body of water allows travel to Ainsel River Main , the northern part of Ainsel River .
