Lake of Rot (腐れ湖) is a subregion located downstream of the Ainsel River .
The Lake of Rot is a large cavernous area beneath Liurnia of the Lakes filled with rotting waters. The lake itself is littered with the crumbling remnants of an ancient dynasty . Within the center of the Lake of Rot are obelisks with stone pressure plates that when activated, raise platforms from beneath the lake, creating a pathway. In the southern part of this area, the Grand Cloister is found; a large walkway infested with rotted-flora and fauna.
The divine essence of an Outer God is sealed away in this lake [ 1 ] , after it was defeated by a blind swordsman with a flowing sword . [ 2 ] The Servants of Rot have a presence here, [ 3 ] as a Mushroom Crown is found in the lake and the Kindred of Rot populate the Grand Cloiser.
The Land of Shadow. A place obscured by the Erdtree. Where the goddess Marika first set foot.
The Realm of Shadow (影の地, Kage no Chi ), also known as the Shadow Realm and the Land of Shadow , is the setting of the DLC expansion for Elden Ring , Shadow of the Erdtree .
All manner of death washes ashore in the Realm of Shadow, a veiled region blessed by the twisted Scadutree —the shadow of the golden Erdtree . [ 1 ] These somber lands are—or once were—the very heart of the Lands Between and the origin of the Crucible . [ 2 ] [ 3 ] [ 4 ] They were the domain of the hornsent , a people who worship the Crucible for the tangled horns it had blessed them with. [ 5 ] It is also where the Empyrean Marika ascended to godhood and later buried her secrets. [citation needed]
Long ago, before the Shattering and the reign of Elden Lord Radagon , [ 6 ] the Realm of Shadow was engulfed in flames during a brutal Crusade led by Messmer the Impaler and his army , acting on the orders of Queen Marika. [ 7 ] The purge aimed to eradicate the hornsent, [ 8 ] [ 9 ] [ 10 ] who lacked the light of Erdtree's grace . [ 11 ] [ 12 ] Eventually, Marika severed all ties with Messmer, shrouding the Land of Shadow beneath the Scadutree to conceal all evidence of her sins. [ 13 ]
The Land of Shadow is the place to which Miquella the Kind departed, divesting himself of his flesh, his strength, his lineage, and all things golden. [citation needed] To access this hidden realm, one must defeat both Starscourge Radahn and Mohg, Lord of Blood , then touch Miquella’s withered arm at the Cocoon of the Empyrean atop the Mohgwyn Dynasty Mausoleum in the subterranean Siofra River .
When the Impaler's army assailed the tower, the ritual of the lion dance was turned toward martial ends—its divinity, its fury, its light-footed beauty. - Remembrance of the Dancing Lion
The Belurat, Tower Settlement is a legacy dungeon in the Realm of Shadow in Shadow of the Erdtree . This area of the map is revealed by Map: Gravesite Plain .
Belurat is a hornsent settlement built at the base of the tower of Enir-Ilim . It is found on the Gravesite Plain , in the Land of the Tower to the west of Castle Ensis . An old lion dance festival was held here in honor of the Divine Beast . [ 1 ] This area was devasted by the army of Messmer the Impaler during the crusade . [ 2 ] [ 3 ] A Sealing Tree veils the tower—and its Gate of Divinity —in shadow.
O tower of ours, hidden in shadow. O lofty spiral piercing the heavens. Lead him safely unto greater Godhood. And in divinity grant our salvation. - Stranded Soul
Enir-Ilim is a subregion of the Realm of Shadow in Shadow of the Erdtree .
Enir-Ilim, the sacred tower of the hornsent , has been shrouded in shadow. It is located on the Gravesite Plain , attached to Belurat, Tower Settlement .
This legacy dungeon is accessible after using Messmer's Kindling to burn the Sealing Tree at the Church of the Bud in the Ancient Ruins of Rauh . Once unsealed, it can also be reached by climbing the ladder in the Divine Beast Theatre .
The peninsula, to Limgrave's south, is named for its unceasing rainfall, redolent of lament. - Map: Weeping Peninsula
The Weeping Peninsula is a subregion located to the south of Limgrave in Elden Ring .
Map of the Weeping Peninsula
The Weeping Peninsula is a crescent-shaped landmass at the southernmost tip of the Lands Between . It is named for its unceasing rainfall, which gives the impression of a land in perpetual lament. [ 1 ] The landscape is marked by steep cliffs, deep ravines, poison swamps, and a mournful atmosphere.
To the northeast, the Bridge of Sacrifice connects the peninsula to Limgrave proper. A Rosus Statue overlooks the bridge from the east, guiding the dead to the Impaler's Catacombs on the northeastern shore. Nearby, the Forest Lookout Tower monitors the Demi-Human Forest Ruins , and south of Rosus lies both an area struck by starfall and the sorcerous Oridys's Rise .
At the center of the peninsula is a plateau dominated by a minor Erdtree and Radagon 's Church of Pilgrimage . The area is home to a Erdtree Guardians and Miranda Blossoms . Rows of ancient black stone ruins flank the plateau, while fallen ruins are embedded in the earth throughout the region.
West of the plateau is Tombsward , where a Wandering Mausoleum tolling solemnly on the plain. This area, and the Fourth Church of Marika , are guarded by a group of Mausoleum Soldiers . A large number of Putrid Corpses aimlessly wander the littered western beach. The Tower of Return rises from the southwest, offering safe passage to the base of Erdtree . [ 2 ] [ 3 ]
The south is home to Castle Morne, located at the peninsula’s southernmost tip. The road to the castle passes through a demolished stone rampart before reaching its gates. Castle Morne was once the site of a storied battle between a lone revenger and Godfrey, First Elden Lord . Today, it is under the stewardship of Castellan Edgar , appointed by Godrick the Grafted . However, the castle has fallen into disarray following a revolt by its Misbegotten workers.
The storied sword of Castle Morne. A revenger's weapon, it is burdened with oceans of anger and regret. - Grafted Blade Greatsword
Castle Morne is a location in Elden Ring . Found at the southernmost point in the Lands Between , it overlooks the southeastern shore of the Weeping Peninsula .
Castle Morne once belonged to the Stormveil faction that later fell to the Erdtree long ago. A clan of warriors rose against Queen Marika , only to be vanquished. The lone survivor, burdened by anger and regret, collected their swords and reforged them into a single Grafted Blade Greatsword . [ 1 ] Morne was the site of their legendary showdown with Godfrey, First Elden Lord , commemorated by a nearby Sword Monument . Although the hero swore an Oath of Vengeance , [ 2 ] they were ultimately defeated by the Elden Lord , and their sword became a treasure of the keep. [ 3 ]
After the Shattering , this fortress fell under the control of Godrick the Grafted , a distant scion of the Golden Lineage , who ruled Limgrave from Stormveil Castle . He appointed Castellan Edgar to oversee the castle and its Godrick Soldier garrison; however, by the time the player arrives, it has fallen to an uprising by its maltreated Misbegotten servants. [ 4 ] [ 5 ] Edgar's blind daughter, Irina of Morne , fled the castle, but her Great Coffin escort was overtaken by Misbegotten on the road near the Bridge of Sacrifice . Edgar is bound by duty to maintain his post until the sword of Morne is reclaimed from the Leonine Misbegotten . [ 6 ]
Caria Manor is a Location in Elden Ring .
A large estate in the north-west of Liurnia. The manor was once the home of the Carian Royal Family [ 1 ] , who ruled over Liurnia and governed the Academy of Raya Lucaria . [ 2 ] After the Academy turned on the Carians, the Cuckoo Knights launched an assault on the manor, catching the Carian Knights off guard. However, the Cuckoos were caught in a magic snare which keeps their souls trapped within the manor. [ 3 ]
In recent times, there have been rumours of vassals of the royal family gathering in the manor's grounds, possibly including the secretive Ranni the Witch . [ 4 ]
Ainsel River is an underground region in Elden Ring .
Map of Ainsel River
One of the two great rivers that flow beneath the Lands Between . Ainsel is said to be the grave of civilisations that flourished before the Erdtree . [ 1 ] The eastern side of Ainsel is dominated by the Uhl Palace Ruins, characterised by their mausoleums and statues, and inhabited by the Claymen who served as priests of the ancient dynasty. [ 2 ]
Nokstella, one of the Eternal Cities, can be found in the western portion of the subterranean space, inhabited by the Nox who were banished underground by the Greater Will long ago. [ 3 ] Deeper still is the Lake of Rot , a putrid underground swamp littered with ancient ruins, where the essence of an Outer God was sealed. [ 4 ] At the deepest point is the lair of Astel , a malformed star who once assailed an Eternal City and took away its sky. [ 5 ] Beyond Astel is a lift which leads to the Moonlight Altar , provided the Dark Moon Ring has been found.
Ainsel can be accessed via the Ainsel River Well in eastern Liurnia of the Lakes . The Ainsel River Main, which encompasses Nokstella, can be accessed via a sending gate in Renna's Rise , after Ranni the Witch gains possession of the Fingerslayer Blade .
Siofra River is an underground region in Elden Ring .
Map of Siofra River
One of the two great rivers that flow beneath the Lands Between . Siofra is said to be the grave of civilizations that flourished before the Erdtree [ 1 ] , and evidence of this can be found in the many ancient structures that litter the vast, subterranean space. The towering remains of an ancient dynasty [ 2 ] are prominent throughout the area, inhabited by the Claymen who once served as the dynasty's priests. [ 3 ]
The lower portion of Siofra River can be accessed via the Siofra River Well in Limgrave 's Mistwood. This wooded area is home to spectral Ancestral Followers , who live alongside a diverse assortment of wildlife. The remains of a great, horned beast can be found in the Hallowhorn Grounds. Interacting with the remains after lighting the flames scattered throughout the area will facilitate an encounter with an Ancestor Spirit . This area also connects to Caelid via the Deep Siofra Well .
Towering over the woodland is Nokron, one of the Eternal Cities inhabited by the Nox . Nokron is initially inaccessible, however a route is opened when a star falls upon Limgrave, following the defeat of Starscourge Radahn . The Fingerslayer Blade , a treasure of Nokron said to be able to harm the Greater Will and its vassal Fingers [ 4 ] , is found within Night's Sacred Ground, beneath a chair-crypt that holds a vast corpse. This upper region also houses another Hallowhorn Grounds, from which the Regal Ancestor Spirit can be encountered. Nearby, the aqueduct hides a coffin which can be used to access Deeproot Depths , guarded by a pair of Valiant Gargoyles .
To the east, on a separate island within the vast cavern, are the ruins of an ancient palace. It is here that Mohg, Lord of Blood has established the seat of his coming Mohgwyn Dynasty, and all the nightmares it may bring. [ 5 ]
The Subterranean Shunning-Grounds are connected to Leyndell, Royal Capital and the Deeproot Depths . The entrance to the Leyndell Catacombs can be found within the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds. It is in the room with the Giant Crayfish .
An intricate system of sewers and dungeons that spreads out below the capital. It is crawling with all kinds of shunned creatures, most notably the Omen , who are imprisoned there unbeknownst to anyone. [ 1 ] The layout is disorienting due to the multitude of tunnels, waterways, and chambers. Deep within the dungeon is a cathedral, where an encounter with Mohg, the Omen occurs. The altar at the back of the cathedral is illusory, and hides a passage which can only be unsealed by killing Morgott, the Omen King in the city above. The passage leads to a catacomb which plunges deep into the earth. It is here that a nomadic tribe was once entombed so as to bury a maddening disease that followed them, [ 2 ] and where, in their despair, they summoned the flame of frenzy . [ 3 ] The Three Fingers can be met behind a door at the lowest level of the catacomb, provided one removes all of their equipment first.
The home of Kenneth Haight , this fortress on the eastern coast of Limgrave has been occupied by soldiers from the army of Godrick the Grafted , led by a knight obsessed with blood.
After the player liberates the fort, Kenneth moves back in, along with a small band of Demi-Humans.
Fort Gael is a location in Elden Ring .
A fort occupied by the forces of General Radahn . The front is heavily fortified and manned by torch-wielding soldiers and an archer who commands gravitational abilities. A lion is confined within the fort, but can only be fought after scaling the outside of the structure and dropping down from above.
Sellia, Town of Sorcery is a location in Elden Ring .
A town in Caelid on the eastern bank of the Swamp of Aeonia .
The Eternal City of Nokron sleeps below Sellia, [ 1 ] and it is said that the Sellians are descended from the city's inhabitants. [ 2 ] Primeval Sorcerer Lusat , one of the founding Glintstone Sorcerers , came from Sellia. [ 3 ] Other Sellian sorcerers followed in Lusat's footsteps, travelling to the Academy of Raya Lucaria to study the Olivinus Conspectus . [ 4 ]
Sellian sorcerers are assassins who are said to hunt their fellow sorcerers, [ 5 ] employing night sorceries that allowed them to turn their weapons, [ 6 ] or their own bodies, [ 7 ] invisible to deceive their enemies.
General Radahn studied gravity sorcery in Sellia in his youth, [ 8 ] learning from an Alabaster Lord . [ 9 ] The knowledge he gained allowed him to challenge the stars [ 10 ] during the Starscourge Conflict , where he held the town of Sellia secure. [ 11 ]
Presently, the town is inhabited by spectral Glintstone Sorcerers and mechanical marionettes , and many of the buildings have been ensnared by the roots that trail from the nearby Swamp of Aeonia . Several buildings are protected by seals , which can be broken by lighting the flames at the tops of the town's three towers. Lighting all three will break the seal that blocks the entrance to the chair-crypt , where two former Nox inhabitants of the Eternal Cities reside.
A derelict castle sinking into a poisonous mire in the north of Altus Plateau. For generations, the Shaded Castle was ruled over by House Marais, who served as both executioners and castellans. [ 1 ] Maleigh Marais , born sickly like all sons of House Marais, became beguiled by Malenia [ 2 ] , claiming to feel her presence when he held the Valkyrie's Prosthesis [ 3 ]
Elemer of the Briar , an infamous killer of instructors and merchants [ 4 ] , was held in the castle for execution. However, he managed to steal the executioner's sword of House Marais and furnished it with the battle skills of his home of Eochaid , thus avoiding execution. [ 5 ] Elemer succeeded in taking over the castle, bringing about the ruin of House Marais. [ 6 ] Maleigh Marais can be found wandering the craggy wasteland to the west of the castle.
Leyndell, Ashen Capital is a legacy dungeon located in Altus Plateau . It is an altered form of Leyndell, Royal Capital which can be accessed after defeating Maliketh, the Black Blade .
With the defeat of Maliketh, the Black Blade , the Rune of Death is unbound, and the Flame of Ruin burns away the impenetrable thorns blocking the entrance to the Erdtree . [ 1 ] The city of Leyndell is blanketed in thick ash, burying all but the tallest buildings. The Tarnished returns to the city after releasing the Rune of Death, finally able to approach the Erdtree and gain entry.
This area is connected to the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds and the Stone Platform . It is still possible to access the Subterranean Shunning-Grounds from this version of Leyndell. A manhole cover that was previously closed is now open, allowing for one to drop down into the sewers below.
In Sol, the sight of an eclipse inspires a dreadful awe, preventing an onlooker from averting his gaze. - Eclipse Shotel
Castle Sol is a landmark in Elden Ring .
Castle Sol is a castle in the northern Mountaintops of the Giants .
Castle Sol was an old fortress built on the northernmost tip of the Lands Between , belonging to those who later became Banished Knights . These drake hunters would gift an Icerind Hatchet , made from a scale of Borealis the Freezing Fog , to Liurnia of the Lakes as part of their diplomatic relationships. [ 1 ]
In the distant past, a frigid, awe-inspiring eclipse mesmerized the knights of Castle Sol. Drained of its color, the lusterless sun repelled Destined Death and granted life to the soulless . [ 2 ] [ 3 ] The castle's inhabitants gathered at its Church of the Eclipse , where they used the storied Eclipse Shotel in worship of the dreadful celestial event . [ 4 ] [ 5 ] [ 6 ]
In a later age , when veteran Commander Niall and his men were garrisoned at Sol, another force defeated them in battle even though they wielded storm and lightning -clad weapons. [ 7 ] In exchange for the captured lives of his fallen men, Niall offered his right leg. Unable to die, and with nowhere to fade to, Niall eternally led the summoned spirits of his army of no nation. [ 8 ] [ 9 ]
Following the Night of Black Knives , Sol's inhabitants fervently prayed for another eclipse, hoping to call a spirit into the soulless demigod interred with their mausoleum . [ 4 ] [ 10 ] The Mausoleum Knights , who beheaded themselves to protect their masters as spirits , displayed the Eclipse to ward off the Destined Death of Godwyn the Golden . [ 11 ]
Later, Miquella the Kind visited to castle and petitioned the master to return the life of his comrade. [ 4 ] [ 12 ] [ 13 ] He bestowed half of a secret medallion to the master that would allow him to access the then-upcoming Haligtree if he had succeeded in his task. [ 14 ] However, the awaited eclipse never came to pass, making the master of the castle unable to visit the Haligtree as he wasn't able to fulfill his duty, thus he lost hope and perished. [ 15 ] Niall, the commander of Castle Sol, left alone in the castle to protect his long-passed master, continue commanding the nationless spirits of his Banished Knight army. [ 9 ] [ 8 ]
Castle Sol is situated on the northern edge of the Mountaintops of the Giants , north Snow Valley Ruins Overlook . It is accessed from the east, after traveling down from the graveyard with Giant Skeletons . The path is guarded by a Tibia Mariner and Death Rite Bird .
The route through this land, crossed east to west by a frozen river, leads to Miquella's Haligtree. This is the path taken by those unchosen, though it is a trial all the same. - [[ Map Consecrated Snowfield ]] — [[ Elden Ring ]]
The Consecrated Snowfield is a subregion located on the Mountaintops of the Giants .
Map of the Consecrated Snowfield
A snow-swept, misty area to the west of the Mountaintops of the Giants . The Consecrated Snowfield is final trial for those who seek Miquella's Haligtree , and can only be accessed by uniting the two halves of the Haligtree Secret Medallion, found in the Village of the Albinaurics and Castle Sol , and bringing them to the Grand Lift of Rold .
Visibility is limited in many parts of the snowfield. Small, golden lights illuminate the path from the upper section to the broad, snowy plane below, through which a frozen river runs. In the south-west are the Yelough Anix Ruins , consumed by the Flame of Frenzy. Far to the north lies the Apostate Derelict , where the gentle yet towering sister of Latenna the Albinauric resides. South-east of there is Ordina, Liturgical Town , which hides the entrance to the Haligtree. There is also a waygate, tucked away on the western cliffs, which leads to Mohgwyn Palace .
A somber plain covered in spiritgraves. The spiral tower of the Hornsent lies to the northwest, and the entire expanse is marred by the harrowing ravages of war. - Map: Gravesite Plain
The Gravesite Plain is a subregion of the Realm of Shadow in Shadow of the Erdtree . This area of the map is revealed by Map: Gravesite Plain .
The Gravesite Plain is a vast wheat field dotted with ruins and ethereal spiritgraves , located in the west of the Realm of Shadow . The spiral tower of the hornsent lies to the northwest of the region. [ 1 ]
Scadu Altus is named after its counterpart in the realm of the Erdtree. At its center lies the shadow keep. - Map: Scadu Altus
Scadu Altus is a subregion of the Realm of Shadow in Shadow of the Erdtree .
The Scadu Altus is a plateau at the center of the Realm of Shadow , occupied by the army of Messmer the Impaler . It was named for its counterpart in the realm of the Erdtree . [ 1 ] Messmer's stronghold, the Shadow Keep , lies to the north of the region.
Here, and here alone, were moon and fire ever together. - Rellana's Twin Blades
Castle Ensis is a legacy dungeon in Shadow of the Erdtree .
Castle Ensis is a medium-sized fortification within the Realm of Shadow , connecting the Gravesite Plain to the Scadu Altus . Located north-northeast of the Three Paths Cross Site of Grace , the castle lies east of Belurat, Tower Settlement , across the Ellac Greatbridge . Castle Ensis is adjacent to the Fog Rift Fort and the Fifth Belfry .
Castle Ensis is the stronghold of Rellana , a princess of the Carian Royal Family . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] Rellana and her oathsworn followed Messmer the Impaler on his crusade against the hornsent . [ 3 ] [ 4 ] As a result, the castle is populated by the enchanted knights of Caria , Lazuli Sorcerers and many Messmer Soldiers .
Scadu Altus is named after its counterpart in the realm of the Erdtree. At its center lies the shadow keep. - Map Scadu Altus
The Shadow Keep is a legacy dungeon in Elden Ring , included in the Shadow of the Erdtree expansion.
A gigantic keep in the Shadow Realm , located at the heart of the Scadu Altus . It serves as Messmer the Impaler 's lair. It is connected to Scaduview , Specimen Storehouse , and Shadow Keep, Church District .
Proud drake warrior, I beg of you. Scale the jagged peak. Face Bayle the Dread. And when you do... Summon me. Summon my soul. - Igon
The Jagged Peak is a subregion of the Realm of Shadow in Shadow of the Erdtree . Collecting Map: Southern Shore will reveal the Jagged Peak on the Shadow Realm map.
Dominating the eastern Southern Shore , the Jagged Peak is a towering mountain visible from many elevated points in the Realm of Shadow . At its base , the Grand Altar of Dragon Communion is tended by an ancient Dragon Communion Priestess , who reveals the occult history and purpose of Dragon Communion . The mountain is populated by powerful dragons and drakes, as well as the lifeless remnants of drake warriors scattered along the perilous ascent. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] The weather grows violent near the peak, with red lightning striking the treacherous slopes and jagged stones. [ 3 ] At the summit awaits Bayle the Dread , an indominable dragon whose burning enmity toward the Dragonlord is legendary. [ 4 ] [ 5 ]

A captivating vista of brilliant blue flowers, intermingled with colossal stone coffins of unknown origin that seemingly drifted to this place. - Map: Southern Shore
The Cerulean Coast is a subregion of the Realm of Shadow in Shadow of the Erdtree .
The Cerulean Coast is located on the Southern Shore of the Realm of Shadow. It is connected to Charo's Hidden Grave , Foot of the Jagged Peak , Gravesite Plain , and the Stone Coffin Fissure . The area is revealed on the Shadow Realm map when Map: Southern Shore has been collected.
The Cerulean Coast is accessible via the Pillar Path Cross south of Castle Ensis . Adventurers can traverse this region by heading north to cliffs, descending via rock formations, and proceeding south through Ellac River Cave . Glowing blue flowers and massive stone arks signify the Cerulean Coast.
The northeast Cerulean Coast contains the Finger Ruins of Rhia , and the Southern Nameless Mausoleum lies on an island to the west. A rocky southern peninsula hides a deep tunnel leading to the Stone Coffin Fissure legacy dungeon , which remains locked by a Miquella's Haligtree seal until Miquella discards his Great Rune . This story event is triggered by entering the Shadow Keep or crossing the bridge east of Bonny Village .
A somber field of ephemeral blue lilies blooms among beached coffin-ships from beyond the Lands Between . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] These stone vesels house the Congealed Putrescence of ancient, tainted life, [ 3 ] once purified in ghostflame by the deathbirds long ago. [ 4 ] [ 5 ] The blue flowers are contrasted by a sea of luminous crimson lilies on the plateau above, said to be the home of the Tibia Mariners and the hidden grave of Charo . [ 6 ] Deep underground, below both fields, wilts St. Trina 's Garden of Deep Purple . [ 7 ]
A thick forest sprawls at the depths of the ravine that is untouched even by sunlight. Known as the sanctum of Sage Midra, and is a region forbidden by the hornsent. - Map: Abyss
The Abyssal Woods (奈落の森, Naraku no Mori ) is a subregion of the Realm of Shadow in Shadow of the Erdtree .
Below the rest of the Realm of Shadow, hidden under a sprawling canopy that blots out the light of the sky, a thick swampy woodland corrupted by Madness . The Hornsent Inquisitors stand guard against the horrors within, and the atmosphere is so harrowing that Torrent refuses to be summoned out of fear. Messages on the ground warn about beings lurking in the woods, creatures that cannot be touched and can kill one with a glance.
The Abyssal Woods can only be accessed by navigating through Darklight Catacombs at the base of Recluses' River in Scadu Altus .
Moonveil is a Katana , a melee armament in Elden Ring .
Katana forged of glintstone . Masterpiece of a Sellian swordsmith .
Light enwreathes the blade when sheathed, explaining its Moonveil moniker.
Unique Skill : Transient Moonlight
Sheathe blade, holding it at the hip in a composed stance. Follow up with either a normal or a strong attack to draw the blade at great speed for an instant slash attack . Both attacks fire off a wave of light.

Rivers of Blood is a Katana , a melee armament in Elden Ring .
Weapon of Okina , swordsman from the Land of Reeds . A cursed weapon that has felled countless men.
When Mohg, the Lord of Blood , first felt Okina's sword, and madness, upon his flesh, he had a proposal, to offer Okina the life of a demon, whose thirst would never go unsated.
Unique Skill : Corpse Piler
Forms a blade of cursed blood for repeated, interweaving successive attacks. Follow up with an additional input for further successive attacks.

The Dark Moon Greatsword is a Greatsword melee armament in Elden Ring .
A Moon Greatsword bestowed by a Carian queen upon her spouse to honor long-standing tradition. One of the legendary armaments .
Ranni 's sigil is a full moon , cold and leaden, and this sword is but a beam of its light .
Unique Skill : Moonlight Greatsword
Raise the sword aloft, bathing it in the light of the dark moon . Temporarily increases magic attack power and imbues blade with frost . Charged attack release blasts of moonlight.

A Moon Greatsword bestowed by a Carian queen upon her spouse to honor long-standing tradition. One of the legendary armaments .

Received at the end of the Lunar Princess Ranni questline.
The Blasphemous Blade is a Greatsword in Elden Ring .
Sacred sword of Rykard, Lord of Blasphemy . Remains of the countless heroes he has devoured writhe upon the surface of this blade.
Now they share the same blood , bound together as family. Some HP is restored upon defeating an enemy.
Unique Skill : Taker's Flames
Raise the sacred sword aloft to set it ablaze with blasphemous flames, then bring it down to fire off a forward blast. The flames steal HP from those they touch.
冒涜の君主、ライカードの聖剣 彼の喰らった無数の人々、英雄たちの亡骸が 剣身の表面でうねうねと蠢いている
それらは、いまや血を同じくした家族であり 敵を倒したとき、ＨＰを回復する
聖剣を掲げ、冒涜の炎を燃やし 激しく前方に放つ戦技 その炎は、ＨＰを奪う
Sacred sword of Rykard, Lord of Blasphemy . Remains of the countless heroes he has devoured writhe upon the surface of this blade.
Now they share the same blood , bound together as family. Some HP is restored upon defeating an enemy.
Unique Skill : Taker's Flames
Raise the sacred sword aloft to set it ablaze with blasphemous flames, then bring it down to fire off a forward blast. The flames steal HP from those they touch.
Trade the Remembrance of the Blasphemous , dropped by Rykard, Lord of Blasphemy , with Finger Reader Enia .
Alternatively, use one of the Wandering Mausoleums with a bell to duplicate one (can only obtain one per playthrough using either method).
The Sacred Relic Sword is a Greatsword , a melee armament in Elden Ring .
Sword wrought from the remains of a god who should have lived a life eternal.
Thoughts on what the weapon portends are many and varied. Some consider it the mark of a great sin , or a sign of a great devastation. Some think it as the end of an age , while others; the beginning.
Unique Skill : Wave of Gold
Imbue the sword with bygone golden glory, then fire it at foes. A wide, golden wave fans out forwards, sweeping through all enemies caught in its path.
永遠に死ぬことのないはずの 神の遺体から生まれる剣
人々はそれに様々な意味を見出す 大いなる罪、破滅、時代の終わり あるいは始まりを
剣身に往時の黄金を宿し、放つ戦技 黄金の波は、前方扇状に大きく広がり あらゆる敵を薙ぎ払う
Sword wrought from the remains of a god who should have lived a life eternal.
Thoughts on what the weapon portends are many and varied. Some consider it the mark of a great sin , or a sign of a great devastation. Some think it as the end of an age , while others; the beginning.
Unique Skill : Wave of Gold
Imbue the sword with bygone golden glory, then fire it at foes. A wide, golden wave fans out forwards, sweeping through all enemies caught in its path.
Trade the Elden Remembrance , dropped by Elden Beast , with Finger Reader Enia .
Alternatively, use one of the Wandering Mausoleums to duplicate one (can only obtain one per playthrough using either method).
The Starscourge Greatsword is a paired melee armament found in Elden Ring .
Curved greatswords of black steel wielded by General Radahn . A pair of weapons decorated with a lion mane motif.
Radahn earned considerable renown as the Starscourge in his youth, and it is said that it was during this time he engraved the gravity crest upon these blades.
Unique Skill : Starcaller Cry
Bring the two swords together and roar into the skies, pulling in enemies with a gravitational wave. Follow up with an additional input to slam down with gravity -infused swords.
将軍ラダーンが振るった黒鉄の大剣 獅子の鬣があしらわれた、二刀一対の得物
若きラダーンの星砕きの伝承で名高く 重力の紋章は、その時に刻んだものだという
両の剣を合わせた後、空に雄叫び 重力波により、敵を引き寄せる戦技 追加入力で、重力を纏った剣を叩きつける
Curved greatswords of black steel wielded by General Radahn . A pair of weapons decorated with a lion mane motif.
Radahn earned considerable renown as the Starscourge in his youth, and it is said that it was during this time he engraved the gravity crest upon these blades.
Unique Skill : Starcaller Cry
Bring the two swords together and roar into the skies, pulling in enemies with a gravitational wave. Follow up with an additional input to slam down with gravity -infused swords.
Trade the Remembrance of the Starscourge , dropped by Starscourge Radahn , with Finger Reader Enia .
Alternatively, use one of the Wandering Mausoleums with a bell to duplicate one (can only obtain one per playthrough using either method).
The Hand of Malenia is a Katana , a melee armament in Elden Ring .
Blade built into Malenia 's prosthetic arm. Through consecration it is resistant to rot .
Malenia's war prosthesis symbolized her victories. Some claim to have seen wings when the weapon was raised aloft; wings of fierce determination that have never known defeat.
Unique Skill : Waterfowl Dance
Perform a series of one-footed leaps in the manner of a waterfowl to unleash a swift yet graceful slashing combo. Repeated inputs allow for up to two follow-up attacks.
マレニアの義手に仕込まれていた武器 聖別された刃は、決して腐ることがない
マレニアの戦義手は、即ち不敗の象徴であった 人々は、掲げられたそれに翼を見たという 敗れを知らぬ、熾烈なる意志の翼を
水鳥のごとく一本足で跳び 超高速の連続斬りに繋げる戦技 追加入力で、二度まで追撃に繋げられる
Blade built into Malenia 's prosthetic arm. Through consecration it is resistant to rot .
Malenia's war prosthesis symbolized her victories. Some claim to have seen wings when the weapon was raised aloft; wings of fierce determination that have never known defeat.
Unique Skill : Waterfowl Dance
Perform a series of one-footed leaps in the manner of a waterfowl to unleash a swift yet graceful slashing combo. Repeated inputs allow for up to two follow-up attacks.
Trade the Remembrance of the Rot Goddess , gained by defeating Malenia, Blade of Miquella , with Finger Reader Enia .
Alternatively, use one of the Wandering Mausoleums with a bell to duplicate one (can only obtain one per playthrough using either method).
The Greatsword is a Colossal Sword , a melee armament in Elden Ring .
A coarse iron lump of an ultra greatsword . Mows down foes by utilizing its incredible weight .
Though handling it likely requires the wielder to have surpassed the realm of the merely human , it is precisely for this reason the weapon is used to slaughter even inhuman foes.
巨大で武骨な鉄塊の剣 凄まじく重く、その重さで敵を薙ぎ払う
およそ人の扱える限界を超えた武器であり それ故に、これは人外をも屠り得る
A coarse iron lump of an ultra greatsword . Mows down foes by utilizing its incredible weight .
Though handling it likely requires the wielder to have surpassed the realm of the merely human , it is precisely for this reason the weapon is used to slaughter even inhuman foes.
The Uchigatana is a Katana , a melee armament in Elden Ring .
A katana with a long single-edged curved blade. A unique weapon wielded by the samurai from the Land of Reeds .
The blade, with its undulating design, boasts extraordinary sharpness, and its slash attacks cause blood loss .
長く反った、切れ味鋭い片刃の剣 刀と呼ばれる、葦の地の侍たち独特の得物
打ち鍛えられた刀身には、波打つ刃文が浮かび その斬撃は対手に出血を強いる
A katana with a long single-edged curved blade. A unique weapon wielded by the samurai from the Land of Reeds .
The blade, with its undulating design, boasts extraordinary sharpness, and its slash attacks cause blood loss .
The Nagakiba is a Katana , a melee armament in Elden Ring .
Katana with a ferociously long blade. Signature weapon of Yura , hunter of Bloody Fingers .
Reminiscent of a reinforced spear , its imposing length can be put to good use with powerful thrusting attacks .
恐ろしく長い刃を持つ刀 血の指の狩人、ユラの得物
その威容は鍛えられた槍のごとく 突き貫く攻撃で真価を発揮する
Katana with a ferociously long blade. Signature weapon of Yura , hunter of Bloody Fingers .
Reminiscent of a reinforced spear , its imposing length can be put to good use with powerful thrusting attacks .
Received with the Piercing Fang Ash of War and Standard affinity on it. Either dropped by Bloody Finger Hunter Yura at the end of his questline at the Second Church of Marika or after being killed by the player. Otherwise, found at the last spot he was encountered before meeting Shabriri on the Mountaintops of the Giants .
The Meteorite Staff is a Glintstone Staff and catalyst used to cast Sorceries in Elden Ring .
Staff embedded with a dark purple glintstone , said to be the fragment of a meteorite . Boasts high sorcery scaling and boosts gravity sorceries as well.
However, this staff cannot be strengthened in any way.
暗紫の輝石が埋め込まれた杖 それは隕石の欠片であるといい 高い魔術補正を持ち、また重力の魔術を強化する
ただし、この杖は強化することができない
Staff embedded with a dark purple glintstone , said to be the fragment of a meteorite . Boasts high sorcery scaling and boosts gravity sorceries as well.
However, this staff cannot be strengthened in any way.
Location : Street of Sages Ruins
Staff of the primeval glintstone sorcerer Lusat . Only those who have glimpsed what lies beyond the wisdom of stone may wield it.
Enhances power of all sorceries , but consumes additional FP .
源流の魔術師の一方、ルーサットの輝石杖 石の知、その遥か先に触れた者だけが これを振るうことができる
すべての魔術の威力を高めるが 消費ＦＰも増加してしまう
Staff of the primeval glintstone sorcerer Lusat . Only those who have glimpsed what lies beyond the wisdom of stone may wield it.
Enhances power of all sorceries , but consumes additional FP .
Found inside a chest after the Nox Swordstress & Nox Monk duo boss fight in Sellia, Town of Sorcery , located in Caelid .
Increases power of Sorceries by +10% and grants a "virtual" increase of 40 to Dexterity, but increases FP consumption by +50%.
Staff of the primeval glintstone sorcerer Azur . Only those who have glimpsed what lies beyond the wisdom of stone may wield it.
Reduces casting time of sorceries , but consumes additional FP .
源流の魔術師の一方、アズールの輝石杖 石の知、その遥か先に触れた者だけが これを振るうことができる
すべての魔術の使用速度を速めるが 消費ＦＰも増加してしまう
Staff of the primeval glintstone sorcerer Azur . Only those who have glimpsed what lies beyond the wisdom of stone may wield it.
Reduces casting time of sorceries , but consumes additional FP .
Found in a secluded room on the highest level of the Church of the Cuckoo . The level can be accessed via the rooftops of the Academy of Raya Lucaria .
From the Debate Parlor site of grace, go outside to the left until you meet two Raya Lucaria Sorcerers . Jump down on the stairs next to them. Continue forward until you can jump onto the rooftops. Then, proceed further and go up the ladder at the end of said rooftops.
After the sorcerer, go down on the rooftops again, until you can see a dome-like structure that has windows. Go through one of the windows, and descend onto the lower floor. One of the exits leads to a enclosed bridge, with a High Page guarding the secluded room. The staff is in the room behind him, in front of the inactive School of Graven Mages .
The Carian Regal Scepter is a Glintstone Staff and catalyst used to cast Sorceries in Elden Ring .
Magic scepter of Rennala, Queen of the Full Moon . The glintstone is known as a Carian Blue , enhancing full moon sorceries .
Only those of the highest intelligence may wield this, the finest of all glintstone staves .
Unique Skill : Spinning Weapon
Channel magic into the glintstone to suspend the scepter in mid air and cause it to spin violently. Those it touches will suffer successive magic attacks.
満月の女王、レナラの魔術王笏 その輝石は、カーリアの青と呼ばれ 満月の魔術を強化する
最高の知性にのみ許される 最上の輝石杖であろう
輝石に魔力を込め、王笏を前方に浮かせ それを高速に回転させる戦技 触れる者に、魔力の連撃をなす
Magic scepter of Rennala, Queen of the Full Moon . The glintstone is known as a Carian Blue , enhancing full moon sorceries .
Only those of the highest intelligence may wield this, the finest of all glintstone staves .
Unique Skill : Spinning Weapon
Channel magic into the glintstone to suspend the scepter in mid air and cause it to spin violently. Those it touches will suffer successive magic attacks.
Trade the Remembrance of the Full Moon Queen , gained by defeating Rennala, Queen of the Full Moon , with Finger Reader Enia .
Alternatively, use one of the Wandering Mausoleums with a bell to duplicate one (can only obtain one per playthrough using either method).
The Erdtree Seal is a Sacred Seal and catalyst in Elden Ring .
A formless sacred seal decorated with an Erdtree crest, once the focus of religion in the Lands Between .
Even though the Elden Ring is shattered , and the Erdtree has dulled from its former radiance, earnest faith continues to hold the answers.
黄金樹の紋章を象った、幻影の聖印 狭間の信仰、かつてその中心にあったもの
エルデンリングが砕け、黄金樹が陰るとも それは、ひたむきな信仰に応え続ける
A formless sacred seal decorated with an Erdtree crest, once the focus of religion in the Lands Between .
Even though the Elden Ring is shattered , and the Erdtree has dulled from its former radiance, earnest faith continues to hold the answers.
Found inside a open cell down the town near the Prison Town Church grace, located in Volcano Manor . There is a Omenkiller enemy near it.
The Dragon Communion Seal is a Sacred Seal in Elden Ring .
Formless drakeblood seal with a dragon communion crest. Enhances Dragon Communion incantations .
The sacrificial devouring of the heart gives power. Indeed, Dragon Communion is too primal in nature for the term "incantation" to be appropriate. This seal scales incantations with one's arcane attribute.
竜餐の紋章を象った、竜血の幻影印 竜餐の祈祷を強化する
心臓を捧げ喰らい、力を得る 竜餐の様は、祈祷と呼ぶには野蛮にすぎ この印は、神秘でも祈祷を補正する
Formless drakeblood seal with a dragon communion crest. Enhances Dragon Communion incantations .
The sacrificial devouring of the heart gives power. Indeed, Dragon Communion is too primal in nature for the term "incantation" to be appropriate. This seal scales incantations with one's arcane attribute.
Dropped by a spectral Banished Knight located in the Fringefolk Hero's Grave in Limgrave . To find it, start at the Stranded Graveyard Site of Grace and head down the first two ramps in the Grave, then head right in the split to go up another two ramps. The Knight is inside a small room at the end of the ramp and is quite tough for the early game. The Chariot in the dungeon can be used to help kill it, though that comes at considerable risk to the player as well.
The Frenzied Flame Seal is a sacred seal in Elden Ring . It enhances Frenzied Flame incantations by 20%.
Uniquely, it has no stat prerequisites, and scales simultaneously with Strength , Dexterity , Intelligence , and Faith .
Formless sacred seal bestowed by the maiden of the Three Fingers . Enhances incantations of the frenzied flame .
This seal is the mark of the Lord of Frenzied Flame . Scales incantations using strength, dexterity, intelligence and faith all together.
三本指の巫女が授ける、幻影の聖印 狂い火の祈祷を強化する
それは、狂い火の王たる証であり 筋力、技量、知力、信仰 そのすべてが祈祷を補正する
Formless sacred seal bestowed by the maiden of the Three Fingers . Enhances incantations of the frenzied flame .
This seal is the mark of the Lord of Frenzied Flame . Scales incantations using strength, dexterity, intelligence and faith all together.
Received upon completing Lightseeker Hyetta 's questline.
Maliketh 's black blade which once harbored the power of the Rune of Death . A sad shadow of its former glory.
After a fragment of Death was stolen on that fateful night , Maliketh bound the blade within his own flesh, such that none might ever rob Death again.
Unique Skill : Destined Death
Set free the remnants of Destined Death , plunging the greatsword into the ground to summon a myriad of blades. In addition to dealing immediate damage, this attack reduces the enemy's maximum HP and continues to wear down HP for a short time.
運命の死を宿したマリケスの黒き剣 その大いなる抜け殻
陰謀の夜に、死の一部が盗まれた後 マリケスはこの剣を、自らの内に封じた もう二度と、誰にも死を盗ませぬように
運命の死、その残滓を解放し 大剣を地に突き立て、無数の刃を生じる戦技 ダメージを与えると共に、最大ＨＰを減少させ ごく短時間の間、ＨＰを細かく削り続ける
Maliketh 's black blade which once harbored the power of the Rune of Death . A sad shadow of its former glory.
After a fragment of Death was stolen on that fateful night , Maliketh bound the blade within his own flesh, such that none might ever rob Death again.
Unique Skill : Destined Death
Set free the remnants of Destined Death , plunging the greatsword into the ground to summon a myriad of blades. In addition to dealing immediate damage, this attack reduces the enemy's maximum HP and continues to wear down HP for a short time.
The blade is acquired by using the Remembrance of the Black Blade , gained by defeating Maliketh, The Black Blade in Crumbling Farum Azula near the end of the game, with Finger Reader Enia .
Alternatively, use one of the Wandering Mausoleums to duplicate one (can only obtain one per playthrough using either method).
Originally rubble from a ruin which fell from the sky, this surviving fragment was honed into a weapon. One of the legendary armaments .
The ruin it came from crumbled when struck by a meteorite , as such this weapon harbors its destructive power.
Unique Skill : Wave of Destruction
Raise the sword up high, then strike it against the ground to fire off a wave of gravitational force .
空から降る遺跡の残骸 その砕けなかった欠片を鍛えた武器 「伝説の武器」のひとつ
その遺跡は隕石により崩壊したとされ この武器は、崩壊の力を宿している
剣を掲げた後、それを叩きつけ 地を走る重力波を放つ戦技
Originally rubble from a ruin which fell from the sky, this surviving fragment was honed into a weapon. One of the legendary armaments .
The ruin it came from crumbled when struck by a meteorite , as such this weapon harbors its destructive power.
Unique Skill : Wave of Destruction
Raise the sword up high, then strike it against the ground to fire off a wave of gravitational force .
The storied sword of Castle Morne . A revenger 's weapon, it is burdened with oceans of anger and regret. One of the legendary armaments .
A lone surviving champion from a country now vanished was so determined to continue fighting that he claimed the swords of an entire clan of warriors.
Unique Skill : Oath of Vengeance
Swear an oath upon the greatsword to avenge the clan, temporarily raising all attributes for a certain duration. While the oath's effects are active, poise will also be increased.
モーンの城 に所蔵された伝説の武器 無数の嘆き、怒りを背負った復讐の大剣 「伝説の武器」のひとつ
かつて、ただ独り生き残った亡国の英雄は 一族の戦士すべての剣を集め、戦い続けた
専用戦技「復讐の誓い」
大剣に一族の復讐を誓い 一定時間、すべての能力値を高める戦技 誓いの瞬間は、強靭度も高まっている
The storied sword of Castle Morne . A revenger 's weapon, it is burdened with oceans of anger and regret. One of the legendary armaments .
A lone surviving champion from a country now vanished was so determined to continue fighting that he claimed the swords of an entire clan of warriors.
Unique Skill : Oath of Vengeance
Swear an oath upon the greatsword to avenge the clan, temporarily raising all attributes for a certain duration. While the oath's effects are active, poise will also be increased.
Location : Castle Morne
The Godslayer's Greatsword is a Colossal Sword , a melee armament in Elden Ring .
Sacred sword of the Gloam-Eyed Queen who controlled the Godskin Apostles before her defeat at the hands of Maliketh .
The black flames wielded by the apostles are channeled from this sword.
Unique Skill : The Queen's Black Flame
Set the blade ablaze with the god -slaying black flame before delivering a sweeping slash. Additional input allows for a follow-up attack. The black flames will continue to wear down HP for a while.
かつて神肌の使徒たちを率い マリケスに敗れた、宵眼の女王の聖剣
使徒たちの操る黒炎は この剣によりもたらされた
専用戦技「女王の黒炎」
剣身に神狩りの黒炎を燃やし、斬り払う戦技 追加入力で追撃に繋げられる また黒炎は、しばらくの間ＨＰを削り続ける

The black flames wielded by the apostles are channeled from this sword.
Unique Skill : The Queen's Black Flame
Set the blade ablaze with the god -slaying black flame before delivering a sweeping slash. Additional input allows for a follow-up attack. The black flames will continue to wear down HP for a while.
Location : Divine Tower of Caelid
The Bolt of Gransax is a Spear , a melee armament in Elden Ring . It is one of the Legendary Armaments .
Spear whittled from the weapon wielded by Gransax . One of the legendary armaments .
A great ancient dragon , Gransax once rained calamity upon the Royal Capital - the only time in historical record that Leyndell's walls have fallen. This marked the dawn of the war against the ancient dragons .
Unique Skill : Ancient Lightning Spear
Imbue the armament with the ancient dragons' red lightning , then throw it as a spear. Can be charged to increase its power .
大古竜グランサクスの得物から削り出した槍 「伝説の武器」のひとつ
大古竜の襲来は、ローデイルの城壁が破れた 歴史上唯一の事例であり 続く古竜たちとの戦いの端緒でもあった
古竜の武器たる赤い雷を武器に纏い それを、槍となして投擲する戦技 タメ使用で強化される
Spear whittled from the weapon wielded by Gransax . One of the legendary armaments .
A great ancient dragon , Gransax once rained calamity upon the Royal Capital - the only time in historical record that Leyndell's walls have fallen. This marked the dawn of the war against the ancient dragons .
Unique Skill : Ancient Lightning Spear
Imbue the armament with the ancient dragons' red lightning , then throw it as a spear. Can be charged to increase its power .
Located in Leyndell, Royal Capital .
Exit the Erdtree Sanctuary and descend with the elevator, then jump over the street railing and down onto the building below. The spear is on top of its gigantic version.
Warning : This item is not present in Leyndell, Ashen Capital . It must be obtained prior to defeating Maliketh, the Black Blade .
Piercing Gravel Stone sword containing primeval lightning . A portion of the Dragonlord 's power, gained from a remembrance .
This weapon commands great power over the paltry, mortal dragons of today.
Unique Skill : Thundercloud Form
Temporarily transform into a red thundercloud and fly through the air, then plunge down with a lightning-infused blade. Hold to increase the reach of the thundercloud form.
原初の雷を宿したさざれ石の刺剣 追憶から得られた、 竜王 の力の片鱗
永遠なき、卑小な竜の末裔たちに 高い威力を発揮する
自らの姿を一時赤い雷雲と化し 空を駆け、雷を纏った剣身で貫く戦技 長押しで、空を駆ける距離が伸びる
Piercing Gravel Stone sword containing primeval lightning . A portion of the Dragonlord 's power, gained from a remembrance .
This weapon commands great power over the paltry, mortal dragons of today.
Unique Skill : Thundercloud Form
Temporarily transform into a red thundercloud and fly through the air, then plunge down with a lightning-infused blade. Hold to increase the reach of the thundercloud form.
Trade the Remembrance of the Dragonlord , gained by defeating Dragonlord Placidusax , with Finger Reader Enia .
Alternatively, use one of the Wandering Mausoleums to duplicate one (can only obtain one per playthrough using either method).
Jagged dagger with a distinctive curved blade. Used by the noble servants of the Lord of Blood .
This dagger rips the flesh as it enters, inflicting blood loss with sickening efficacy. A proud testament to the success of its vicious design, this weapon is perpetually coated in blood .
Unique Skill : Reduvia Blood Blade
Slash with the wicked dagger, transforming its never-drying bloodstains into airborne blood blades that cause hemorrhaging. Can be fired in rapid succession.
ねじ曲がったぎざ刃を持つ異形の短刀 血の君主 に 仕える貴族たち の得物
その刃は、傷口を壊し出血を強い それを誇るかのように、常に血濡れている
専用戦技「レドゥビアの血刃」
ぎざ刃の乾かぬ血濡れを 出血を強いる刃となし放つ戦技 連続で放つことができる
Jagged dagger with a distinctive curved blade. Used by the noble servants of the Lord of Blood .
This dagger rips the flesh as it enters, inflicting blood loss with sickening efficacy. A proud testament to the success of its vicious design, this weapon is perpetually coated in blood .
Unique Skill : Reduvia Blood Blade
Slash with the wicked dagger, transforming its never-drying bloodstains into airborne blood blades that cause hemorrhaging. Can be fired in rapid succession.
Eleonora's Poleblade is a Twinblade , a melee armament in Elden Ring .
Twinned naginata forged in the Land of Reeds . Chosen weapon of Eleonora, Violet Bloody Finger .
Her mastery of the sword was such that her onslaught was likened to a whirlwind , but now her legacy is stained by accursed blood .
Unique Skill : Bloodblade Dance
Leap at foe to perform a flurry of tornado-like attacks. Follow up with an additional input to perform an attack that ends in an evasive maneuver.
葦の地で鍛えられた双薙刀 純紫の血指、エレオノーラの得物
一陣の旋風のごとき卓越した剣技は 今は呪われた血に汚されている
跳躍から、旋風のごとき連撃を繰り出す戦技 追加入力で、追撃の後に引いて距離を取る
Twinned naginata forged in the Land of Reeds . Chosen weapon of Eleonora, Violet Bloody Finger .
Her mastery of the sword was such that her onslaught was likened to a whirlwind , but now her legacy is stained by accursed blood .
Unique Skill : Bloodblade Dance
Leap at foe to perform a flurry of tornado-like attacks. Follow up with an additional input to perform an attack that ends in an evasive maneuver.
Defeating Eleonora, Violet Bloody Finger at the Second Church of Marika in the Altus Plateau .

Milady is a melee armament in Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree .
A light greatsword ; that is, a sword whose blade matches the length of a greatsword, while being constrained to a minimal weight.
Nicknamed after ladies of noble status for its refined appearance. With cultivated form, one can wield this weapon as swiftly as one might a straightsword .

A light greatsword ; that is, a sword whose blade matches the length of a greatsword, while being constrained to a minimal weight.
Nicknamed after ladies of noble status for its refined appearance. With cultivated form, one can wield this weapon as swiftly as one might a straightsword .

Steel greatsword wielded by the Knights of the Solitary Gaol .
Through a secret rite, they relinquished their hearts for heightened battle prowess. Next, they engraved their blades with two crests: one depicting the light of birth, and the other, solitude.

Sharply slash downward using the greatsword, shooting forward an arc of light. Strong attack allows for an advancing follow-up.

Weapon of Messmer the Impaler . A greatspear with a warped blade in the shape of undulating flame .

The Shattering of the Elden Ring
Ahh, the Great Runes are the stuff of the Demigods; the children of the goddess, Queen Marika. She who is vessel of the Elden Ring. Tainted by the strength of their runes, her children warred, but none could become Elden Lord. - Finger Reader Enia
The Great Runes ( 大ルーン , Dai Rūn ) are Key Items in Elden Ring .
The Great Runes are mighty shards of the Elden Ring [ 1 ] [ 2 ] which were inherited by some of the demigods. [ 3 ] The great strength they granted tainted the demigods, compelling them to war over control of the Lands Between . [ 4 ]
The known Great Runes are as follows:
The Great Runes are the shards of the Elden Ring, currently making up the Golden Order , and represent the concepts of order and discipline that the demigods enforced on the physical world. [ 6 ] They were inherited by some of the demigod offspring of Queen Marika the Eternal following the shattering of the Elden Ring. The mad taint of the newfound strength granted by the Great Runes precipitated the Shattering , [ 3 ] wherein the demigods fought for control of the Lands Between. [ 4 ] The demigods who inherited Great Runes were known as Shardbearers .
The Tarnished , upon returning to the Lands Between, were compelled by the Two Fingers to seek out demigods to relieve them of their Great Runes in order to become Elden Lord . [ 7 ] [ 8 ] The Tarnished required one Great Rune to be granted audience with the Two Fingers in the inner chamber of the Roundtable Hold . [ 9 ] They also required enough Great Runes to repair the Elden Ring before the Two Fingers would permit them to enter Leyndell, Royal Capital to have an audience with Queen Marika to become Elden Lord. [ 10 ] During the course of the game, this is two Great Runes, however since the Shardbearer Morgott, the Omen King guards the entrance to the Erdtree and must be killed to access it, they will have at least three when granted audience. Finger Reader Enia has only ever seen two Great Runes together once before this. [ 11 ]
Remembrances are special Tools that are obtained upon defeating certain bosses in Elden Ring . They can either be used to obtain a large amount of runes or traded with Finger Reader Enia for exclusive items.
Wandering Mausoleums and Remembrance Coffins can be used once each to duplicate a Remembrance, even if the Remembrance has already been used. Mausoleums with bells can duplicate any remembrance, but the two mausoleums without bells at the Mausoleum Compound site of grace can only duplicate a Legend remembrance. Coffins found in the Shadow of the Erdtree expansion can duplicate any remembrance.
Ashes of War are special items in Elden Ring that can be used to modify the Skills of certain armaments , and (optionally) infuse them with one of a selection of possible Affinities . With any Whetblade , they can be applied to compatible armaments while resting at a Site of Grace , or by Smithing Master Hewg . [ 1 ] [ 2 ]
Ashes of War are not consumed when applied; rather, they are slotted into the armament, and can be removed at any time.
Each Ash of War corresponds to a specific Skill, and can only be applied to armaments compatible with that skill; for instance, Ash of War: Piercing Fang can only be applied to weapons capable of thrusting attacks, but Ash of War: Kick can be applied to any melee weapon. Ashes of War also cannot be applied to any weapon that is upgraded using Somber Smithing Stones .
Ashes of War also each have a corresponding "native" Affinity; for instance, Ash of War: Bloody Slash has the Blood affinity . When being applied to an armament, this Affinity can optionally be infused to change the weapon's base damage values, damage scaling, and/or status effect buildups; alternatively, the armament can be left with the Standard affinity to keep the default scaling, and other affinities can be chosen if corresponding Whetblades are held.
Ashes of War can be freely removed from weapons — refunding the Ash and reverting the weapon to its default Skill — or directly transferred between weapons. They can also be duplicated by Hewg with Lost Ashes of War — whether in the inventory or already on a weapon — consuming them in the process.
Ashes of War are most commonly obtained as a drop from certain Teardrop Scarabs ; however, they are sometimes contained in chests, sold by merchants, dropped by certain enemies such as Night's Cavalry or the unique Godrick Knight in Fort Haight , or occasionally are available as potential rewards from boss Remembrances — for example, Ash of War: Waves of Darkness from the Remembrance of the Naturalborn .
Additionally, some weapons have Ashes of War pre-equipped on acquisition, such that they can be applied to other weapons or duplicated from them. For example, the Nagakiba has Ash of War: Piercing Fang equipped on acquisition, despite having Unsheathe as its base skill when Piercing Fang is removed; and Backhand Blade has Ash of War: Blind Spot pre-equipped while simultaneously having Blind Spot as its underlying base skill. This often occurs when the Ash is otherwise impossible to obtain naturally.
It depends on the Ash of War individually if the Skill it grants scales with the weapon's attack rating, or your character's stats and the weapon's upgrades.
For example: Ash of War: Lion's Claw will deal over 1000 damage on a Keen-infused +25 Flamberge equipped to a character with 20str/40dex and less than 1000 if the Ash of War's default Heavy-infusion was chosen instead; meanwhile, Ash of War: Ground Slam will deal less damage if any infusion option other than Heavy is chosen, even if the weapon's attack rating would be higher with something else.
There are a total of 91 Ashes of War in the Elden Ring base game:
Standard 12, Keen 11, Quality 12, Lightning 3, Magic 10, Sacred 11, Heavy 14, Fire 3, Blackflame/Flame Art 2, Poison 2, Cold 3, Blood 4, Occult 4
Golden Seed is a Bolstering Material in Elden Ring .
A golden seed, found at the base of an illusory tree .
Increases a Sacred Flask 's number of uses. (Can be used after resting at a site of grace .)
When the Elden Ring was shattered , these seeds flew from the Erdtree , scattering across the various lands, as if life itself knew that its end has come.

Larval Tears are Key Items in Elden Ring .
Core of a creature of mimicry known as a silver tear . As much a substance as it is a living organism.
Material required by the amber egg cradled by Rennala, Queen of the Full Moon , to birth people anew.
Being born anew allows the reallocation of attributes boosted by leveling up .
銀の雫と呼ばれる、変態生物の核 生物と物質の中間にあるもの
満月の女王レナラの抱く、琥珀のタマゴ その秘めたる「産まれ直し」の素材となる
産まれ直しでは レベルアップを最初からやり直すことができる
Core of a creature of mimicry known as a silver tear . As much a substance as it is a living organism.
Material required by the amber egg cradled by Rennala, Queen of the Full Moon , to birth people anew.
Being born anew allows the reallocation of attributes boosted by leveling up .
There are 18 Larval Tears to find in the Lands Between .
Somber Smithing Stones (also simply known as Somberstones ) are Bolstering Materials in Elden Ring , of which 10 variants exist. They are rarer counterparts of ordinary Smithing Stones required for upgrading certain special Weapons .
They can be used by Smithing Master Hewg or War Counselor Iji to incrementally upgrade such special Weapons in exchange for runes , up to +10, consuming one stone in the process. Each "tier" of Somber Smithing Stone can upgrade an armament once, to the same level as the number in their name. Somber Ancient Dragon Smithing Stones are the sole exception to this naming scheme, being the equivalent of a Somber Smithing Stone 10.
However, for ordinary armaments, regular Smithing Stones are needed instead; such armaments can be upgraded all the way to +25, and require 12 stones per 3 upgrades, except for the final one which only requires 1 Ancient Dragon Smithing Stone .
They can be found scattered through both the Lands Between and the Realm of Shadow , sometimes looted from certain enemies when killed, or purchased from some Merchants in usually limited quantity. However, excepting Somber Ancient Dragon Smithing Stones, they can be purchased in unlimited quantity from the Twin Maiden Husks after giving them Somberstone Miner's Bell Bearings , of which 4 are scattered throughout the Lands Between.
Grave Gloveworts are a type of bolstering material in Elden Ring and Shadow of the Erdtree . They are used to upgrade the power of Spirit Ashes .
Grave Gloveworts are the standard form of the white glovewort found growing in the many catacombs of the Lands Between . After Roderika becomes a spirit tuner at the Roundtable Hold , she can use Grave Gloveworts to incrementally upgrade the power and durability of Ashes up to a maximum of +10 .
There are 10 varieties of Grave Gloveworts to be found in the game.

The ancient dragons , who ruled in the prehistoric era before the Age of the Erdtree , would protect their lord as a wall of living rock. And so it is that the shape of the dragon has become symbolic of all manner of protections.

Scadutree Fragment is a bolstering material in Shadow of the Erdtree .
A splinter of the Scadutree that contains golden brilliance. Acquired at the Church of Marika and other places in the realm of shadow .
Consume these at sites of grace to bolster your Scadutree Blessing . The Scadutree Blessing bolsters the bearer's ability to deal and negate damage but has no influence outside the realm of shadow.
It is said that when the Scadutree crumbles from its core that it will scatter across the entire realm of shadow. The people of the Erdtree collect the splinters and use them in prayer.
黄金の輝きを含んだ、影樹の破片 影の地の、マリカの教会などで手に入る
祝福で、これを消費することで 「影樹の加護」を上げることができる その加護は、それを受けた者の 攻撃力とカット率を高めるが 影の地の外では効果を発揮しない
それは、影樹が内から壊れるとき 影の地の全土に飛び散るのだといい 黄金樹の民は、それを集めて祈っている
A splinter of the Scadutree that contains golden brilliance. Acquired at the Church of Marika and other places in the realm of shadow .
Consume these at sites of grace to bolster your Scadutree Blessing . The Scadutree Blessing bolsters the bearer's ability to deal and negate damage but has no influence outside the realm of shadow.
It is said that when the Scadutree crumbles from its core that it will scatter across the entire realm of shadow. The people of the Erdtree collect the splinters and use them in prayer.
This item is consumed at Sites of Grace to improve the Scadutree Blessing , which is only active while you are within the Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree DLC area, the Land of Shadow .
The Scadutree Blessing reduces all incoming damage to the player while also increasing all damage dealt. When you have collected all of them, the damage increase is equal to 200.5% , and the damage decrease is equal to 51.3% .
There are a total of 50 Scadutree Fragments within the Land of Shadow.
Revered Spirit Ash is a Bolstering Material in Shadow of the Erdtree .
Spirit ash of those who came before, infused with potent spirituality . Acquired from the corpses of hornsent and other objects that ritually decorate townships and villages across the Realm of Shadow .
Consume these at Sites of Grace to bolster your Revered Spirit Ash Blessing. The Revered Spirit Ash Blessing enhances the abilities of summoned spirits and spectral steeds to deal and negate damage but has no influence outside the realm of shadow.
The withered corpses were called tutelary deities , and Revered Spirit Ash was said to quietly accumulate in the palms of their hands.
強い霊性を纏った祖先の遺灰 影の地の各地にある、街や村に祀られた 角人の遺体などから手に入る
祝福で、これを消費することで 「霊灰の加護」を上げることができる その加護は、召喚する霊体と霊馬の 攻撃力とカット率を高めるが 影の地の外では効果を発揮しない
その乾いた遺体は、土地神と呼ばれ 霊灰は、その掌にそっと生じるという
Spirit ash of those who came before, infused with potent spirituality . Acquired from the corpses of hornsent and other objects that ritually decorate townships and villages across the Realm of Shadow .
Consume these at Sites of Grace to bolster your Revered Spirit Ash Blessing. The Revered Spirit Ash Blessing enhances the abilities of summoned spirits and spectral steeds to deal and negate damage but has no influence outside the realm of shadow.
The withered corpses were called tutelary deities , and Revered Spirit Ash was said to quietly accumulate in the palms of their hands.
Revered Spirit Ash are used at Sites of Grace to increase the Revered Spirit Ash Blessing level. The Blessing reduces the damage taken by Torrent while mounted and by summoned Spirit Ashes , while also increasing the damage dealt by Spirit Ashes. However, this effect is only active while within the Realm of Shadow .
Collecting all available ashes and reaching Blessing level 10 results in:
The Ash collects in their hands
A total of 25 Revered Spirit Ashes are found throughout the Realm of Shadow :
